**Overlap spans to check:** "is why the believers will say to him on the day of resurrection you are the first messenger"

## 10:1-2 — verses 1-2 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Tafsir of Surat Yunus

[It is Meccan]

In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful

As for the disconnected letters at the beginnings of the surahs, the discussion of them has already been given in full at the beginning of Surat al-Baqarah.

Abu al-Duha said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas, regarding His saying "Alif Lam Ra": it means "I am Allah, I see." Al-Dahhak and others said the same.

{These are the verses of the wise Book} means: these are the verses of the clear, precisely ordered Qur'an. Mujahid said concerning {Alif Lam Ra. These are the verses of the wise Book}: [he said: the Torah and the Gospel].

[Al-Hasan said: the Torah and the Psalms].

Qatadah said regarding {These are the verses of the Book}: he said: the books that existed before the Qur'an.

I do not know the basis or the meaning of this last opinion.

His saying: {Was it a source of wonder to the people that We revealed to a man from among them, saying: "Warn mankind and give glad tidings to those who believe"} and the rest of the verse: the Exalted is here rejecting those among the disbelievers who found it strange that messengers should be sent from among mankind, just as He informed us about the peoples of the past who said: {Shall mere men guide us?} [al-Taghabun: 6]. Hud and Salih said to their respective peoples: {Do you wonder that a reminder from your Lord has come to you through a man from among you?} [al-A'raf: 63, 69]. And the Exalted told us that the disbelievers of Quraysh said: {Has he made the gods into one God? Indeed this is a strange thing} [Sad: 5].

Al-Dahhak said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas: when Allah the Exalted sent Muhammad ﷺ as a messenger, the Arabs, or those among them who rejected it, denied this, saying: Allah is too great for His messenger to be a human being like Muhammad. He said: so Allah, Mighty and Majestic, revealed: {Was it a source of wonder to the people that We revealed to a man from among them}.

Regarding His saying: {that they have a truthful footing (qadam sidq) with their Lord}, the commentators differed on it. Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas, concerning His saying {that they have a truthful footing [with their Lord]}: he means: happiness was already decreed for them in the first record.

Al-'Awfi said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas: {that they have a truthful footing with their Lord} means: a good reward, for what they had sent forth. Al-Dahhak, al-Rabi' ibn Anas, and Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said the same. This is like His saying: {to warn of severe punishment from Him, and to give glad tidings to the believers who do righteous deeds that they will have a good reward, abiding therein forever} [al-Kahf: 2, 3].

Mujahid said concerning {that they have a truthful footing with their Lord}: he said: it refers to the righteous deeds, their prayer, their fasting, their charity, and their glorification of Allah.

[Amr ibn al-Harith said, on the authority of Qatadah or al-Hasan, regarding {that they have a truthful footing with their Lord}]: he said: Muhammad ﷺ is an intercessor for them. Zayd ibn Aslam and Muqatil ibn Hayyan said the same.

Qatadah said: a truthful precedence with their Lord.

Ibn Jarir preferred the opinion of Mujahid, that it refers to the righteous deeds which they had sent forth, saying: just as one says "he has a footing (qadam) in Islam." From this comes the saying of [Hassan], may Allah be pleased with him:

"To You belongs our foremost footing, and behind us follows our predecessor in obedience to Allah..."

And the saying of Dhu al-Rummah:

"You have a footing that people cannot deny, which, along with ancestral nobility, has overflowed even the sea."

His saying, the Exalted: {The disbelievers said: 'Indeed this is clearly a magician'} means: despite the fact that We sent to them a messenger from among themselves, a man of their own kind, bringing glad tidings and warning, {the disbelievers said: 'Indeed this is clearly a magician'}, meaning: openly so, though they were lying in saying this.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

تَفْسِيرُ سُورَةِ يُونُسَ

[وَهِيَ مَكِّيَّةٌ] 

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ الرَّحِيمِ

* *

أَمَّا الْحُرُوفُ الْمُقَطَّعَةُ فِي أَوَائِلِ السُّوَرِ، فَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ الْكَلَامُ عَلَيْهَا [مُسْتَوْفًى] فِي أَوَائِلِ سُورَةِ الْبَقَرَةِ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو الضُّحَى، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: "الر"، أَيْ: أَنَا اللَّهُ أَرَى. وَكَذَا قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ وَغَيْرُهُ.

﴿تِلْكَ آيَاتُ الْكِتَابِ الْحَكِيمِ﴾ أَيْ: هَذِهِ آيَاتُ الْقُرْآنِ الْمُحْكَمِ الْمُبِينِ وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿الر تِلْكَ آيَاتُ الْكِتَابِ الْحَكِيمِ﴾ [قَالَ: التَّوْرَاةُ وَالْإِنْجِيلُ] . 

[وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ: التَّوْرَاةُ وَالزَّبُورُ] . 

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿تِلْكَ آيَاتُ الْكِتَابِ﴾ قَالَ: الْكُتُبُ الَّتِي كَانَتْ قَبْلَ الْقُرْآنِ.

وَهَذَا الْقَوْلُ لَا أَعْرِفُ وَجْهَهُ وَلَا مَعْنَاهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَكَانَ لِلنَّاسِ عَجَبًا أَنْ أَوْحَيْنَا إِلَى رَجُلٍ مِنْهُمْ أَنْ أَنْذِرِ النَّاسَ وَبَشِّرِ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا﴾ الْآيَةَ، يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُنْكِرًا عَلَى مَنْ تَعَجَّبَ مِنَ الْكُفَّارِ مِنْ إِرْسَالِ الْمُرْسَلِينَ مِنَ الْبَشَرِ، كَمَا أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى عَنِ الْقُرُونِ الْمَاضِيَةِ مِنْ قَوْلِهِمْ: ﴿أَبَشَرٌ يَهْدُونَنَا﴾ [التَّغَابُنُ: ٦] وَقَالَ هُودٌ وَصَالِحٌ لِقَوْمِهِمَا: ﴿أَوَعَجِبْتُمْ أَنْ جَاءَكُمْ ذِكْرٌ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ عَلَى رَجُلٍ مِنْكُمْ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٦٣: ٦٩] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ كُفَّارِ قُرَيْشٍ أَنَّهُمْ قَالُوا: ﴿أَجَعَلَ الآلِهَةَ إِلَهًا وَاحِدًا إِنَّ هَذَا لَشَيْءٌ عُجَابٌ﴾ [ص: ٥] .

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: لَمَّا بَعَثَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى مُحَمَّدًا ﷺ رَسُولًا أَنْكَرَتِ الْعَرَبُ ذَلِكَ، أَوْ مَنْ أَنْكَرَ مِنْهُمْ، فَقَالُوا: اللَّهُ أَعْظَمُ مِنْ أَنْ يَكُونَ رَسُولُهُ بَشَرًا مِثْلَ محمد. قال: فأنزل الله عز وَجَلَّ: ﴿أَكَانَ لِلنَّاسِ عَجَبًا أَنْ أَوْحَيْنَا إِلَى رَجُلٍ مِنْهُمْ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَنَّ لَهُمْ قَدَمَ صِدْقٍ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ﴾ اخْتَلَفُوا فِيهِ، فَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَنَّ لَهُمْ قَدَمَ صِدْقٍ [عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ] ﴾ يَقُولُ: سَبَقَتْ لَهُمُ السَّعَادَةُ فِي الذِّكْرِ الْأَوَّلِ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿أَنَّ لَهُمْ قَدَمَ صِدْقٍ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ﴾ يَقُولُ: أَجْرًا حَسَنًا، بِمَا قَدَّمُوا. وَكَذَا قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، وَالرَّبِيعُ بْنُ أَنَسٍ، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ. وَهَذَا كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿لِيُنْذِرَ بَأْسًا شَدِيدًا مِنْ لَدُنْهُ وَيُبَشِّرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ الَّذِينَ يَعْمَلُونَ الصَّالِحَاتِ أَنَّ لَهُمْ أَجْرًا حَسَنًا مَاكِثِينَ فِيهِ أَبَدًا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ٢، ٣]

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿أَنَّ لَهُمْ قَدَمَ صِدْقٍ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ﴾ قَالَ: الْأَعْمَالُ الصَّالِحَةُ صَلَاتُهُمْ وَصَوْمُهُمْ وَصَدَقَتُهُمْ وَتَسْبِيحُهُمْ.

[وَقَالَ عَمْرُو بْنُ الْحَارِثِ عَنْ قَتَادَةَ أَوِ الْحَسَنِ ﴿أَنَّ لَهُمْ قَدَمَ صِدْقٍ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ] ﴾ قَالَ: مُحَمَّدٌ ﷺ شَفِيعٌ لَهُمْ. وَكَذَا قَالَ زَيْدُ بْنُ أَسْلَمَ، وَمُقَاتِلُ بْنُ حَيَّانَ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: سَلفُ صِدْقٍ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ.

وَاخْتَارَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ قَوْلَ مُجَاهِدٍ -أَنَّهَا الْأَعْمَالُ الصَّالِحَةُ الَّتِي قَدَّمُوهَا -قَالَ: كَمَا يُقَالُ: "لَهُ قَدَمٌ فِي الْإِسْلَامِ" وَمِنْهُ قَوْلُ [حَسَّانَ] رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ.

لَنَا القَدَمُ العُليا إِلَيْكَ وخَلْفُنا لأوَّلِنا فِي طاعَة اللهِ تَابعُ ...

وَقَوْلُ ذِي الرُّمة:

لكُم قَدَمٌ لَا يُنْكرُ الناسُ أَنَّهَا ... مَعَ الحسَبِ العَادِيّ طَمَّت عَلَى البَحْرِ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿قَالَ الْكَافِرُونَ إِنَّ هَذَا لَسَاحِرٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ أَيْ: مَعَ أَنَّا بَعَثْنَا إِلَيْهِمْ رَسُولًا مِنْهُمْ، رَجُلًا مِنْ جِنْسِهِمْ، بَشِيرًا وَنَذِيرًا، ﴿قَالَ الْكَافِرُونَ إِنَّ هَذَا لَسَاحِرٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ أَيْ: ظَاهِرٌ، وَهُمُ الْكَاذِبُونَ فِي ذَلِكَ.

---

## 10:3 — verse 3

### Translation

He, exalted, informs that He is the Lord of the entire universe, and that He created the heavens and the earth in six days. It has been said: like these days of ours; and it has been said: each day is like a thousand years of what you count, as will be explained [if God, exalted, wills]. Then He rose upon the Throne (al-Arsh), and the Throne is the greatest of created things and their ceiling.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Isma'il ibn Abi Khalid said: I heard Sa'd al-Ta'i say: the Throne is a red ruby.

Wahb ibn Munabbih said: God created it from His light.

This is gharib (a singular, unusual report).

{He governs the affair} means: He governs the affair of all created beings, {not even the weight of an atom escapes Him in the heavens or on the earth} [Saba: 3]. No matter distracts Him from another matter, no questions burden Him, He is not wearied by the persistence of those who press their requests, and His governance of the great does not divert Him from the small, whether in the mountains, the seas, inhabited lands, or barren wastelands. {There is no creature on earth but that its provision is upon God, and He knows its dwelling place and its resting place; all is in a clear record} [Hud: 6]. {Not a leaf falls but that He knows it, nor a grain in the darkness of the earth, nor anything moist or dry, but that it is in a clear record} [al-An'am: 59].

Al-Darawardi reported, from Sa'd ibn Ishaq ibn Ka'b [ibn 'Ujrah], that he said: when this verse was revealed, {Indeed your Lord is God, who created the heavens and the earth in six days}, a large group of riders met them, appearing to be Arabs. They were asked: who are you? They said: we are jinn; we have come out from Medina, this verse drove us out. Ibn Abi Hatim reported it.

[His saying] {There is no intercessor except after His permission} is like His saying, exalted is He: {Who is it that intercedes with Him except by His permission} [al-Baqarah: 255], and like His saying, exalted is He: {How many an angel is there in the heavens whose intercession avails nothing, except after God gives permission to whom He wills and is pleased with} [al-Najm: 26], and His saying: {Intercession does not benefit anyone with Him except one to whom He has given permission} [Saba: 23].

His saying: {That is God, your Lord, so worship Him. Will you not then remember?} means: single Him out alone for worship, with no partner for Him. {Will you not then remember?} means: O you polytheists, in your affair you worship other than God alongside Him, while you know that He alone is the sole Creator, as in His saying, exalted is He: {And if you ask them who created them, they will surely say: God} [al-Zukhruf: 87], and His saying: {Say: Who is the Lord of the seven heavens and the Lord of the mighty Throne? They will say: God's. Say: Will you not then fear Him?} [al-Mu'minun: 86-87], and likewise the verse before it and the verse after it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أنه رب العالم جميعه، وَأَنَّهُ خَلَق السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ فِي سِتَّةِ أَيَّامٍ -قِيلَ: كَهَذِهِ الْأَيَّامِ، وَقِيلَ: كُلُّ يَوْمٍ كَأَلْفِ سَنَةٍ مِمَّا تَعُدُّونَ. كَمَا سَيَأْتِي بَيَانُهُ [إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى] ثم استوى عَلَى الْعَرْشِ، وَالْعَرْشُ أَعْظَمُ الْمَخْلُوقَاتِ وَسَقْفُهَا.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا حَجَّاجُ بْنُ حَمْزَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو أُسَامَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ أَبِي خالد قال: سمعت سعد الطَّائِيَّ يَقُولُ: الْعَرْشُ يَاقُوتَةٌ حَمْرَاءُ.

وَقَالَ وَهْبُ بْنُ مُنَبِّهٍ: خَلَقَهُ اللَّهُ مِنْ نُورِهِ.

وَهَذَا غَرِيبٌ.

﴿يُدَبِّرُ الأمْرَ﴾ أَيْ: يُدَبِّرُ أَمْرَ الْخَلَائِقِ، ﴿لَا يَعْزُبُ عَنْهُ مِثْقَالُ ذَرَّةٍ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَلا فِي الأرْضِ﴾ [سَبَأٍ: ٣] ، وَلَا يَشْغَلُهُ شَأْنٌ عَنْ شَأْنٍ، وَلَا تُغَلِّظُهُ الْمَسَائِلُ، وَلَا يَتَبَرَّمُ بِإِلْحَاحِ الْمُلِحِّينَ وَلَا يُلْهِيهِ تَدْبِيرُ الْكَبِيرِ عَنِ الصَّغِيرِ، فِي الْجِبَالِ وَالْبِحَارِ وَالْعِمْرَانِ وَالْقَفَارِ، ﴿وَمَا مِنْ دَابَّةٍ فِي الأرْضِ إِلا عَلَى اللَّهِ رِزْقُهَا وَيَعْلَمُ مُسْتَقَرَّهَا وَمُسْتَوْدَعَهَا كُلٌّ فِي كِتَابٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ [هُودٍ: ٦] . ﴿وَمَا تَسْقُطُ مِنْ وَرَقَةٍ إِلا يَعْلَمُهَا وَلا حَبَّةٍ فِي ظُلُمَاتِ الأرْضِ وَلا رَطْبٍ وَلا يَابِسٍ إِلا فِي كِتَابٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٥٩] . 

وَقَالَ الدَّرَاوَرْدِيُّ، عَنْ سَعْدِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ بْنِ كَعْبِ [بْنِ عُجْرَةَ] أَنَّهُ قَالَ حِينَ نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: ﴿إِنَّ رَبَّكُمُ اللَّهُ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضَ فِي سِتَّةِ أَيَّامٍ﴾ لَقِيَهُمْ رَكْبٌ عَظِيمٌ [لَا يَرَوْنَ إِلَّا أَنَّهُمْ] مِنَ الْعَرَبِ، فَقَالُوا لَهُمْ: مَنْ أَنْتُمْ؟ قَالُوا. مِنَ الْجِنِّ، خَرَجْنَا مِنَ الْمَدِينَةِ، أَخْرَجَتْنَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

[وَقَوْلُهُ] ﴿مَا مِنْ شَفِيعٍ إِلا مِنْ بَعْدِ إِذْنِهِ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَنْ ذَا الَّذِي يَشْفَعُ عِنْدَهُ إِلا بِإِذْنِهِ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٥٥] وَكَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَكَمْ مِنْ مَلَكٍ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ لَا تُغْنِي شَفَاعَتُهُمْ شَيْئًا إِلا مِنْ بَعْدِ أَنْ يَأْذَنَ اللَّهُ لِمَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيَرْضَى﴾ [النَّجْمِ: ٢٦] وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا تَنْفَعُ الشَّفَاعَةُ عِنْدَهُ إِلا لِمَنْ أَذِنَ لَهُ﴾ [سَبَأٍ: ٢٣] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ذَلِكُمُ اللَّهُ رَبُّكُمْ فَاعْبُدُوهُ أَفَلا تَذَكَّرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: أَفْرِدُوهُ بِالْعِبَادَةِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، ﴿أَفَلا تَذَكَّرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: أَيُّهَا الْمُشْرِكُونَ فِي أَمْرِكُمْ، تَعْبُدُونَ مَعَ اللَّهِ غَيْرَهُ، وَأَنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّهُ الْمُتَفَرِّدُ بِالْخَلْقِ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَئِنْ سَأَلْتَهُمْ مَنْ خَلَقَهُمْ لَيَقُولُنَّ اللَّهُ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ: ٨٧] ، وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قُلْ مَنْ رَبُّ السَّمَاوَاتِ السَّبْعِ وَرَبُّ الْعَرْشِ الْعَظِيمِ سَيَقُولُونَ لِلَّهِ قُلْ أَفَلا تَتَّقُونَ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ٨٦ -٨٧] ، وَكَذَا الْآيَةُ الَّتِي قَبْلَهَا وَالَّتِي بعدها.

---

## 10:4 — verse 4

### Translation

He, Exalted, informs that to Him is the return of all creation on the Day of Resurrection. He will not leave any one of them behind until He brings him back just as He originated him. Then He, Exalted, mentions that just as He originated creation, so likewise He will bring it back: {And He is the One who originates creation, then brings it back, and that is easier for Him} [al-Rum: 27].

{That He may reward those who believed and did righteous deeds with justice}, that is, with fairness and full recompense. {And those who disbelieved will have a drink of scalding water and a painful punishment because of what they used to disbelieve}, that is, on account of their disbelief they will be punished on the Day of Resurrection with various kinds of torment, from {scorching wind and scalding water and shade of black smoke} [al-Waqi'ah: 42-43]. {This, so let them taste it: scalding water and pus, and other similar kinds in pairs} [Sad: 57-58]. {This is Hell, which the criminals deny; they will circulate between it and scalding, boiling water} [al-Rahman: 43-44].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّ إِلَيْهِ مَرْجِعَ الْخَلَائِقِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، لَا يَتْرُكُ مِنْهُمْ أَحَدًا حَتَّى يُعِيدَهُ كَمَا بَدَأَهُ. ثُمَّ ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ كَمَا بَدَأَ الْخَلْقَ كَذَلِكَ يُعِيدُهُ، ﴿وَهُوَ الَّذِي يَبْدَأُ الْخَلْقَ ثُمَّ يُعِيدُهُ وَهُوَ أَهْوَنُ عَلَيْهِ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٢٧] .

﴿لِيَجْزِيَ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ بِالْقِسْطِ﴾ أَيْ: بِالْعَدْلِ وَالْجَزَاءِ الْأَوْفَى، ﴿وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا لَهُمْ شَرَابٌ مِنْ حَمِيمٍ وَعَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ بِمَا كَانُوا يَكْفُرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: بِسَبَبِ كُفْرِهِمْ يُعَذَّبُونَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ بِأَنْوَاعِ الْعِقَابِ، مِنْ ﴿سَمُومٍ وَحَمِيمٍ وَظِلٍّ مِنْ يَحْمُومٍ﴾ [الْوَاقِعَةِ: ٤٢، ٤٣] . ﴿هَذَا فَلْيَذُوقُوهُ حَمِيمٌ وَغَسَّاقٌ وَآخَرُ مِنْ شَكْلِهِ أَزْوَاجٌ﴾ [ص: ٥٧، ٥٨] . ﴿هَذِهِ جَهَنَّمُ الَّتِي يُكَذِّبُ بِهَا الْمُجْرِمُونَ يَطُوفُونَ بَيْنَهَا وَبَيْنَ حَمِيمٍ آنٍ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ: ٤٣، ٤٤] .

---

## 10:5-6 — verses 5-6 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs about what He has created of signs indicating the completeness of His power and the greatness of His dominion, and that He made the radiance emanating from the body of the sun a light (diya') and the radiance of the moon a light (nur). This is one kind and that is another kind, and He made a difference between them so that they would not be confused with one another. He made the dominion of the sun by day and the dominion of the moon by night, and He determined phases for the moon. At first it appears small, then its light and its body increase until it becomes full and its fullness is complete, then it begins to diminish until it returns to its original state at the completion of a month, as the Almighty said: {And the moon, We have determined for it phases, until it returns like the old dried curved palm branch. It is not for the sun to overtake the moon, nor does the night outstrip the day, and each in an orbit they swim} [Ya-Sin: 39, 40]. And He said: {And the sun and the moon for reckoning. That is the determination of the Almighty, the All-Knowing} [al-An'am: 96].

And He said in this noble verse: {and determined it} meaning the moon, {and determined it in phases so that you may know the number of years and the reckoning}. By the sun the days are known, and by the movement of the moon the months and years are known.

{Allah did not create that except in truth}, meaning: He did not create it in vain, rather there is a great wisdom in it and a conclusive proof, as the Almighty said: {And We did not create the heaven and the earth and what is between them in vain. That is the assumption of those who disbelieve, so woe to those who disbelieve, from the Fire} [Sad: 27]. And the Almighty said: {Did you then think that We created you in vain and that you would not be returned to Us? Exalted is Allah, the True King, there is no god but He, Lord of the Noble Throne} [al-Mu'minun: 115, 116].

His saying: {We detail the signs}, meaning: We make clear the proofs and evidences, {for a people who know}.

His saying: {Indeed in the alternation of the night and the day}, meaning: their succession, when this one comes that one goes, and when that one goes this one comes, without any delay whatsoever, as the Almighty said: {He covers the night with the day, seeking it swiftly} [al-A'raf: 54], and He said: {It is not for the sun to overtake the moon, nor does the night outstrip the day} [Ya-Sin: 40], and the Almighty said: {The Cleaver of the daybreak, and He made the night for rest, and the sun and the moon for reckoning. That is the determination of the Almighty, the All-Knowing} [al-An'am: 96].

His saying: {and what Allah has created in the heavens and the earth}, meaning: of the signs indicating His greatness, as He said: {And how many a sign in the heavens and the earth do they pass by while they turn away from it} [Yusuf: 105], [and He said: {Say, look at what is in the heavens and the earth}] {and the signs and warnings do not avail a people who do not believe} [Yunus: 101]. And He said: {Have they not looked at what is before them and what is behind them of the heaven and the earth} [Saba: 9]. And He said: {Indeed in the creation of the heavens and the earth and the alternation of the night and the day are signs for people of understanding} [Al 'Imran: 190], meaning: of sound minds. And He said here: {signs for a people who fear} meaning: who fear Allah's punishment, His wrath, and His torment.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَمَّا خَلَقَ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الدَّالَّةِ عَلَى كَمَالِ قُدْرَتِهِ، وَعَظِيمِ سُلْطَانِهِ، وَأَنَّهُ جَعَلَ الشُّعَاعَ الصَّادِرَ عَنْ جُرْمِ الشَّمْسِ ضِيَاءً وَشُعَاعَ الْقَمَرِ نُورًا، هَذَا فَنٌّ وَهَذَا فَنٌّ آخَرُ، فَفَاوَتَ بَيْنَهُمَا لِئَلَّا يَشْتَبِهَا، وَجَعَلَ سُلْطَانَ الشَّمْسِ بِالنَّهَارِ، وَسُلْطَانَ الْقَمَرِ بِاللَّيْلِ، وَقَدَّرَ الْقَمَرَ مَنَازِلَ، فَأَوَّلُ مَا يَبْدُو صَغِيرًا، ثُمَّ يَتَزَايَدُ نُوره وَجِرْمُهُ، حَتَّى يَسْتَوْسِقَ وَيَكْمُلَ إِبْدَارُهُ، ثُمَّ يَشْرَعُ فِي النَّقْصِ حَتَّى يَرْجِعَ إِلَى حَالِهِ الْأَوَّلِ فِي تَمَامِ شَهْرٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَالْقَمَرَ قَدَّرْنَاهُ مَنَازِلَ حَتَّى عَادَ كَالْعُرْجُونِ الْقَدِيمِ لَا الشَّمْسُ يَنْبَغِي لَهَا أَنْ تُدْرِكَ الْقَمَرَ وَلا اللَّيْلُ سَابِقُ النَّهَارِ وَكُلٌّ فِي فَلَكٍ يَسْبَحُونَ﴾ [يس: ٣٩، ٤٠] . وَقَالَ: ﴿وَالشَّمْسَ وَالْقَمَرَ حُسْبَانًا ذَلِكَ تَقْدِيرُ الْعَزِيزِ الْعَلِيمِ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٩٦] .

وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: ﴿وَقَدَّرَهُ﴾ أَيْ: الْقَمَرَ ﴿وَقَدَّرَهُ مَنَازِلَ لِتَعْلَمُوا عَدَدَ السِّنِينَ وَالْحِسَابَ﴾ فَبِالشَّمْسِ تُعْرَفُ الْأَيَّامُ، وَبِسَيْرِ الْقَمَرِ تُعْرَفُ الشُّهُورُ وَالْأَعْوَامُ.

﴿مَا خَلَقَ اللَّهُ ذَلِكَ إِلا بِالْحَقِّ﴾ أَيْ: لَمْ يَخْلُقْهُ عَبَثًا بَلْ لَهُ حِكْمَةٌ عَظِيمَةٌ فِي ذَلِكَ، وَحُجَّةٌ بَالِغَةٌ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا خَلَقْنَا السَّمَاءَ وَالأرْضَ وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَا بَاطِلا ذَلِكَ ظَنُّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا فَوَيْلٌ لِلَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنَ النَّارِ﴾ [ص: ٢٧] . وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَفَحَسِبْتُمْ أَنَّمَا خَلَقْنَاكُمْ عَبَثًا وَأَنَّكُمْ إِلَيْنَا لَا تُرْجَعُونَ فَتَعَالَى اللَّهُ الْمَلِكُ الْحَقُّ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا هُوَ رَبُّ الْعَرْشِ الْكَرِيمِ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ١١٥، ١١٦] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿نُفَصِّلُ الآيَاتِ﴾ أَيْ: نُبَيِّنُ الْحُجَجَ وَالْأَدِلَّةَ ﴿لِقَوْمٍ يَعْلَمُونَ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ فِي اخْتِلافِ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ﴾ أَيْ: تَعَاقُبُهُمَا إِذَا جَاءَ هَذَا ذَهَبَ هَذَا، وَإِذَا ذَهَبَ هَذَا جَاءَ هَذَا، لَا يَتَأَخَّرُ عَنْهُ شَيْئًا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يُغْشِي اللَّيْلَ النَّهَارَ يَطْلُبُهُ حَثِيثًا﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٥٤] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿لَا الشَّمْسُ يَنْبَغِي لَهَا أَنْ تُدْرِكَ الْقَمَرَ وَلا اللَّيْلُ سَابِقُ النَّهَارِ﴾ [يس: ٤٠] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَالِقُ الإصْبَاحِ وَجَعَلَ اللَّيْلَ سَكَنًا وَالشَّمْسَ وَالْقَمَرَ حُسْبَانًا ذَلِكَ تَقْدِيرُ الْعَزِيزِ الْعَلِيمِ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٩٦] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا خَلَقَ اللَّهُ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الدَّالَّةِ عَلَى عَظَمَتِهِ تَعَالَى، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَكَأَيِّنْ مِنْ آيَةٍ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ [يَمُرُّونَ عَلَيْهَا وَهُمْ عَنْهَا مُعْرِضُونَ] ﴾ [يُوسُفَ: ١٠٥] ، [وَقَالَ ﴿قُلِ انْظُرُوا مَاذَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ] وَمَا تُغْنِي الآيَاتُ وَالنُّذُرُ عَنْ قَوْمٍ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ١٠١] . وَقَالَ: ﴿أَفَلَمْ يَرَوْا إِلَى مَا بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمَا خَلْفَهُمْ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ [سَبَأٍ: ٩] . وَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ فِي خَلْقِ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ وَاخْتِلافِ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ لآيَاتٍ لأولِي الألْبَابِ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٩٠] . أَيْ: الْعُقُولِ، وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿لآيَاتٍ لِقَوْمٍ يَتَّقُونَ﴾ أَيْ: عِقَابَ اللَّهِ، وسخطه، وعذابه.

---

## 10:7-8 — verses 7-8 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Allah, exalted is He, informs of the state of the wretched ones who disbelieved in the meeting with Allah on the Day of Resurrection, who hope for nothing from the meeting with Allah, and who were content with this worldly life and whose souls found rest and reassurance in it.

Al-Hasan said: "By Allah, they did not adorn it nor elevate it, yet still they were content with it," being heedless of the signs of Allah in creation, so they do not reflect upon them, and heedless of the legislative signs, so they do not act in accordance with them. Their abode on the Day of their Return will be the Fire, as a recompense for what they used to earn in their worldly life of sins, wrongdoings, and crimes, along with what they were upon of disbelief in Allah, His Messenger, and the Last Day.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ حَالِ الْأَشْقِيَاءِ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا بِلِقَاءِ اللَّهِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَلَا يَرْجُونَ فِي لِقَاءِ اللَّهِ شَيْئًا، وَرَضُوا بِهَذِهِ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَاطْمَأَنَّتْ إِلَيْهَا أَنْفُسُهُمْ.

قَالَ الْحَسَنُ: وَاللَّهِ مَا زَيَّنُوهَا وَلَا رَفَعُوهَا، حَتَّى رَضُوا بِهَا وَهُمْ غَافِلُونَ عَنْ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ الْكَوْنِيَّةِ فَلَا يَتَفَكَّرُونَ فِيهَا، وَالشَّرْعِيَّةِ فَلَا يَأْتَمِرُونَ بِهَا، بِأَنَّ مَأْوَاهُمْ يَوْمَ مَعَادِهِمُ النَّارُ، جَزَاءً عَلَى مَا كَانُوا يَكْسِبُونَ فِي دُنْيَاهُمْ مِنَ الْآثَامِ وَالْخَطَايَا وَالْإِجْرَامِ، مَعَ مَا هُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الْكُفْرِ بِاللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ.

---

## 10:9-10 — verses 9-10 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is an account of the state of the fortunate ones who believed in Allah, affirmed the messengers as true, and complied with what they were commanded, so they did righteous deeds, in that He will guide them because of their faith.

It is possible that the "ba" here indicates causation, so the meaning would be: because of their faith in the worldly life, Allah will guide them on the Day of Resurrection over the Sirat (bridge), until they cross it and arrive safely at Paradise. It is also possible that it indicates means, as Mujahid said concerning His statement: {Their Lord will guide them by their faith}, he said: [It will be a light for them by which they walk].

Ibn Jurayj said concerning [His statement: {Their Lord will guide them by their faith}, he said]: his deed will be represented to him in a beautiful form and a pleasant scent when he rises from his grave, it will meet its companion and give him glad tidings of every good thing, and he will say to it: Who are you? And it will say: I am your deed. Then it will be made a light in front of him until it brings him into Paradise. That is the meaning of His statement, the Exalted: {Their Lord will guide them by their faith}. As for the disbeliever, his deed will be represented to him in an evil form and a foul smell, and it will cling to its companion and stick to him closely until it hurls him into the Fire.

Something similar has been narrated from Qatadah as mursal (a report missing the Companion link), and Allah knows best.

Concerning His statement: {Their call therein will be, "Glory be to You, O Allah," and their greeting therein will be, "Peace," and the last of their call will be, "Praise be to Allah, Lord of the worlds"}, meaning: this is the state of the people of Paradise.

Ibn Jurayj said: I was informed that His statement, {Their call therein will be, "Glory be to You, O Allah"} [means: when a bird passes by them that they desire, they say, "Glory be to You, O Allah,"] and that is their call. Then the angel brings them what they desire, and greets them with peace, and they return the greeting to him. That is the meaning of His statement: {and their greeting therein will be, "Peace"}. He said: Then when they have eaten, they praise Allah their Lord, and that is the meaning of His statement: {and the last of their call will be, "Praise be to Allah, Lord of the worlds"}.

Muqatil ibn Hayyan said: When the people of Paradise wish to call for food, one of them says, {Glory be to You, O Allah}. He said: Then ten thousand servants attend to each one of them, each servant carrying a golden dish containing food unlike what is in any other, he said: and he eats from all of them.

Sufyan al-Thawri said: When one of them wishes to call for something, he says, {Glory be to You, O Allah}.

This verse bears resemblance to His statement: {Their greeting on the Day they meet Him will be, "Peace," and He has prepared for them a generous reward} [al-Ahzab: 44], and His statement: {They will not hear therein any vain talk or sin, only the saying of "Peace, Peace"} [al-Waqi'ah: 25-26], and His statement: {"Peace," a word from a Merciful Lord} [Ya-Sin: 58], and His statement: {And the angels will enter upon them from every gate, "Peace be upon you for what you patiently endured, and excellent is the final home"} [al-Ra'd: 23-24].

Concerning His statement: {and the last of their call will be, "Praise be to Allah, Lord of the worlds"}, this indicates that Allah, the Exalted, is the One who is praised forever, the One worshipped throughout eternity. This is why He praised Himself at the beginning of His creation and its continuation, at the beginning of His Book, and at the beginning of His revelation, where He, the Exalted, says: {Praise be to Allah, who sent down the Book upon His servant} [al-Kahf: 1], {Praise be to Allah, who created the heavens and the earth} [al-An'am: 1], and other such instances too numerous to elaborate upon. He is the One praised in the first and in the last, in the life of this world and in the Hereafter, in every state. This is why it has come in the hadith: "The people of Paradise are inspired to glorify and praise Allah just as they are inspired to breathe." This is so because of what they see of the multiplying of Allah's favors upon them, which are repeated, renewed, and increased, having no end and no limit. So there is no god but He and no Lord besides Him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

وَهَذَا إِخْبَارٌ عَنْ حَالِ السُّعَدَاءِ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَصَدَّقُوا الْمُرْسَلِينَ، وَامْتَثَلُوا مَا أُمِرُوا، بِهِ فَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ، بِأَنَّهُ سَيَهْدِيهِمْ بِإِيمَانِهِمْ.

يُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ تَكُونَ "الْبَاءُ" هَاهُنَا سَبَبِيَّةً فَتَقْدِيرُهُ: بِسَبَبِ إِيمَانِهِمْ فِي الدنيا يهديهم الله يوم القيامة عَلَى الصِّرَاطِ، حَتَّى يَجُوزُوهُ ويخلصُوا إِلَى الْجَنَّةِ. وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ تَكُونَ لِلِاسْتِعَانَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿يَهْدِيهِمْ رَبُّهُمْ بِإِيمَانِهِمْ﴾ قَالَ: [يَكُونُ لَهُمْ نُورًا يَمْشُونَ بِهِ] . 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج فِي [قَوْلِهِ: ﴿يَهْدِيهِمْ رَبُّهُمْ بِإِيمَانِهِمْ﴾ قَالَ] : يمثُل لَهُ عَمَلُهُ فِي صُورَةٍ حَسَنَةٍ وَرِيحٍ طَيِّبَةٍ إِذَا قَامَ مِنْ قَبْرِهِ، يُعَارِضُ صَاحِبَهُ وَيُبَشِّرُهُ بِكُلِّ خَيْرٍ، فَيَقُولُ لَهُ: مَنْ أَنْتَ؟ فَيَقُولُ: أَنَا عَمَلُكَ. فَيُجْعَلُ لَهُ نُورًا. مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ حَتَّى يُدْخِلَهُ الْجَنَّةَ، فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَهْدِيهِمْ رَبُّهُمْ بِإِيمَانِهِمْ﴾ وَالْكَافِرُ يَمْثُلُ لَهُ عَمَلُهُ فِي صُورَةٍ سَيِّئَةٍ وَرِيحٍ مُنْتِنَةٍ فَيُلَازِمُ صَاحِبَهُ ويلازُّه حَتَّى يَقْذِفَهُ فِي النَّارِ.

وَرُوِيَ نَحْوُهُ عَنْ قَتَادَةَ مُرْسَلًا فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿دَعْوَاهُمْ فِيهَا سُبْحَانَكَ اللَّهُمَّ وَتَحِيَّتُهُمْ فِيهَا سَلامٌ وَآخِرُ دَعْوَاهُمْ أَنِ الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: هَذَا حَالُ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: أخبرتُ أَنَّ قَوْلَهُ: ﴿دَعْوَاهُمْ فِيهَا سُبْحَانَكَ اللَّهُمَّ﴾ [قَالَ: إِذَا مَرَّ بِهِمُ الطَّيْرُ يَشْتَهُونَهُ، قَالُوا: سُبْحَانَكَ اللَّهُمَّ] وَذَلِكَ دَعْوَاهُمْ فَيَأْتِيهِمُ الْمَلَكُ بِمَا يَشْتَهُونَهُ، فَيُسَلِّمُ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَيَرُدُّونَ عَلَيْهِ. فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَتَحِيَّتُهُمْ فِيهَا سَلامٌ﴾ قَالَ: فَإِذَا أَكَلُوا حَمِدُوا اللَّهَ رَبَّهُمْ، فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَآخِرُ دَعْوَاهُمْ أَنِ الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾

وَقَالَ مُقَاتِلُ بْنُ حَيَّانَ: إِذَا أَرَادَ أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ أَنْ يَدْعُوَا بِالطَّعَامِ قَالَ أَحَدُهُمْ: ﴿سُبْحَانَكَ اللَّهُمَّ﴾ قَالَ: فَيَقُومُ عَلَى أَحَدِهِمْ عَشَرَةُ آلَافِ خَادِمٍ، مَعَ كُلِّ خَادِمٍ صَحْفَةٌ مِنْ ذَهَبٍ، فِيهَا طَعَامٌ لَيْسَ فِي الْأُخْرَى، قَالَ: فَيَأْكُلُ مِنْهُنَّ كُلِّهِنَّ.

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ: إِذَا أَرَادَ أَحَدُهُمْ أَنْ يَدْعُوَ بِشَيْءٍ قَالَ: ﴿سُبْحَانَكَ اللَّهُمَّ﴾

وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ فِيهَا شَبَهٌ مِنْ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿تَحِيَّتُهُمْ يَوْمَ يَلْقَوْنَهُ سَلامٌ وَأَعَدَّ لَهُمْ أَجْرًا كَرِيمًا﴾ [الْأَحْزَابِ: ٤٤] ، وَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَا يَسْمَعُونَ فِيهَا لَغْوًا وَلا تَأْثِيمًا إِلا قِيلا سَلامًا سَلامًا﴾ [الْوَاقِعَةِ: ٢٥، ٢٦] . وَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿سَلامٌ قَوْلا مِنْ رَبٍّ رَحِيمٍ﴾ [يس: ٥٨] . وَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَالْمَلائِكَةُ يَدْخُلُونَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ كُلِّ بَابٍ سَلامٌ عَلَيْكُمْ بِمَا صَبَرْتُمْ فَنِعْمَ عُقْبَى الدَّارِ﴾ [الرَّعْدِ: ٢٣، ٢٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَآخِرُ دَعْوَاهُمْ أَنِ الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ هَذَا فِيهِ دَلَالَةٌ عَلَى أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى هُوَ الْمَحْمُودُ أَبَدًا، الْمَعْبُودُ عَلَى طُولِ الْمَدَى؛ وَلِهَذَا حَمِدَ نَفْسَهُ عِنْدَ ابْتِدَاءِ خَلْقِهِ وَاسْتِمْرَارِهِ، وَفِي ابْتِدَاءِ كِتَابِهِ، وَعِنْدَ ابْتِدَاءِ تَنْزِيلِهِ، حَيْثُ يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي أَنزلَ عَلَى عَبْدِهِ الْكِتَابَ﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ١] ، ﴿الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١] إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْأَحْوَالِ الَّتِي يطول بسطها، وأنه الْمَحْمُودُ فِي الْأَوَّلِ وَ [فِي] الْآخِرِ، فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَفِي الْآخِرَةِ، فِي جَمِيعِ الْأَحْوَالِ؛ وَلِهَذَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "إِنَّ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ يُلْهَمُونَ التَّسْبِيحَ وَالتَّحْمِيدَ كَمَا يُلْهَمُونَ النَّفَس" وَإِنَّمَا يَكُونُ ذَلِكَ كَذَلِكَ لِمَا يَرَوْنَ مِنْ تَضَاعُفِ نِعَمِ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَتُكَرَّرُ وَتُعَادُ وَتُزَادُ، فَلَيْسَ لَهَا انْقِضَاءٌ وَلَا أَمَدٌ، فَلَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ وَلَا رَبَّ سِوَاهُ.

---

## 10:11 — verse 11

### Translation

God Most High informs of His forbearance and gentleness toward His servants: that He does not answer them when they invoke harm against themselves, their wealth, or their children in a state of distress and anger, and that He knows from them that they do not truly intend what they say. For this reason He does not respond to them in this situation, out of gentleness and mercy, just as He does respond to them when they invoke good, blessing, and increase for themselves, their wealth, and their children. Therefore He said: {And if God were to hasten for people the harm they seek as they seek to hasten good, their term would have been decided for them}, meaning: if He answered every such invocation of theirs in that regard, He would have destroyed them. But it is not proper to do this excessively, as has come in the hadith which the hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar related in his Musnad:

[chain] Muhammad ibn Ma'mar told us, Ya'qub ibn Muhammad told us, Hatim ibn Isma'il told us, Ya'qub ibn Mujahid Abu Hazra told us, from Ubada ibn al-Walid, Jabir told us, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Do not invoke against yourselves, do not invoke against your children, do not invoke against your wealth, lest you coincide with a moment from God in which supplications are answered, and He answers you."

Abu Dawud also related it, from the hadith of Hatim ibn Isma'il, with the same chain.

Al-Bazzar said: Ubada ibn al-Walid ibn Ubada ibn al-Samit al-Ansari related it alone; no one shared it with him. This is like His saying, Most High: {And man invokes evil as he invokes good, and man is ever hasty} [al-Isra: 11].

Mujahid said in his exegesis of this verse, {And if God were to hasten for people the harm they seek as they seek to hasten good}: it refers to a man's saying about his child or his wealth, when he becomes angry with it: "O God, do not bless it, and curse it." So if He hastened the response to them in that matter, just as He answers them in matters of good, He would have destroyed them.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ حِلْمِهِ وَلُطْفِهِ بِعِبَادِهِ: أَنَّهُ لَا يَسْتَجِيبُ لَهُمْ إِذَا دَعَوْا عَلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ أَوْ أَمْوَالِهِمْ أَوْ أَوْلَادِهِمْ فِي حَالِ ضَجَرِهِمْ وَغَضَبِهِمْ، وَأَنَّهُ يَعْلَمُ مِنْهُمْ عَدَمَ الْقَصْدِ إِلَى إِرَادَةِ ذَلِكَ، فَلِهَذَا لَا يَسْتَجِيبُ لَهُمْ -وَالْحَالَةُ هَذِهِ -لُطْفًا وَرَحْمَةً، كَمَا يَسْتَجِيبُ لَهُمْ إِذَا دَعَوْا لِأَنْفُسِهِمْ أَوْ لِأَمْوَالِهِمْ وَأَوْلَادِهِمْ بِالْخَيْرِ وَالْبَرَكَةِ وَالنَّمَاءِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلَوْ يُعَجِّلُ اللَّهُ لِلنَّاسِ الشَّرَّ اسْتِعْجَالَهُمْ بِالْخَيْرِ لَقُضِيَ إِلَيْهِمْ أَجَلُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: لَوِ اسْتَجَابَ لَهُمْ كُلَّ مَا دَعَوْهُ بِهِ فِي ذَلِكَ، لَأَهْلَكَهُمْ، وَلَكِنْ لَا يَنْبَغِي الْإِكْثَارُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ:

حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ مَعْمَر، حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا حَاتِمُ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ، حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ بْنُ مُجَاهِدٍ أَبُو حَزْرَة عَنْ عُبَادَةَ بْنِ الْوَلِيدِ، حَدَّثَنَا جَابِرٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا تَدْعُوَا عَلَى أَنْفُسِكُمْ، لَا تَدْعُوا عَلَى أَوْلَادِكُمْ، لَا تَدْعُوا عَلَى أَمْوَالِكُمْ، لَا تُوَافِقُوا مِنَ اللَّهِ سَاعَةً فِيهَا إِجَابَةٌ فَيَسْتَجِيبُ لَكُمْ".

وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ حَاتِمِ بْنِ إِسْمَاعِيلَ، بِهِ. 

وَقَالَ الْبَزَّارُ: [وَ] تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ عُبَادَةُ بْنُ الْوَلِيدِ بْنِ عُبَادَةَ بْنِ الصَّامِتِ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ، لَمْ يُشَارِكْهُ أَحَدٌ فِيهِ، وَهَذَا كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَدْعُ الإنْسَانُ بِالشَّرِّ دُعَاءَهُ بِالْخَيْرِ وَكَانَ الإنْسَانُ عَجُولا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ١١] .

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿وَلَوْ يُعَجِّلُ اللَّهُ لِلنَّاسِ الشَّرَّ اسْتِعْجَالَهُمْ بِالْخَيْرِ﴾ هُوَ قَوْلُ الْإِنْسَانِ لِوَلَدِهِ وَمَالِهِ إِذَا غَضِبَ عَلَيْهِ: "اللَّهُمَّ لَا تُبَارِكْ فِيهِ وَالْعَنْهُ". فَلَوْ يعجل لهم الاستجابة في ذَلِكَ، كَمَا يُسْتَجَابُ لَهُمْ فِي الْخَيْرِ لَأَهْلَكَهُمْ.

---

## 10:12 — verse 12

### Translation

He, exalted, informs about man and his distress and unease when harm touches him, as in His saying: {And when evil touches him, he is full of extensive supplication} [Fussilat: 51], meaning abundant, and the two verses share the same meaning. This is because when hardship befalls him, he becomes anxious and distraught over it, and increases his supplication at that time, calling upon Allah to remove it and take it away from him while lying down, sitting, and standing, and in all his states. But when Allah relieves his hardship and removes his distress, he turns away and withdraws to his own side, going on as if nothing of that had ever afflicted him: {He passes on as if he had never called upon Us for a harm that touched him.}

Then He, exalted, condemned whoever has this attribute and this way, saying: {Thus is that which the transgressors used to do made pleasing to them.} As for the one whom Allah has favored with guidance, uprightness, success, and right direction, he is excepted from this, as He, exalted, said: {Except those who are patient and do righteous deeds} [Hud: 11], and as in the saying of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ: "Amazing is the affair of the believer. Allah never decrees anything for him except that it is good for him: if hardship befalls him he is patient, and that is good for him, and if ease befalls him he is grateful, and that is good for him." And this is not the case for anyone except the believer.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنِ الْإِنْسَانِ وَضَجَرِهِ وَقَلَقِهِ إِذَا مَسَّهُ الضُّرُّ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِذَا مَسَّهُ الشَّرُّ فَذُو دُعَاءٍ عَرِيضٍ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٥١] أَيْ: كَثِيرٍ، وَهُمَا فِي مَعْنًى وَاحِدٍ؛ وَذَلِكَ لِأَنَّهُ إِذَا أَصَابَتْهُ شِدَّةٌ قَلِقَ لَهَا وَجَزِعَ مِنْهَا، وَأَكْثَرَ الدُّعَاءَ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ، فَدَعَا اللَّهَ فِي كَشْفِهَا وَزَوَالِهَا عَنْهُ فِي حَالِ اضْطِجَاعِهِ وَقُعُودِهِ وَقِيَامِهِ، وَفِي جَمِيعِ أَحْوَالِهِ، فَإِذَا فَرَّجَ اللَّهُ شِدَّتَهُ وَكَشَفَ كُرْبَتَهُ، أَعْرَضَ وَنَأَى بِجَانِبِهِ، وَذَهَبَ كَأَنَّهُ مَا كَانَ بِهِ مِنْ ذَاكَ شَيْءٌ، ﴿مَرَّ كَأَنْ لَمْ يَدْعُنَا إِلَى ضُرٍّ مَسَّهُ﴾

ثُمَّ ذَمَّ تَعَالَى مَنْ هَذِهِ صِفَتُهُ وَطَرِيقَتُهُ فَقَالَ: ﴿كَذَلِكَ زُيِّنَ لِلْمُسْرِفِينَ مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ﴾ فَأَمَّا مَنْ رَزَقَهُ اللَّهُ الْهِدَايَةَ وَالسَّدَادَ وَالتَّوْفِيقَ وَالرَّشَادَ، فَإِنَّهُ مُسْتَثْنَى مِنْ ذَلِكَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِلا الَّذِينَ صَبَرُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١١] ، وَكَقَوْلِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "عَجَبًا لِأَمْرِ الْمُؤْمِنِ لَا يَقْضِي اللَّهُ لَهُ قَضَاءً إِلَّا كَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُ: إِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ ضَرَّاءُ صَبَرَ فَكَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُ، وَإِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ سَرَّاءُ شَكَرَ فَكَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُ"، وَلَيْسَ ذَلِكَ لِأَحَدٍ إِلَّا لِلْمُؤْمِنِ.

---

## 10:13-14 — verses 13-14 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted is He, informs of what He brought upon the past generations because they denied the messengers regarding the clear proofs and manifest evidences that had come to them. Then God made these people successors after them, and He sent to them a messenger to see whether they would obey him and follow His messenger. In Sahih Muslim, from the hadith of Abu Nadrah, from Abu Sa'id, he said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Indeed the world is sweet and green, and God is making you successors in it, and He will look at what you do. So beware of the world and beware of women, for the first trial of the Children of Israel was concerning women."

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Awf ibn Malik said to Abu Bakr: I saw in a dream, as one sees while sleeping, as though a rope was let down from the sky, and the Messenger of God ﷺ was pulled up by it, then it was let down again, and Abu Bakr was pulled up by it, then the people were measured around the pulpit, and Umar exceeded them by three cubits toward the pulpit. Umar said: leave us from your dream, we have no need of it! Then when Umar was made successor (khalifah), he said: O Awf, your dream! Awf said: do you now have any interest in my dream? Did you not rebuke me for it? Umar said: woe to you! I disliked that you should proclaim the death of the successor of the Messenger of God ﷺ to himself! So Awf recounted the dream to him, until when he reached: "the people were measured to the pulpit by these three cubits," Umar said: as for the first of them, it means he will become a successor (khalifah). As for the second, it means he will not fear, for God's sake, the blame of any blamer. As for the third, it means he will be a martyr. Then Umar said: God, exalted is He, says: {Then We made you successors in the land after them, that We might observe how you would act}. So you have indeed been made a successor, O son of Umm Umar, so look to how you act! As for his saying "I do not fear, for God's sake, the blame of any blamer," that is as God wills! As for his saying "I am a martyr," how could martyrdom come to Umar while the Muslims surround him protectively?

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى عَمَّا أَحَلَّ بِالْقُرُونِ الْمَاضِيَةِ، فِي تَكْذِيبِهِمُ الرُّسُلَ فِيمَا جَاءُوهُمْ بِهِ مِنَ الْبَيِّنَاتِ وَالْحُجَجِ الْوَاضِحَاتِ، ثُمَّ اسْتَخْلَفَ اللَّهُ هَؤُلَاءِ القومَ مَنْ بَعْدِهِمْ، وَأَرْسَلَ إِلَيْهِمْ رَسُولًا لِيَنْظُرَ طَاعَتَهُمْ لَهُ، وَاتِّبَاعَهُمْ رَسُولَهُ، وَفِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي نَضْرَة، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ الدُّنْيَا حُلْوَةٌ خَضِرة، وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ مُسْتَخْلِفُكُمْ فِيهَا فَنَاظِرٌ مَاذَا تَعْمَلُونَ، فَاتَّقُوا الدُّنْيَا وَاتَّقُوا النِّسَاءَ؛ فَإِنَّ أَوَّلَ فِتْنَةِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ كَانَتْ فِي النِّسَاءِ". 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي الْمُثَنَّى، حَدَّثَنَا زَيْدُ بْنُ عَوْفٍ أَبُو رَبِيعَةَ فَهْدٌ حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادٌ، عن ثابت البُناني، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ أَبِي لَيْلَى؛ أَنَّ عَوْفَ بْنَ مَالِكٍ قَالَ لِأَبِي بَكْرٍ: رَأَيْتُ فِيمَا يَرَى النَّائِمُ كَأَنَّ سَبَبًا دُلِّي مِنَ السَّمَاءِ، فانتُشط رسولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، ثُمَّ أُعِيدَ، فانتُشط أَبُو بَكْرٍ، ثُمَّ ذُرعَ النَّاسُ حَوْلَ الْمِنْبَرِ، فَفَضُلَ عُمَرُ بِثَلَاثِ أَذْرُعٍ إِلَى الْمِنْبَرِ. فَقَالَ عُمَرُ: دَعْنَا مِنْ رُؤْيَاكَ، لَا أرَبَ لَنَا فِيهَا! فَلَمَّا اسْتُخْلِفَ عُمَرُ قَالَ: يَا عَوْفُ، رُؤْيَاكَ! فَقَالَ: وَهَلْ لَكَ فِي رُؤْيَايَ مِنْ حَاجَةٍ؟ أَوْلَمَ تَنْتَهِرْنِي ؟ فَقَالَ: وَيْحَكَ! إِنِّي: كَرِهْتُ أَنْ تنعَى لِخَلِيفَةِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ نَفْسَهُ! فَقَصَّ عَلَيْهِ الرُّؤْيَا، حَتَّى إِذَا بَلَغَ: "ذُرع النَّاسُ إِلَى الْمِنْبَرِ بِهَذِهِ الثَّلَاثِ الْأَذْرُعِ"، قَالَ: أَمَّا إِحْدَاهُنَّ فَإِنَّهُ كَائِنٌ خَلِيفَةً. وَأَمَّا الثَّانِيَةُ فَإِنَّهُ لَا يَخَافُ فِي اللَّهِ لَوْمَةَ لَائِمٍ. وَأَمَّا الثَّالِثَةُ فَإِنَّهُ شَهِيدٌ. قَالَ: فَقَالَ: يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿ثُمَّ جَعَلْنَاكُمْ خَلائِفَ فِي الأرْضِ مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ لِنَنْظُرَ كَيْفَ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ فَقَدِ استُخلفت يَا ابْنَ أُمِّ عُمَرَ، فَانْظُرْ كَيْفَ تَعْمَلُ؟ وَأَمَّا قَوْلُهُ: "فَإِنِّي لَا أَخَافُ فِي اللَّهِ لَوْمَةَ لَائِمٍ"، فَمَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ! وَأَمَّا قَوْلُهُ: [إِنِّي] شَهِيدٌ فَأَنَّى لِعُمَرَ الشَّهَادَةُ وَالْمُسْلِمُونَ مطيفون به.

---

## 10:15-16 — verses 15-16 (shared commentary)

### Translation

God Almighty informs us of the stubborn defiance of the disbelievers among the polytheists of Quraysh, those who rejected the truth and turned away from it, that when the Messenger ﷺ recited to them the Book of God and its clear proofs, they said to him: {Bring a Qur'an other than this} meaning: withdraw this one and bring us another of a different style, or change it into another form. God said to His Prophet ﷺ: {Say: It is not for me to change it of my own accord} meaning: this is not within my power, I am only a servant commanded, and a messenger conveying from God, {I only follow what is revealed to me; indeed I fear, if I disobey my Lord, the punishment of a tremendous day}.

Then He said, arguing against them for the validity of what he had brought them: {Say: If God had willed, I would not have recited it to you, nor would He have made it known to you} meaning: I have only brought this to you by God's permission to me in that matter and by His will and desire, and the proof that I have not invented it myself nor fabricated it is that you are incapable of producing anything to match it, and that you know my truthfulness and trustworthiness from the time I grew up among you until the time God, Mighty and Majestic, sent me as a prophet. You cannot find fault with me in anything by which you might disparage me. This is why He said: {I have dwelt among you a lifetime before it; will you not then reason?} meaning: do you not have minds by which you can distinguish truth from falsehood?

This is why, when Heraclius, the king of the Romans, questioned Abu Sufyan and those with him about the description of the Prophet ﷺ, among what he asked was: "Did you accuse him of lying before he said what he said?" Abu Sufyan said: I said, "No." Abu Sufyan at that time was the chief of the disbelievers and the leader of the polytheists, yet despite this he acknowledged the truth:

"Virtue is that which enemies themselves testify to..."

So Heraclius said to him: "Then I know that he would not have refrained from lying about people only to go and lie about God!"

And Ja'far ibn Abi Talib said to the Negus, the king of Abyssinia: "God sent among us a messenger whose lineage, truthfulness, and trustworthiness we know." The duration of his stay, peace be upon him, among us before prophethood was forty years. And it is reported from Sa'id ibn al-Musayyab: forty-three years. But the correct and well known view is the first one.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ تَعَنُّتِ الْكُفَّارِ مِنْ مُشْرِكِي قُرَيْشٍ الْجَاحِدِينَ الْحَقَّ الْمُعْرِضِينَ عَنْهُ، أَنَّهُمْ إِذَا قَرَأ عَلَيْهِمُ الرَّسُولُ ﷺ كِتَابَ اللَّهِ وحُجَجه الْوَاضِحَةَ قَالُوا لَهُ: ﴿ائْتِ بِقُرْآنٍ غَيْرِ هَذَا﴾ أَيْ: رُدَّ هَذَا وَجِئْنَا بِغَيْرِهِ مِنْ نَمَطٍ آخَرَ، أَوْ بَدّله إِلَى وَضْعٍ آخَرَ، قَالَ اللَّهُ لِنَبِيِّهِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، ﴿قُلْ مَا يَكُونُ لِي أَنْ أُبَدِّلَهُ مِنْ تِلْقَاءِ نَفْسِي﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسَ هَذَا إِلَيَّ، إِنَّمَا أَنَا عَبْدٌ مَأْمُورٌ، وَرَسُولٌ مُبَلِّغٌ عَنِ اللَّهِ، ﴿إِنْ أَتَّبِعُ إِلا مَا يُوحَى إِلَيَّ إِنِّي أَخَافُ إِنْ عَصَيْتُ رَبِّي عَذَابَ يَوْمٍ عَظِيمٍ﴾

ثُمَّ قَالَ مُحْتَجًّا عَلَيْهِمْ فِي صِحَّةِ مَا جَاءَهُمْ بِهِ: ﴿قُلْ لَوْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ مَا تَلَوْتُهُ عَلَيْكُمْ وَلا أَدْرَاكُمْ بِهِ﴾ أَيْ: هَذَا إِنَّمَا جِئْتُكُمْ بِهِ عَنْ إِذَنِ اللَّهِ لِي فِي ذَلِكَ وَمَشِيئَتِهِ وَإِرَادَتِهِ، وَالدَّلِيلُ عَلَى أَنِّي لَسْتُ أَتَقَوَّلُهُ مِنْ عِنْدِي وَلَا افْتَرَيْتُهُ أَنَّكُمْ عَاجِزُونَ عَنْ مُعَارَضَتِهِ، وَأَنَّكُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ صِدْقِي وَأَمَانَتِي مُنْذُ نَشَأْتُ بَيْنَكُمْ إِلَى حِينِ بَعَثَنِي اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، لَا تَنْتَقِدُونَ عَلَيَّ شَيْئًا تَغمصوني بِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَقَدْ لَبِثْتُ فِيكُمْ عُمُرًا مِنْ قَبْلِهِ أَفَلا تَعْقِلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: أَفَلَيْسَ لَكُمْ عُقُولٌ تَعْرِفُونَ بِهَا الْحَقَّ مِنَ الْبَاطِلِ؛ وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا سَأَلَ هِرَقْلُ مَلِكُ الروم أَبَا سُفْيَانَ وَمَنْ مَعَهُ، فِيمَا سَأَلَهُ مِنْ صِفَةِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، قَالَ: هَلْ كُنْتُمْ تَتَّهِمُونَهُ بِالْكَذِبِ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَقُولَ مَا قَالَ؟ قَالَ أَبُو سُفْيَانَ: فَقُلْتُ: لَا -وَقَدْ كَانَ أَبُو سُفْيَانَ إِذْ ذَاكَ رَأْسَ الْكَفَرَةِ وَزَعِيمَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، وَمَعَ هَذَا اعْتَرَفَ بِالْحَقِّ:

وَالفَضْلُ مَا شَهدَتْ بِهِ الأعداءُ ...

فَقَالَ لَهُ هِرَقْلُ: فَقَدْ أَعْرِفُ أَنَّهُ لَمْ يَكُنْ ليدَعَ الْكَذِبَ عَلَى النَّاسِ ثُمَّ يَذْهَبُ فَيَكْذِبُ عَلَى اللَّهِ. !

وَقَالَ جَعْفَرُ بْنُ أَبِي طَالِبٍ لِلنَّجَاشِيِّ مَلِكِ الْحَبَشَةِ: بَعَثَ اللَّهُ فِينَا رَسُولًا نَعْرِفُ نَسَبَهُ وَصِدْقَهُ وَأَمَانَتَهُ، وَقَدْ كَانَتْ مُدَّةَ مَقَامِهِ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، بَيْنَ أَظْهُرِنَا قَبْلَ النُّبُوَّةِ أَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً. وَعَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ: ثَلَاثًا وَأَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً. وَالصَّحِيحُ الْمَشْهُورُ الْأَوَّلُ.

---

## 10:17 — verse 17

### Translation

The Almighty says: no one is more unjust, more tyrannical, or more grievous in crime {than one who fabricates a lie against Allah}, invents a claim against Allah and asserts that Allah has sent him when this is not so. There is no one more enormous in crime nor greater in wrongdoing than such a person. And the matter of one like this is not hidden even from the dull-witted, so how could his condition be confused with that of the prophets! For whoever makes such a claim, whether truthful or lying, Allah will inevitably set up for him proofs of his righteousness or his corruption clearer than the sun itself. The difference between Muhammad ﷺ and Musaylimah the Liar (may Allah curse him), for anyone who witnessed them both, is more evident than the difference between the time of forenoon and the time of midnight in pitch darkness. From the very appearance, speech, and actions of each of them, anyone possessing insight can deduce the truthfulness of Muhammad ﷺ and the falsehood of Musaylimah the Liar, Sajah, and al-Aswad al-Ansi.

Abdullah ibn Salam said: When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ came to Madinah, the people surged forth, and I was among those who surged forth. When I saw him, I recognized that his face was not the face of a liar. The first thing I heard him say was: "O people, spread the greeting of peace, feed others food, [maintain the ties of kinship,] and pray at night while people are sleeping, and you will enter Paradise in peace."

When Dimam ibn Tha'labah came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ representing his people, Banu Sa'd ibn Bakr, he said to the Messenger of Allah, among what he said: "Who raised up this sky?" He said: "Allah." He said: "And who set up these mountains?" He said: "Allah." He said: "And who spread out this earth?" He said: "Allah." He said: "Then by the One who raised up this sky, and set up these mountains, and spread out this earth: has Allah sent you to all of mankind?" He said: "By Allah, yes." Then he asked him about prayer, zakat, hajj, and fasting, swearing this same oath before each question, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ would swear in turn. Then he said to him: "You have spoken the truth. By the One who sent you with the truth, I will neither add to this nor subtract from it."

This man was satisfied with merely this, having become certain of his truthfulness ﷺ, through what he saw and witnessed of the proofs pointing to him, just as Hassan ibn Thabit said:

"Even had there been no clear signs in him, his very spontaneous speech would bring you the truth of the matter."

As for Musaylimah, whoever among people of insight witnessed him knew his true condition without doubt, through his feeble utterances which lacked eloquence, his deeds which were not good but rather repugnant, and his so-called qur'an by which he will be made to dwell eternally in the Fire on the Day of regret and disgrace. What a difference there is between the words of the Almighty: {Allah, there is no god but He, the Ever-Living, the Sustainer of all existence. Neither drowsiness overtakes Him nor sleep. To Him belongs whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on the earth. Who is it that can intercede with Him except by His permission? He knows what is before them and what is behind them, and they encompass nothing of His knowledge except what He wills. His Kursi (footstool) extends over the heavens and the earth, and their preservation tires Him not. He is the Most High, the Most Great} [al-Baqarah: 255], and the babblings of Musaylimah, may Allah disfigure him and curse him: "O frog, daughter of two frogs, croak as you croak, you neither muddy the water nor prevent the drinker." And his saying, may he be disfigured and cursed: "Allah has indeed favored the pregnant woman, bringing forth from her a moving being from between the abdominal wall and the innards." And his saying, may Allah make him dwell forever in the Fire of Hell, as indeed He has done: "The elephant, and what will make you know what the elephant is? It has a long trunk." And his saying, may Allah remove him far from His mercy: "By the kneading women who knead, and the baking women who bake, and the ones who take mouthfuls, morsel by morsel, of fat and clarified butter, indeed Quraysh are a people who transgress." And other such ravings and nonsense which even children would be ashamed to utter, except in mockery and ridicule. For this reason Allah humiliated him, and he drank his death on the day of "the Garden of Death," and his following was torn apart, and his own companions and people cursed him. They came to al-Siddiq (Abu Bakr) as repentant men, coming eagerly to the religion of Allah, and al-Siddiq, the Caliph of the Messenger ﷺ, and may Allah be pleased with him, asked them to recite to him something from the so-called qur'an of Musaylimah, may Allah curse him. They asked to be excused from this, but he refused to excuse them, insisting they recite something of it so that those who had not heard it could hear it, and thereby recognize the excellence of the guidance and knowledge they now possessed. So they recited to him from what we have mentioned and things similar to it. When they finished, al-Siddiq, may Allah be pleased with him, said to them: "Woe to you! Where were your minds being taken? By Allah, this never came from anything divine (ill)."

It is mentioned that Amr ibn al-As came to visit Musaylimah, having been his friend in pre-Islamic times, and Amr had not yet embraced Islam. Musaylimah said to him: "Woe to you, O Amr, what has been revealed to your companion," meaning the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, "during this period?" He said: "I have heard his companions reciting a great but short surah." He said: "What is it?" He said: {By the time. Indeed mankind is in loss, except those who believe and do righteous deeds, and enjoin upon each other truth, and enjoin upon each other patience} [Surat al-Asr]. Musaylimah reflected for a moment, then said: "Something similar has been revealed to me as well." He said: "What is it?" He said: "O wabr (hyrax), you are nothing but two ears and a chest, and the rest of you is a mere insignificant peck. How do you see it, O Amr?" Amr said to him: "By Allah, you certainly know, as I know, that you are lying." If this response came from a polytheist while he was still in his polytheism, and he was not confused about the condition of Muhammad ﷺ, believing him, nor about the condition of Musaylimah, may Allah curse him, disbelieving him, then how much more so for those possessed of insight, of sound reason, and of upright and healthy intellects and understanding! For this reason Allah the Almighty said: {And who is more unjust than one who fabricates a lie against Allah, or says, "It has been revealed to me," when nothing has been revealed to him, and one who says, "I will send down the like of what Allah has sent down"} [al-An'am: 93], and He said in this noble verse: {And who is more unjust than one who fabricates a lie against Allah or denies His signs? Indeed, the wrongdoers will not succeed} [al-An'am: 21]. Likewise, whoever denies the truth which the messengers brought, and against whom the proofs have been established, there is no one more unjust than him, just as it has come in the hadith: "The most tyrannical of people against Allah is a man who kills a prophet, or whom a prophet kills."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: لَا أَحَدَ أَظْلَمَ وَلَا أَعْتَى وَلَا أَشَدَّ إِجْرَامًا ﴿مِمَّنِ افْتَرَى عَلَى اللَّهِ كَذِبًا﴾ وتَقَوّل عَلَى اللَّهِ، وَزَعَمَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ أَرْسَلَهُ، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ كَذَلِكَ، فَلَيْسَ أَحَدٌ أَكْبَرَ جُرْمًا وَلَا أَعْظَمَ ظُلما مِنْ هَذَا، وَمِثْلُ هَذَا لَا يَخْفَى أَمْرُهُ عَلَى الْأَغْبِيَاءِ، فَكَيْفَ يُشْتَبَهُ حَالُ هَذَا بِالْأَنْبِيَاءِ! فَإِنَّ مَنْ قَالَ هَذِهِ الْمَقَالَةَ صَادِقًا أَوْ كَاذِبًا، فَلَا بُدَّ أَنَّ اللَّهَ يَنصب عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْأَدِلَّةِ عَلَى برِّه أَوْ فُجُوره مَا وَأَظْهَرَ مِنَ الشَّمْسِ، فَإِنَّ الْفَرْقَ بَيْنَ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ وَبَيْنَ مُسَيْلِمَةَ الْكَذَّابِ [لَعَنَهُ اللَّهُ] لِمَنْ شَاهَدَهُمَا أَظْهَرُ مِنَ الْفَرْقِ بَيْنَ وَقْتِ الضُّحَى وَوَقْتِ نِصْفِ اللَّيْلِ فِي حنْدس الظَّلْمَاءِ، فَمِنْ سِيمَا كُلٍّ مِنْهُمَا وَكَلَامِهِ وَفِعَالِهِ يَستدّل مَنْ لَهُ بَصِيرَةٌ عَلَى صِدْقِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ وَكَذِبِ مُسَيْلِمَةَ الْكَذَّابِ، وسَجَاح، وَالْأَسْوَدِ العَنْسي. 

قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ سَلَامٍ: لَمَّا قَدِمَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ الْمَدِينَةَ انْجَفَل النَّاسُ، فَكُنْتُ فِيمَنِ انْجَفَلَ، فَلَمَّا رَأَيْتُهُ عَرَفَتْ أَنَّ وَجْهَهُ لَيْسَ بِوَجْهِ رَجُلٍ كَذَّابٍ، فَكَانَ أَوَّلَ مَا سَمِعْتُهُ يَقُولُ: "يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ أَفْشُوا السَّلَامَ، وَأَطْعِمُوا الطَّعَامَ، [وَصِلُوا الْأَرْحَامَ] وَصَلُّوا بِاللَّيْلِ وَالنَّاسُ نِيَامٌ، تَدْخُلُونَ الْجَنَّةَ بِسَلَامٍ". 

وَلَمَّا قَدم ضِمَامُ بْنُ ثَعْلَبَةَ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي قَوْمِهِ بَنِي سَعْدِ بْنِ بَكْرٍ قَالَ لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ فِيمَا قَالَ لَهُ مَنْ رَفَعَ هَذِهِ السَّمَاءَ؟ قَالَ: "اللَّهُ". قَالَ: وَمَنْ نَصَبَ هَذِهِ الْجِبَالَ؟ قَالَ: "اللَّهُ". قال: ومن سَطَحَ هَذِهِ الْأَرْضَ؟ قَالَ: "اللَّهُ". قَالَ: فَبِالَّذِي رَفَعَ هَذِهِ السَّمَاءَ، وَنَصَبَ هَذِهِ الْجِبَالَ، وسَطَح هَذِهِ الْأَرْضَ: اللَّهُ أَرْسَلَكَ إِلَى النَّاسِ كُلِّهِمْ؟ قَالَ: "اللَّهُمَّ نَعَمْ" ثُمَّ سَأَلَهُ عَنِ الصَّلَاةِ، وَالزَّكَاةِ، وَالْحَجِّ، وَالصِّيَامِ، وَيَحْلِفُ عِنْدَ كُلِّ وَاحِدَةٍ هَذِهِ الْيَمِينَ، وَيَحْلِفُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَقَالَ لَهُ: صَدَقْتَ، وَالَّذِي بَعَثَكَ بِالْحَقِّ لَا أَزِيدُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ وَلَا أَنْقُصُ. 

فَاكْتَفَى هَذَا الرَّجُلُ بِمُجَرَّدِ هَذَا، وَقَدْ أَيْقَنَ بِصِدْقِهِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، بِمَا رَأَى وَشَاهَدَ مِنَ الدَّلَائِلِ الدَّالَّةِ عَلَيْهِ، كَمَا قَالَ حَسَّانُ بْنُ ثَابِتٍ:

لَو لَمْ تَكُن فِيهِ آياتٌ مُبَيّنة كَانَتْ بَديهَتُه تَأتيكَ بالخَبَرِ

وَأَمَّا مُسَيْلِمَةُ فَمَنْ شَاهَدَهُ مِنْ ذَوي الْبَصَائِرِ، عَلِمَ أَمْرَهُ لَا مَحَالَةَ، بِأَقْوَالِهِ الرَّكِيكَةِ الَّتِي لَيْسَتْ بِفَصِيحَةٍ، وَأَفْعَالِهِ غَيْرِ الْحَسَنَةِ بَلِ الْقَبِيحَةِ، وَقُرْآنِهِ الَّذِي يُخَلَّدُ بِهِ فِي النَّارِ يَوْمَ الْحَسْرَةِ وَالْفَضِيحَةِ، وَكَمْ مِنْ فَرْقٍ بَيْنَ قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿اللَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا هُوَ الْحَيُّ الْقَيُّومُ لَا تَأْخُذُهُ سِنَةٌ وَلا نَوْمٌ لَهُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الأرْضِ مَنْ ذَا الَّذِي يَشْفَعُ عِنْدَهُ إِلا بِإِذْنِهِ يَعْلَمُ مَا بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمَا خَلْفَهُمْ وَلا يُحِيطُونَ بِشَيْءٍ مِنْ عِلْمِهِ إِلا بِمَا شَاءَ وَسِعَ كُرْسِيُّهُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضَ وَلا يَئُودُهُ حِفْظُهُمَا وَهُوَ الْعَلِيُّ الْعَظِيمُ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٥٥] . وَبَيْنَ عُلاك مُسَيْلِمَةَ قَبَّحَهُ اللَّهُ وَلَعَنَهُ: "يَا ضُفْدَعُ بِنْتَ الضُّفْدَعَيْنِ، نَقِّي كَمَا تُنَقِّينَ لَا الْمَاءُ تُكَدِّرِينَ، وَلَا الشَّارِبُ تَمْنَعِينَ". وَقَوْلُهُ -قُبّح وَلُعِنَ -: "لَقَدْ أَنْعَمَ اللَّهُ عَلَى الْحُبْلَى، إِذْ أَخْرَجَ مِنْهَا نَسَمة تَسْعَى، مِنْ بَيْنِ صِفَاق وحَشَى". وَقَوْلُهُ -خَدّره اللَّهُ فِي نَارِ جَهَنَّمَ، وَقَدْ فَعَلَ -: "الْفِيلُ وَمَا أَدْرَاكَ مَا الْفِيلُ؟ لَهُ زُلقُومٌ طَوِيلٌ" وَقَوْلُهُ -أَبْعَدَهُ اللَّهُ مِنْ رَحْمَتِهِ: "وَالْعَاجِنَاتِ عَجْنًا، وَالْخَابِزَاتِ خَبْزًا، وَاللَّاقِمَاتِ لَقْمًا، إِهَالَةً وَسَمْنًا، إِنَّ قُرَيْشًا قَوْمٌ يَعْتَدُونَ" إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْهَذَيَانَاتِ وَالْخُرَافَاتِ الَّتِي يَأْنَفُ الصِّبْيَانُ أَنْ يَتَلَفَّظُوا بِهَا، إِلَّا عَلَى وَجْهِ السُّخْرِيَةِ وَالِاسْتِهْزَاءِ؛ وَلِهَذَا أَرْغَمَ اللَّهُ أَنْفَهُ، وَشَرِبَ يَوْمَ "حَدِيقَةِ الْمَوْتِ" حَتْفَهُ. ومَزّق شَمْلَهُ. وَلَعَنَهُ صحبُه وَأَهْلُهُ. وَقَدِمُوا عَلَى الصِّدِّيقِ تَائِبِينَ، وَجَاءُوا فِي دِينِ اللَّهِ رَاغِبِينَ، فَسَأَلَهُمُ الصِّدِّيقُ خَلِيفَةُ الرَّسُولِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، وَرَضِيَ [اللَّهُ] عَنْهُ -أَنْ يَقْرَءُوا عَلَيْهِ شَيْئًا مِنْ قُرْآنِ مُسَيْلِمَةَ لَعَنَهُ اللَّهُ، فَسَأَلُوهُ أَنْ يُعْفِيَهُمْ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، فَأَبَى عَلَيْهِمْ إِلَّا أَنْ يَقْرَءُوا شَيْئًا مِنْهُ لِيُسْمِعَهُ مَنْ لَمْ يَسْمَعْهُ مِنَ النَّاسِ، فَيَعْرِفُوا فَضْلَ مَا هُمْ عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْهُدَى وَالْعِلْمِ. فَقَرَءُوا عَلَيْهِ مِنْ هَذَا الَّذِي ذَكَرْنَاهُ وَأَشْبَاهَهُ، فَلَمَّا فَرَغُوا قَالَ لَهُمُ الصِّدِّيقُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: وَيْحَكُمْ! أَيْنَ كَانَ يُذهب بِعُقُولِكُمْ؟ وَاللَّهِ إِنَّ هَذَا لَمْ يَخْرُجْ من إلٍّ.

وَذَكَرُوا أَنْ وَفَدَ عَمْرُو بْنُ الْعَاصِ عَلَى مُسَيْلِمَةَ، وَكَانَ صَدِيقًا لَهُ فِي الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ، وَكَانَ عَمْرٌو لَمْ يُسْلِمْ بعدُ، فَقَالَ لَهُ مُسَيْلِمَةُ: وَيْحَكَ يَا عَمْرُو، مَاذَا أُنْزِلَ عَلَى صَاحِبِكُمْ -يَعْنِي: رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ -فِي هَذِهِ الْمُدَّةِ؟ فَقَالَ: لَقَدْ سَمِعْتُ أَصْحَابَهُ يَقْرَءُونَ سُورَةً عَظِيمَةً قَصِيرَةً فَقَالَ: وَمَا هِيَ؟ فَقَالَ: ﴿وَالْعَصْرِ إِنَّ الإنْسَانَ لَفِي خُسْرٍ إِلا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ وَتَوَاصَوْا بِالْحَقِّ وَتَوَاصَوْا بِالصَّبْرِ﴾ [سُورَةُ الْعَصْرِ] ، فَفَكَّرَ مُسَيْلِمَةُ سَاعَةً، ثُمَّ قَالَ: وَقَدْ أُنْزِلَ عَلِيَّ مِثْلُهُ. فَقَالَ: وَمَا هُوَ؟ فَقَالَ: "يَا وَبْرُ إِنَّمَا أَنْتَ أُذُنَانِ وَصَدْرٌ، وَسَائِرُكَ حَقْرٌ نَقْر، كَيْفَ تَرَى يَا عَمْرُو؟ " فَقَالَ لَهُ عَمْرٌو: وَاللَّهِ إِنَّكَ لَتَعْلَمُ أَنِّي أَعْلَمُ أَنَّكَ لَتَكْذِبُ"، فَإِذَا كَانَ هَذَا مِنْ مُشْرِكٍ فِي حَالِ شِرْكِهِ، لَمْ يُشْتَبَهْ عَلَيْهِ حَالُ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ وَصَدَّقَهُ، وَحَالُ مُسَيْلِمَةَ -لَعَنَهُ اللَّهُ -وَكَذَبَّهُ، فَكَيْفَ بِأُولِي الْبَصَائِرِ وَالنُّهَى، وَأَصْحَابِ الْعُقُولِ السَّلِيمَةِ الْمُسْتَقِيمَةِ وَالْحِجَى! وَلِهَذَا قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَنْ أَظْلَمُ مِمَّنِ افْتَرَى عَلَى اللَّهِ كَذِبًا أَوْ قَالَ أُوحِيَ إِلَيَّ وَلَمْ يُوحَ إِلَيْهِ شَيْءٌ وَمَنْ قَالَ سَأُنزلُ مِثْلَ مَا أَنزلَ اللَّهُ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٩٣] ، وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: ﴿وَمَنْ أَظْلَمُ مِمَّنِ افْتَرَى عَلَى اللَّهِ كَذِبًا أَوْ كَذَّبَ بِآيَاتِهِ إِنَّهُ لَا يُفْلِحُ الظَّالِمُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٢١] ، وَكَذَلِكَ مَنْ كَذَّبَ بِالْحَقِّ الَّذِي جَاءَتْ بِهِ الرُّسُلُ، وَقَامَتْ عَلَيْهِ الْحُجَجُ، لَا أَحَدَ أَظْلَمُ مِنْهُ كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "أَعْتَى النَّاسِ عَلَى اللَّهِ رجلٌ قَتَلَ نَبِيًّا، أَوْ قَتَلَهُ نَبِيٌّ".

---

## 10:18-19 — verses 18-19 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted, is denouncing the polytheists who worshipped, besides God, others than Him, imagining that those deities' intercession would benefit them with God. So He, exalted, informed that they neither benefit nor harm, nor possess anything, and that none of what they claim regarding them will occur, nor will this ever happen. Therefore He, exalted, said: {Say: Do you inform God of what He does not know in the heavens or in the earth?}

Ibn Jarir said: its meaning is, "Do you tell God of what does not exist in the heavens or on the earth?" Then He declared Himself exalted above their polytheism and unbelief, saying: {Glory be to Him, and exalted is He above what they associate with Him}.

Then He, exalted, informed that this polytheism arose among mankind, coming into being after not having existed, and that all people had once been upon one religion, namely Islam. Ibn Abbas said: "Between Adam and Noah (peace be upon him) there were ten generations, all of them upon Islam. Then disagreement occurred among people, and idols, rivals, and images came to be worshipped. So God sent the messengers with His signs, His clear proofs, His conclusive arguments, and His overwhelming demonstrations, {so that whoever would perish might perish upon clear evidence, and whoever would live might live upon clear evidence} [al-Anfal: 42]."

His saying: {And were it not for a word that had already gone forth from your Lord, it would have been decided between them concerning that in which they differ} means: were it not for what had already been decreed by God, exalted, that He does not punish anyone except after the proof has been established against him, and that He has granted creation a term appointed until a numbered time, He would have judged between them concerning that in which they differed, granting felicity to the believers and bringing distress upon the disbelievers.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُنْكِرُ تَعَالَى عَلَى الْمُشْرِكِينَ الَّذِينَ عَبَدُوا مَعَ اللَّهِ غَيْرَهُ، ظَانِّينَ أَنَّ تِلْكَ الْآلِهَةَ تَنْفَعُهُمْ شفاعتُها عِنْدَ اللَّهِ، فَأَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهَا لَا تَنْفَعُ وَلَا تَضُرُّ وَلَا تَمْلِكُ شَيْئًا، وَلَا يَقَعُ شَيْءٌ مِمَّا يَزْعُمُونَ فِيهَا، وَلَا يَكُونُ هَذَا أَبَدًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ أَتُنَبِّئُونَ اللَّهَ بِمَا لَا يَعْلَمُ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَلا فِي الأرْضِ﴾ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: مَعْنَاهُ أَتُخَبِّرُونَ اللَّهَ بِمَا لَا يَكُونُ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَلَا فِي الْأَرْضِ؟ ثُمَّ نَزَّهَ نَفْسَهُ عَنْ شِرْكِهِمْ وَكُفْرِهِمْ، فَقَالَ: ﴿سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى عَمَّا يُشْرِكُونَ﴾ .

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّ هَذَا الشِّرْكَ حَادِثٌ فِي النَّاسِ، كَائِنٌ بَعْدَ أَنْ لَمْ يَكُنْ، وَأَنَّ النَّاسَ كُلَّهُمْ كَانُوا عَلَى دِينٍ وَاحِدٍ، وَهُوَ الْإِسْلَامُ؛ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: كَانَ بَيْنَ آدَمَ وَنُوحٍ عَشَرَةُ قُرُونٍ، كُلُّهُمْ عَلَى الْإِسْلَامِ، ثُمَّ وَقَعَ الِاخْتِلَافُ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ، وعُبدت الْأَصْنَامُ وَالْأَنْدَادُ وَالْأَوْثَانُ، فَبَعَثَ اللَّهُ الرُّسُلَ بِآيَاتِهِ وَبَيِّنَاتِهِ وحُجَجه الْبَالِغَةِ وَبَرَاهِينِهِ الدَّامِغَةِ، ﴿لِيَهْلِكَ مَنْ هَلَكَ عَنْ بَيِّنَةٍ وَيَحْيَا مَنْ حَيَّ عَنْ بَيِّنَةٍ﴾ [الْأَنْفَالِ: ٤٢] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَوْلا كَلِمَةٌ سَبَقَتْ مِنْ رَبِّكَ لَقُضِيَ بَيْنَهُمْ فِيمَا فِيهِ يَخْتَلِفُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَوْلَا مَا تَقَدَّمَ مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ لَا يُعَذِّبُ أَحَدًا إِلَّا بَعْدَ قِيَامِ الْحُجَّةِ عَلَيْهِ؛ وَأَنَّهُ قَدْ أَجَّلَ الْخَلْقَ إِلَى أَجَلٍ مَعْدُودٍ لَقَضَى بَيْنَهُمْ فِيمَا فِيهِ اخْتَلَفُوا، فَأَسْعَدَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وأعنَتَ الْكَافِرِينَ.

---

## 10:20 — verse 20

### Translation

That is: these disbelievers, deniers, obstinate rejecters, say: "Why has not a sign from his Lord been sent down upon Muhammad," meaning, like the she-camel that God gave to Thamud, or that Safa be turned into gold for them, or that the mountains of Mecca be removed from them and gardens and rivers be placed in their stead, and similar things which God is able to do, but He is Wise in His actions and His words. As He, Exalted, said: {Blessed is He who, if He willed, could make for you better than that, gardens beneath which rivers flow, and could make for you palaces} [al-Furqan: 10-11]. And He, Exalted, said: {And nothing prevented Us from sending signs except that the former peoples denied them. And We gave Thamud the she-camel as a visible sign, but they wronged her. And We send not the signs except as a warning} [al-Isra: 59].

He, Exalted, says: My established way with My creation is that if I give them what they ask for, then either they believe or else I hasten the punishment upon them. For this reason, when the Messenger of God, upon him be prayer and peace, was given the choice between being given what they asked for, so that either they would respond or else be hastened to punishment, and between leaving them and granting them respite, he chose to grant them respite, just as he showed forbearance toward them more than once, God's prayers be upon him.

For this reason God, Exalted, said, guiding His Prophet toward the answer to what they asked: {So say, the unseen belongs only to God}, meaning, the entire matter belongs to God, and He knows the outcomes of affairs. {So wait; indeed, I am with you among those who wait}, meaning, if you will not believe until you witness what you have asked for, then wait for God's judgment concerning me and concerning you.

This is despite the fact that they had already witnessed miracles of his, upon him be peace, greater than what they asked for, when he pointed in their presence to the moon on the night of its fullness, and it split into two, one part behind the mountain and one part in front of it. This is greater than all the earthly signs, whether of what they asked for or what they did not ask for. Had God known of them that they were asking for that seeking guidance and seeking to be firmly convinced, He would have answered them. But He knew that they were asking only out of obstinacy and stubborn contention, so He left them in their doubt, and He knew that not one of them would believe, as He, Exalted, said: {Indeed, those upon whom the word of your Lord has come into effect will not believe, even if every sign should come to them, until they see the painful punishment} [Yunus: 96-97].

And He, Exalted, said: {And even if We had sent down to them the angels, and the dead had spoken to them, and We had gathered together every thing before them in ranks, they would not have believed, unless God willed, but most of them are ignorant} [al-An'am: 111]. And because of the stubborn arrogance within them, as He, Exalted, said: {And even if We opened for them a gate into the heaven and they continued therein to ascend, they would say, "Our eyes have only been dazzled, rather we are a people bewitched"} [al-Hijr: 14-15].

And He, Exalted, said: {And if they were to see a piece of the sky falling, they would say, "A cloud heaped up"} [al-Tur: 44]. And He, Exalted, said: {And even if We had sent down to you a written scripture on parchment and they had touched it with their hands, those who disbelieved would have said, "This is nothing but clear magic"} [al-An'am: 7].

People such as these are less deserving than to be given what they asked for, because there is no benefit in answering them, since it revolves only around their stubborn contention and obstinacy, due to the abundance of their wickedness and corruption. For this reason He said: {So wait; indeed, I am with you among those who wait}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

أَيْ: وَيَقُولُ هَؤُلَاءِ الْكَفَرَةُ [الْمُلْحِدُونَ] الْمُكَذِّبُونَ الْمُعَانِدُونَ: "لَوْلَا أُنْزِلَ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ آيَةٌ مِنْ رَبِّهِ"، يَعْنُونَ كَمَا أَعْطَى اللَّهُ ثَمُودَ النَّاقَةَ، أَوْ أَنْ يُحَوِّلَ لَهُمُ الصَّفَا ذَهَبَا، أَوْ يُزِيحَ عَنْهُمْ جِبَالَ مَكَّةَ وَيَجْعَلَ مَكَانَهَا بَسَاتِينَ وَأَنْهَارًا، وَنَحْوَ ذَلِكَ مِمَّا اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ قَادِرٌ وَلَكِنَّهُ حَكِيمٌ فِي أَفْعَالِهِ وَأَقْوَالِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿تَبَارَكَ الَّذِي إِنْ شَاءَ جَعَلَ لَكَ خَيْرًا مِنْ ذَلِكَ جَنَّاتٍ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الأنْهَارُ وَيَجْعَلْ لَكَ قُصُورًا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ: ١٠، ١١] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا مَنَعَنَا أَنْ نُرْسِلَ بِالآيَاتِ إِلا أَنْ كَذَّبَ بِهَا الأوَّلُونَ وَآتَيْنَا ثَمُودَ النَّاقَةَ مُبْصِرَةً فَظَلَمُوا بِهَا وَمَا نُرْسِلُ بِالآيَاتِ إِلا تَخْوِيفًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٥٩] ، يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: إِنَّ سُنَّتِي فِي خَلْقِي أَنِّي إِذَا آتَيْتُهُمْ مَا سَأَلُوا، فَإِنْ آمَنُوا وَإِلَّا عَاجَلْتُهُمْ بِالْعُقُوبَةِ. وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا خيَّر رَسُولُ اللَّهِ، عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ، بَيْنَ أَنْ يُعطى مَا سَأَلُوا، فَإِنْ أَجَابُوا وَإِلَّا عُوجلوا، وَبَيْنَ أَنْ يَتْرُكَهُمْ ويُنْظرهم، اخْتَارَ إِنْظَارَهُمْ، كَمَا حَلَمَ عَنْهُمْ غَيْرَ مَرَّةٍ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى إِرْشَادًا لِنَبِيِّهِ إِلَى الْجَوَابِ عَمَّا سَأَلُوا: ﴿فَقُلْ إِنَّمَا الْغَيْبُ لِلَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: الْأَمْرُ كُلُّهُ لِلَّهِ، وَهُوَ يَعْلَمُ الْعَوَاقِبَ فِي الْأُمُورِ، ﴿فَانْتَظِرُوا إِنِّي مَعَكُمْ مِنَ الْمُنْتَظِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: إِنْ كُنْتُمْ لَا تُؤَمِّنُونَ حَتَّى تُشَاهِدُوا مَا سَأَلْتُمْ فَانْتَظَرُوا حُكْمَ اللَّهِ فيَّ وَفِيكُمْ. هَذَا مَعَ أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ شَاهَدُوا مِنْ مُعْجِزَاتِهِ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ أَعْظَمَ مِمَّا سَأَلُوا حِينَ أَشَارَ بِحَضْرَتِهِمْ إِلَى الْقَمَرِ لَيْلَةَ إِبْدَارِهِ، فَانْشَقَّ بِاثْنَتَيْنِ فِرْقَةٍ مِنْ وَرَاءِ الْجَبَلِ، وَفِرْقَةٍ مِنْ دُونِهِ. وَهَذَا أَعْظَمُ مِنْ سَائِرِ الْآيَاتِ الْأَرْضِيَّةِ مِمَّا سَأَلُوا وَمَا لَمْ يَسْأَلُوا، وَلَوْ عَلِمَ اللَّهُ مِنْهُمْ أَنَّهُمْ سَأَلُوا ذَلِكَ اسْتِرْشَادًا وَتَثَبُّتًا لَأَجَابَهُمْ، وَلَكِنْ عَلِمَ أَنَّهُمْ إِنَّمَا يَسْأَلُونَ عِنَادًا وَتَعَنُّتًا، فَتَرَكَهُمْ فِيمَا رَابَهُمْ، وَعَلِمَ أَنَّهُمْ لَا يُؤْمِنُ مِنْهُمْ أَحَدٌ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ حَقَّتْ عَلَيْهِمْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ وَلَوْ جَاءَتْهُمْ كُلُّ آيَةٍ حَتَّى يَرَوُا الْعَذَابَ الألِيمَ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٩٦، ٩٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ أَنَّنَا نزلْنَا إِلَيْهِمُ الْمَلائِكَةَ وَكَلَّمَهُمُ الْمَوْتَى وَحَشَرْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ قُبُلا مَا كَانُوا لِيُؤْمِنُوا إِلا أَنْ يَشَاءَ اللَّهُ وَلَكِنَّ أَكْثَرَهُمْ يَجْهَلُونَ﴾ [الأنعام: ١١١] ، وَلِمَا فِيهِمْ مِنَ الْمُكَابَرَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ فَتَحْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ بَابًا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ فَظَلُّوا فِيهِ يَعْرُجُونَ لَقَالُوا إِنَّمَا سُكِّرَتْ أَبْصَارُنَا بَلْ نَحْنُ قَوْمٌ مَسْحُورُونَ﴾ [الْحِجْرِ: ١٤، ١٥] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنْ يَرَوْا كِسْفًا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ سَاقِطًا يَقُولُوا سَحَابٌ مَرْكُومٌ﴾ [الطُّورِ: ٤٤] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ نزلْنَا عَلَيْكَ كِتَابًا فِي قِرْطَاسٍ فَلَمَسُوهُ بِأَيْدِيهِمْ لَقَالَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا إِنْ هَذَا إِلا سِحْرٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٧] ، فَمِثْلُ هَؤُلَاءِ أَقَلُّ مِنْ أَنْ يُجَابُوا إِلَى مَا سَأَلُوهُ؛ لِأَنَّهُ لَا فَائِدَةَ فِي جَوَابِ هَؤُلَاءِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ دَائِرٌ عَلَى تَعَنُّتِهِمْ وَعِنَادِهِمْ، لِكَثْرَةِ فُجُورِهِمْ وَفَسَادِهِمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَانْتَظِرُوا إِنِّي مَعَكُمْ مِنَ الْمُنْتَظِرِينَ﴾

---

## 10:21-23 — verses 21-23 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs that when He gives people a taste of mercy after adversity has touched them, such as ease after hardship, fertility after drought, rain after dearth, and the like, {then they have a plot against Our signs}.

Mujahid said: mockery and denial. As He said: {And when affliction touches man, he calls upon Us lying on his side or sitting or standing, but when We remove his affliction from him, he passes on as if he had not called upon Us for an affliction that touched him} [Yunus: 12]. And it is established in the Sahih that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ led them in the dawn prayer following a rainfall that had come upon them during the night, then he said: "Do you know what your Lord said tonight?" They said: "Allah and His Messenger know best." He said: "He said: 'Some of My servants have become believers in Me and some disbelievers. As for the one who said: we were given rain by the bounty of Allah and His mercy, that one is a believer in Me and a disbeliever in the star. And as for the one who said: we were given rain by the rising of such and such a star, that one is a disbeliever in Me and a believer in the star.'"

Concerning His saying, {Say: Allah is swifter in plotting}, meaning: more severe in gradual seizing (istidraj) and granting respite, until the one who supposes among the wrongdoers imagines that he is not being punished and that he is merely being given a delay, then he is seized while unaware. The noble scribes write down everything he does and keep account of it against him, then it is presented to the Knower of the unseen and the witnessed, and He repays him for the small and the great, down to the naqir (speck) and the qitmir (thin membrane of a date stone).

Then the Almighty informs that: {He is the One who enables you to travel on land and sea}, meaning: He preserves you and guards you with His protection, {until when you are in ships, and they sail with them by a good wind, and they rejoice in it}, meaning: because of the swiftness and comfort of their travel. Then while they are in that state, {there comes to it}, meaning: to those ships, {a violent wind}, meaning: a severe one, {and the waves come upon them from every side}, meaning: the sea surges violently against them, {and they think that they are surrounded}, meaning: that they are about to perish, {they call upon Allah, sincere in religion for Him alone}, meaning: they do not call upon any idol or image along with Him, but rather they single Him out with supplication and earnest pleading, as the Almighty said: {And when affliction touches you at sea, those you call upon besides Him forsake you, but when He saves you to dry land, you turn away, and man is ever ungrateful} [al-Isra: 67]. And He says here: {they call upon Allah, sincere in religion for Him alone: if You save us from this}, meaning: this condition, {we will surely be among the grateful}, meaning: we will not associate anyone with You, and we will single You out with worship there just as we singled You out with supplication here. The Almighty said: {But when He saves them}, meaning: from that predicament, {behold, they transgress in the earth without right}, meaning: as if none of that had ever happened, {as if he had not called upon Us for an affliction that touched him}.

Then the Almighty said: {O mankind, your transgression is only against yourselves}, meaning: it is you yourselves who taste the consequence of this transgression, and you do not harm by it anyone but yourselves, as has come in the hadith: "There is no sin more deserving that Allah hasten its punishment in this world, along with what Allah stores up for its doer in the Hereafter, than transgression and severing the ties of kinship."

Concerning His saying, {an enjoyment of the life of this world}, meaning: you have only a fleeting enjoyment in this base and paltry worldly life, {then to Us is your return}, meaning: your final destination and outcome, {and We will inform you}, meaning: We will tell you of all your deeds and repay you for them in full. So whoever finds good, let him praise Allah, and whoever finds other than that, let him blame no one but himself.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ إِذَا أَذَاقَ النَّاسَ رَحْمَةً مِنْ بَعْدِ ضَرَّاءَ مَسَّتْهُمْ، كَالرَّخَاءِ بَعْدَ الشِّدَّةِ، وَالْخِصْبِ بَعْدَ الْجَدْبِ، وَالْمَطَرِ بَعْدَ الْقَحْطِ وَنَحْوَ ذَلِكَ ﴿إِذَا لَهُمْ مَكْرٌ فِي آيَاتِنَا﴾ .

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: اسْتِهْزَاءٌ وَتَكْذِيبٌ. كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَإِذَا مَسَّ الإنْسَانَ الضُّرُّ دَعَانَا لِجَنْبِهِ أَوْ قَاعِدًا أَوْ قَائِمًا فَلَمَّا كَشَفْنَا عَنْهُ ضُرَّهُ مَرَّ كَأَنْ لَمْ يَدْعُنَا إِلَى ضُرٍّ مَسَّهُ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ١٢] ، وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ صَلَّى بِهِمُ الصُّبْحَ عَلَى أَثَرِ سَمَاءٍ -مَطَرٍ -أَصَابَهُمْ مِنَ اللَّيْلِ ثُمَّ قَالَ: "هَلْ تَدْرُونَ مَاذَا قَالَ رَبُّكُمُ اللَّيْلَةَ؟ " قَالُوا اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ. قَالَ: "قَالَ: أَصْبَحَ مِنْ عِبَادِي مُؤْمِنٌ بِي وَكَافِرٌ، فَأَمَّا مَنْ قَالَ: مُطرنا بِفَضْلِ اللَّهِ وَرَحْمَتِهِ، فَذَلِكَ مُؤْمِنٌ بِي كَافِرٌ بِالْكَوْكَبِ، وَأَمَّا مَنْ قَالَ: مُطِرْنَا بِنَوْءِ كَذَا وَكَذَا، فَذَاكَ كَافِرٌ بِي مُؤْمِنٌ بِالْكَوْكَبِ". 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قُلِ اللَّهُ أَسْرَعُ مَكْرًا﴾ أَيْ: أَشَدُّ اسْتِدْرَاجًا وَإِمْهَالًا حَتَّى يَظُنَّ الظَّانَّ مِنَ الْمُجْرِمِينَ أَنَّهُ لَيْسَ بِمُعَذَّبٍ، وَإِنَّمَا هُوَ فِي مُهْلَةٍ، ثُمَّ يُؤْخَذُ عَلَى غِرَّةٍ مِنْهُ، وَالْكَاتِبُونَ الْكِرَامُ يَكْتُبُونَ عَلَيْهِ جَمِيعَ ما يفعله، ويحصونه عليه، ثم يعرضون عَلَى عَالِمِ الْغَيْبِ وَالشَّهَادَةِ، فَيُجَازِيهِ عَلَى الْحَقِيرِ وَالْجَلِيلِ وَالنَّقِيرِ والقِطْمير.
