ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ: ﴿هُوَ الَّذِي يُسَيِّرُكُمْ فِي الْبَرِّ وَالْبَحْرِ﴾ أَيْ: يَحْفَظُكُمْ وَيَكْلَؤُكُمْ بِحِرَاسَتِهِ ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا كُنْتُمْ فِي الْفُلْكِ وَجَرَيْنَ بِهِمْ بِرِيحٍ طَيِّبَةٍ وَفَرِحُوا بِهَا﴾ أَيْ: بِسُرْعَةِ سَيْرِهِمْ رَافِقِينِ، فَبَيْنَمَا هُمْ كَذَلِكَ إِذْ ﴿جَاءَتْهَا﴾ أَيْ: تِلْكَ السُّفُنَ ﴿رِيحٌ عَاصِفٌ﴾ أَيْ: شَدِيدَةٌ ﴿وَجَاءَهُمُ الْمَوْجُ مِنْ كُلِّ مَكَانٍ﴾ أَيْ: اغْتَلَمَ الْبَحْرُ عَلَيْهِمْ ﴿وَظَنُّوا أَنَّهُمْ أُحِيطَ بِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: هَلَكُوا ﴿دَعَوُا اللَّهَ مُخْلِصِينَ لَهُ الدِّينَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَدْعُونَ مَعَهُ صَنَمًا وَلَا وَثَنًا، بَلْ يُفْرِدُونَهُ بِالدُّعَاءِ وَالِابْتِهَالِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِذَا مَسَّكُمُ الضُّرُّ فِي الْبَحْرِ ضَلَّ مَنْ تَدْعُونَ إِلا إِيَّاهُ فَلَمَّا نَجَّاكُمْ إِلَى الْبَرِّ أَعْرَضْتُمْ وَكَانَ الإنْسَانُ كَفُورًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٦٧] ، وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿دَعَوُا اللَّهَ مُخْلِصِينَ لَهُ الدِّينَ لَئِنْ أَنْجَيْتَنَا مِنْ هَذِهِ﴾ أَيْ: هَذِهِ الْحَالُ ﴿لَنَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الشَّاكِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا نُشْرِكُ بِكَ أَحَدًا، وَلَنُفْرِدَنَّكَ بِالْعِبَادَةِ هُنَاكَ كَمَا أَفْرَدْنَاكَ بِالدُّعَاءِ هَاهُنَا، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَلَمَّا أَنْجَاهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ تِلْكَ الْوَرْطَةِ ﴿إِذَا هُمْ يَبْغُونَ فِي الأرْضِ بِغَيْرِ الْحَقِّ﴾ أَيْ: كَأَنْ لَمْ يَكُنْ مِنْ ذَاكَ شَيْءٌ ﴿كَأَنْ لَمْ يَدْعُنَا إِلَى ضُرٍّ مَسَّهُ﴾

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ إِنَّمَا بَغْيُكُمْ عَلَى أَنْفُسِكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا يَذُوقُ وَبَالَ هَذَا الْبَغْيِ أَنْتُمْ أَنْفُسُكُمْ وَلَا تَضُرُّونَ بِهِ أَحَدًا غَيْرَكُمْ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "مَا مِنْ ذَنْبٍ أَجْدَرَ أَنْ يُعَجِّلَ اللَّهُ عُقُوبَتَهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا، مَعَ مَا يَدخر اللَّهُ لِصَاحِبِهِ فِي الْآخِرَةِ، مِنَ الْبَغْيِ وَقَطِيعَةِ الرَّحِمِ". 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مَتَاعَ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا لَكُمْ مَتَاعٌ فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا الدَّنِيئَةِ الْحَقِيرَةِ ﴿ثُمَّ إِلَيْنَا مَرْجِعُكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: مَصِيرُكُمْ وَمَآلُكُمْ ﴿فَنُنَبِّئُكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: فَنُخْبِرُكُمْ بِجَمِيعِ أَعْمَالِكُمْ، وَنُوَفِّيكُمْ إِيَّاهَا، فَمَنْ وَجَدَ خَيْرًا فَلْيَحْمَدِ اللَّهَ، وَمِنْ وجد غير ذلك فَلَا يَلُومَنَّ إِلَّا نَفْسَهُ.

---

## 10:24-25 — verses 24-25 (shared commentary)

### Translation

[Tabaraka wa] Ta'ala struck a parable for the flourishing of the life of this world and its adornment, and the swiftness of its passing away and vanishing, using the vegetation which Allah brings forth from the earth by means of the water He sends down from the sky, from which people eat crops and fruits of various kinds and varieties, and from which livestock eat herbage and fresh fodder and other things. {Until, when the earth has taken on its ornament}, that is, its perishable adornment, {and is beautified}, that is, made lovely by what emerges from its hillocks of fresh flowers of differing shapes and colors, {and its people think}, those who planted and cultivated it, {that they have power over it}, that is, over cutting and harvesting it, then while they are in that state a thunderbolt strikes it, or a sudden wind, and dries up its leaves and destroys its fruits. Therefore Allah, Ta'ala, says: {Our command comes to it by night or by day, and We make it a mown stubble}, that is, dry after that greenness and freshness, {as if it had not flourished yesterday}, that is, as if it had never been beautiful before that.

Qatadah said: {as if it had not flourished} means as if it had never enjoyed prosperity.

This is how affairs are after they pass away: as if they had never been. Therefore it is reported in the hadith that the most prosperous person of this world will be brought and dipped once into the Fire, then it will be said to him: "Have you ever seen any good? Has any comfort ever passed by you?" and he will say: "No." And the person who suffered the most severe torment in this world will be brought and dipped once into bliss, then it will be said to him: "Have you ever seen any hardship?" and he will say: "No."

Allah, Ta'ala, said, informing about those who were destroyed: {And they became, in their homes, fallen prostrate, as if they had never flourished therein} [Hud: 94, 95].

Then Allah, Ta'ala, says: {Thus do We set out in detail the signs}, that is, We make clear the proofs and evidences, {for a people who reflect}, so that they take heed by this parable regarding the swift passing away of this world from its people despite their being deceived by it and their being given a hold on its promises, and its slipping away from them. For it is in its very nature to flee from whoever seeks it, and to seek out whoever flees from it. Allah has struck the parable of the life of this world with the vegetation of the earth in more than one verse of His Mighty Book. He said in Surat al-Kahf: {And strike for them the parable of the life of this world: like water which We send down from the sky, so the vegetation of the earth mixes with it, and then it becomes dry debris scattered by the winds. And Allah is ever Powerful over all things} [al-Kahf: 45]. Likewise in Surat al-Zumar and al-Hadid He strikes the parable of the life of this world with water in a similar way.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Abd al-Rahman ibn Abi Bakr ibn Abd al-Rahman ibn al-Harith ibn Hisham said: I heard Marwan, meaning Ibn al-Hakam, reciting on the pulpit: "and is beautified, and its people think that they have power over it, and Allah would not destroy it except for the sins of its people." He said: I have recited it thus, but it is not in the mushaf. Abbas ibn Abd Allah ibn Abbas said: This is how Ibn Abbas recites it. So they sent to Ibn Abbas, and he said: This is how Ubayy ibn Ka'b taught me to recite it.

This is a gharib (singular) recitation, and it seems to be an addition by way of explanation.

Concerning His saying, {And Allah calls to the Abode of Peace} and the rest of the verse: when Allah, Ta'ala, mentioned this world and the swiftness of [its ruin and] its passing away, He encouraged desire for Paradise and called to it, and named it the Abode of Peace, that is, safe from afflictions, defects, and calamities. He said: {And Allah calls to the Abode of Peace and guides whom He wills to a straight path}.

Ayyub reported from Abu Qilabah, from the Prophet ﷺ, that he said: "It was said to me: 'Let your eye sleep, let your heart comprehend, and let your ear hear.' So my eye slept, my heart comprehended, and my ear heard. Then it was said: 'A master built a house, then prepared a banquet, and sent out a caller. Whoever answered the caller entered the house and ate from the banquet, and the master was pleased with him. And whoever did not answer the caller did not enter the house and did not eat from the banquet, and the master was not pleased with him. Allah is the Master, the house is Islam, the banquet is Paradise, and the caller is Muhammad ﷺ.'"

This is a mursal (chain missing the Companion) hadith, but it has come with a connected chain through the hadith of al-Layth, from Khalid ibn Yazid, from Sa'id ibn Abi Hilal, from Jabir ibn Abd Allah, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ came out to us one day and said: "I saw in a dream as if Gabriel were at my head and Michael at my feet, and one of them said to his companion: 'Strike a parable for him.' So he said: 'Listen, let your ear hear, and comprehend, let your heart comprehend. Your example and the example of your nation is like that of a king who took a house, then built within it a dwelling, then placed within it a banquet, then sent a messenger calling people to his food. Some of them answered the messenger, and some of them left him. Allah is the King, the house is Islam, the dwelling is Paradise, and you, O Muhammad, are the messenger. Whoever answers you enters Islam, and whoever enters Islam enters Paradise, and whoever enters Paradise eats from it.'" Narrated by Ibn Jarir.

Qatadah said: Khulayd al-Asari related to me, from Abu al-Darda, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "There is no day whose sun rises except that on its two sides are two angels calling out, heard by all of Allah's creation except mankind and jinn: 'O people, come to your Lord. Indeed what is little and sufficient is better than what is abundant and distracting.'" He said: And that was revealed in the Qur'an, in His saying: {And Allah calls to the Abode of Peace and guides whom He wills to a straight path}. Narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim and Ibn Jarir.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

ضَرَبَ [تَبَارَكَ وَ] تَعَالَى مَثَلًا لِزَهْرَةِ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَزِينَتِهَا وَسُرْعَةِ انْقِضَائِهَا وَزَوَالِهَا، بِالنَّبَاتِ الَّذِي أَخْرَجَهُ اللَّهُ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ بِمَا أَنْزَلَ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مِنَ الْمَاءِ، مِمَّا يَأْكُلُ النَّاسُ مِنْ زَرْعٍ وَثِمَارٍ، عَلَى اخْتِلَافِ أَنْوَاعِهَا وَأَصْنَافِهَا، وَمَا تَأْكُلُ الْأَنْعَامُ مِنْ أَبٍّ وقَضْب وَغَيْرِ ذَلِكَ، ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا أَخَذَتِ الأرْضُ زُخْرُفَهَا﴾ أَيْ: زِينَتَهَا الْفَانِيَةَ، ﴿وَازَّيَّنَتْ﴾ أَيْ: حَسُنت بِمَا خَرَجَ مِنْ رُباها مِنْ زُهُورٍ نَضِرة مُخْتَلِفَةِ الْأَشْكَالِ وَالْأَلْوَانِ، ﴿وَظَنَّ أَهْلُهَا﴾ الَّذِينَ زَرَعُوهَا وَغَرَسُوهَا ﴿أَنَّهُمْ قَادِرُونَ عَلَيْهَا﴾ أي: على جَذاذها وحصادها فبيناهم كذلك إذ جاءتها صاعقة، أو ريح بادرة، فَأَيْبَسَتْ أَوْرَاقَهَا، وَأَتْلَفَتْ ثِمَارَهَا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَتَاهَا أَمْرُنَا لَيْلا أَوْ نَهَارًا فَجَعَلْنَاهَا حَصِيدًا﴾ أَيْ: يَبَسًا بَعْدَ [تِلْكَ] الْخُضْرَةِ وَالنَّضَارَةِ، ﴿كَأَنْ لَمْ تَغْنَ بِالأمْسِ﴾ أَيْ: كَأَنَّهَا مَا كَانَتْ حَسْنَاءَ قَبْلَ ذَلِكَ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿كَأَنْ لَمْ تَغْنَ﴾ كَأَنَّ لَمْ تَنْعَمْ.

وَهَكَذَا الْأُمُورُ بَعْدَ زَوَالِهَا كَأَنَّهَا لَمْ تَكُنْ؛ وَلِهَذَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ يُؤْتَى بِأَنْعَمِ أَهْلِ الدُّنْيَا، فيُغْمَس فِي النَّارِ غَمْسَة ثُمَّ يُقَالُ لَهُ: هَلْ رَأَيْتَ خَيْرًا قَطُّ؟ [هَلْ مَرَّ بِكَ نَعِيمٌ قَطُّ؟] فَيَقُولُ: لَا. وَيُؤْتَى بِأَشَدِّ النَّاسِ عَذَابًا فِي الدُّنْيَا فَيُغْمَسُ فِي النَّعِيمِ غَمْسَةً، ثُمَّ يُقَالُ لَهُ: هَلْ رَأَيْتَ بُؤْسًا قَطُّ؟ فَيَقُولُ: لَا" 

وَقَالَ تَعَالَى إِخْبَارًا عَنِ الْمُهْلَكِينَ: ﴿فَأَصْبَحُوا فِي دِيَارِهِمْ جَاثِمِينَ كَأَنْ لَمْ يَغْنَوْا فِيهَا﴾ [هُودٍ: ٩٤، ٩٥] .

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿كَذَلِكَ نُفَصِّلُ الآيَاتِ﴾ أَيْ: نُبَيِّنُ الحُجج وَالْأَدِلَّةَ، ﴿لِقَوْمٍ يَتَفَكَّرُونَ﴾ فَيَعْتَبِرُونَ بِهَذَا الْمَثَلِ فِي زَوَالِ الدُّنْيَا مِنْ أَهْلِهَا سَرِيعًا مَعَ اغْتِرَارِهِمْ بِهَا، وَتَمَكُّنِهِمْ بِمَوَاعِيدِهَا وتَفَلّتها مِنْهُمْ، فَإِنَّ مِنْ طَبْعِهَا الْهَرَبَ مِمَّنْ طَلَبَهَا، وَالطَّلَبَ لِمَنْ هَرَبَ مِنْهَا، وَقَدْ ضَرَبَ اللَّهُ مَثَلَ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا بِنَبَاتِ الْأَرْضِ، فِي غَيْرِ مَا آيَةٍ مِنْ كِتَابِهِ الْعَزِيزِ، فَقَالَ فِي سُورَةِ الْكَهْفِ: ﴿وَاضْرِبْ لَهُمْ مَثَلَ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا كَمَاءٍ أَنزلْنَاهُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ فَاخْتَلَطَ بِهِ نَبَاتُ الأرْضِ فَأَصْبَحَ هَشِيمًا تَذْرُوهُ الرِّيَاحُ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ مُقْتَدِرًا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ٤٥] ، وَكَذَا فِي سُورَةِ الزُّمَرِ وَالْحَدِيدِ يَضْرِبُ بِذَلِكَ مَثَلَ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا كَمَاءٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي الْحَارِثُ حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ دِينَارٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ بْنِ هشام قال: سمعت مروان -يعني: ابن الْحَكَمِ -يَقْرَأُ عَلَى الْمِنْبَرِ: "وَازَّيَّنَتْ وَظَنَّ أَهْلُهَا أَنَّهُمْ قَادِرُونَ عَلَيْهَا وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُهْلِكَهَا إِلَّا بِذُنُوبِ أَهْلِهَا"، قَالَ: قَدْ قَرَأْتُهَا وَلَيْسَتْ فِي الْمُصْحَفِ فَقَالَ عَبَّاسُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: هَكَذَا يَقْرَؤُهَا ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ. فَأَرْسَلُوا إِلَى ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فَقَالَ: هَكَذَا أَقْرَأَنِي أُبَيُّ بْنُ كَعْبٍ. 

وَهَذِهِ قِرَاءَةٌ غَرِيبَةٌ، وَكَأَنَّهَا زِيَادَةٌ لِلتَّفْسِيرِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَاللَّهُ يَدْعُو إِلَى دَارِ السَّلامِ﴾ الْآيَةَ: لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى الدُّنْيَا وَسُرْعَةَ [عَطَبِهَا وَ] زَوَالِهَا، رغَّب فِي الْجَنَّةِ وَدَعَا إِلَيْهَا، وَسَمَّاهَا دَارَ السَّلَامِ أَيْ: مِنَ الْآفَاتِ، وَالنَّقَائِصِ وَالنَّكَبَاتِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَاللَّهُ يَدْعُو إِلَى دَارِ السَّلامِ وَيَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ إِلَى صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ﴾ .

قَالَ أَيُّوبُ عَنْ أَبِي قِلابة عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "قِيلَ لِي: لتنَمْ عينُك، وليعقلْ قَلْبُكَ، وَلْتَسْمَعْ أُذُنُكَ فَنَامَتْ عَيْنِي، وَعَقَلَ قَلْبِي، وَسَمِعَتْ أُذُنِي. ثُمَّ قِيلَ: سيّدٌ بَنَى دَارًا، ثُمَّ صَنَعَ مَأْدُبَةً، وَأَرْسَلَ دَاعِيًا، فَمَنْ أَجَابَ الدَّاعِيَ دَخَلَ الدَّارَ، وَأَكَلَ مِنَ الْمَأْدُبَةِ، وَرَضِيَ عَنْهُ السَّيِّدُ، وَمَنْ لَمْ يُجِبِ الدَّاعِيَ لَمْ يَدْخُلِ الدَّارَ، وَلَمْ يَأْكُلْ مِنَ الْمَأْدُبَةِ، وَلَمْ يَرْضَ عَنْهُ السَّيِّدُ فَاللَّهُ السَّيِّدُ، وَالدَّارُ الْإِسْلَامُ، وَالْمَأْدُبَةُ الْجَنَّةُ، وَالدَّاعِي مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ. 

وَهَذَا حَدِيثٌ مُرْسَلٌ، وَقَدْ جَاءَ مُتَّصِلًا مِنْ حَدِيثِ اللَّيْثِ، عَنْ خَالِدِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بن أبي هلال، عَنْ جَابِرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: خَرَجَ عَلَيْنَا رسولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَوْمًا فَقَالَ: "إِنِّي رَأَيْتُ فِي الْمَنَامِ كَأَنَّ جِبْرِيلَ عِنْدَ رَأْسِي، وَمِيكَائِيلَ عِنْدَ رِجْلِي، يَقُولُ أَحَدُهُمَا لِصَاحِبِهِ: اضْرِبْ لَهُ مَثَلًا. فَقَالَ: اسْمَعْ سَمعت أُذُنُكَ، وَاعْقِلْ عَقَل قَلْبُكَ، إِنَّمَا مَثَلُك وَمَثَلُ أمَّتك كَمَثَلِ مَلِكٍ اتَّخَذَ دَارًا، ثُمَّ بَنَى فِيهَا بَيْتًا، ثُمَّ جَعَلَ فِيهَا مَأْدُبَةً، ثُمَّ بَعَثَ رَسُولًا يَدْعُو النَّاسَ إِلَى طَعَامِهِ، فَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ أَجَابَ الرَّسُولَ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ تَرَكَهُ، فَاللَّهُ الْمَلِكُ، وَالدَّارُ الْإِسْلَامُ، وَالْبَيْتُ الْجَنَّةُ، وَأَنْتَ يَا مُحَمَّدُ الرسُول، فَمَنْ أَجَابَكَ دَخَلَ الْإِسْلَامَ، وَمَنْ دَخَلَ الْإِسْلَامَ دَخَلَ الْجَنَّةَ، وَمَنْ دَخَلَ الْجَنَّةَ أَكَلَ مِنْهَا" رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ. 

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: حَدَّثَنِي خُلَيْد العَصَري، عَنْ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا مِنْ يَوْمٍ طَلَعَتْ فِيهِ شَمْسُهُ إِلَّا وبجنَبَتَيْها مَلَكَانِ يُنَادِيَانِ يَسْمَعُهُمَا خَلْقُ اللَّهِ كُلُّهُمْ إِلَّا الثَّقَلَيْنِ: يَا أيها الناس، هَلُمُّوا إِلَى رَبِّكُمْ، إِنَّ مَا قلَّ وكَفَى، خَيْرٌ مِمَّا كَثُرَ وَأَلْهَى". قَالَ: وَأَنْزَلَ ذَلِكَ فِي الْقُرْآنِ، فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَاللَّهُ يَدْعُو إِلَى دَارِ السَّلامِ وَيَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ إِلَى صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ﴾ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

---

## 10:26 — verse 26

### Translation

The Almighty informs that whoever does good in this world through faith and righteous deeds, He will give him better in exchange in the abode of the hereafter, as the Almighty said: {Is the reward of goodness anything but goodness?} [Al-Rahman: 60].

As for His saying, {and increase}, this is the multiplication of the reward of deeds, a good deed being multiplied tenfold up to seven hundredfold, and an increase beyond that as well. It encompasses what Allah gives them in the Gardens of palaces and Houris, and His being pleased with them, and what He has hidden for them of delight for the eyes. And better than that and higher still is the looking upon His Noble Face, for that is an increase greater than everything else they were given, which they do not deserve by their deeds, but rather by His grace and mercy.

The interpretation of "the increase" as looking upon the Noble Face of Allah has been reported from Abu Bakr al-Siddiq, Hudhayfah ibn al-Yaman, and Abdullah ibn Abbas [al-Baghawi said: and Abu Musa and Ubadah ibn al-Samit], and Sa'id ibn al-Musayyib, Abd al-Rahman ibn Abi Layla, Abd al-Rahman ibn Sabit, Mujahid, Ikrimah, Amir ibn Sa'd, Ata', al-Dahhak, al-Hasan, Qatadah, al-Suddi, Muhammad ibn Ishaq, and others among the predecessors and successors.

Many hadiths have been transmitted on this subject from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ. Among them is what Imam Ahmad narrated:

[chain] Affan, Hammad ibn Salamah, from Thabit al-Bunani, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Abi Layla, from Suhayb: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ recited this verse, {For those who have done good is the best reward, and increase}, and said: "When the people of Paradise enter Paradise and the people of the Fire enter the Fire, a caller will call out: O people of Paradise, you have with Allah a promise which He wishes to fulfill for you. They will say: What is it? Has He not made our scales heavy, whitened our faces, admitted us into Paradise, and removed us far from the Fire? He said: Then the veil will be lifted for them, and they will look upon Him. By Allah, Allah never gave them anything more beloved to them than looking upon Him, nor more delightful to their eyes."

Thus it was narrated by Muslim and a group of the imams, from the hadith of Hammad ibn Salamah, with the same chain. Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Yunus, Ibn Wahb, Shabib, from Aban, from Abu Tamimah al-Hujaymi, that he heard Abu Musa al-Ash'ari narrate from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ: "Indeed Allah will send forth on the Day of Resurrection a caller who will call out: O people of Paradise, in a voice heard by the first of them and the last of them: Allah has promised you the best reward and an increase. The best reward is Paradise, and the increase is looking upon the Face of the Most Merciful, Mighty and Majestic is He."

It was also narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim, from the hadith of Abu Bakr al-Hudhali, from Abu Tamimah al-Hujaymi, with the same chain.

Ibn Jarir also said: [chain] Ibn Humayd, Ibrahim ibn al-Mukhtar, from Ibn Jurayj, from Ata', from Ka'b ibn Ujrah, from the Prophet ﷺ concerning His saying, {For those who have done good is the best reward, and increase}: he said it means looking upon the Face of the Most Merciful, Mighty and Majestic is He.

He also said: [chain] Ibn Abd al-Rahim, Amr ibn Abi Salamah, I heard Zuhayr from one who heard Abu al-Aliyah, Ubayy ibn Ka'b narrated: that he asked the Messenger of Allah ﷺ about the saying of Allah, Mighty and Majestic: {For those who have done good is the best reward, and increase}. He said: "The best reward is Paradise, and the increase is looking upon the Face of Allah, Mighty and Majestic is He."

This was also narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim, from the hadith of Zuhayr, with the same chain.

As for the Almighty's saying, {and no darkness will cover their faces}, that is, no gloom or blackness in the open spaces of the gathering, such as afflicts the faces of the disbelieving sinners in the form of darkness and dust. {nor humiliation}, that is, no disgrace or lowliness, meaning no humiliation will befall them, neither inwardly nor outwardly. Rather they will be as the Almighty said concerning them: {So Allah protected them from the evil of that day, and made them meet with radiance and joy}, meaning radiance on their faces and joy in their hearts. May Allah make us among them by His grace and mercy. Amin.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّ لِمَنْ أَحْسَنَ الْعَمَلَ فِي الدُّنْيَا بِالْإِيمَانِ وَالْعَمَلِ الصَّالِحِ أَبْدَلَهُ الْحُسْنَى فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿هَلْ جَزَاءُ الإحْسَانِ إِلا الإحْسَانُ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ: ٦٠] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَزِيَادَة﴾ هِيَ تَضْعِيفُ ثَوَابِ الْأَعْمَالِ بِالْحَسَنَةِ عَشْرَ أَمْثَالِهَا إِلَى سَبْعِمِائَةِ ضِعْفٍ، وَزِيَادَةٌ عَلَى ذَلِكَ [أَيْضًا] وَيَشْمَلُ مَا يُعْطِيهِمُ اللَّهُ فِي الْجِنَانِ مِنَ القُصُور والحُور وَالرِّضَا عَنْهُمْ، وَمَا أَخْفَاهُ لَهُمْ مِنْ قُرَّةِ أَعْيُنٍ، وَأَفْضَلُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ وَأَعْلَاهُ النظرُ إِلَى وَجْهِهِ الْكَرِيمِ، فَإِنَّهُ زِيَادَةٌ أَعْظَمُ مِنْ جَمِيعِ مَا أُعْطُوهُ، لَا يَسْتَحِقُّونَهَا بِعَمَلِهِمْ، بَلْ بِفَضْلِهِ وَرَحْمَتِهِ وَقَدْ رُوِيَ تَفْسِيرُ الزِّيَادَةِ بِالنَّظَرِ إِلَى وَجْهِ اللَّهِ الْكَرِيمِ، عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرٍ الصِّدِّيقِ، وَحُذَيْفَةَ بْنِ الْيَمَانِ، وَعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [قَالَ الْبَغَوِيُّ وَأَبُو مُوسَى وَعُبَادَةُ بْنُ الصَّامِتِ] وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ الْمُسَيَّبِ، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ أَبِي لَيْلَى، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ سَابِطٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَعَامِرُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، وَعَطَاءٌ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ مِنَ السَّلَفِ وَالْخَلَفِ.

وَقَدْ وَرَدَتْ فِي ذَلِكَ أحاديثُ كَثِيرَةٌ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَمِنْ ذَلِكَ مَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، أَخْبَرَنَا حَمَّادِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ ثَابِتٍ البُناني، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ أَبِي لَيْلَى، عَنْ صُهَيْبٍ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ تَلَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿لِلَّذِينَ أَحْسَنُوا الْحُسْنَى وَزِيَادَةٌ﴾ وَقَالَ: "إِذَا دَخَلَ أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ الْجَنَّةَ، وَأَهْلُ النَّارِ النَّارَ، نَادَى مُنَادٍ: يَا أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ، إِنَّ لَكُمْ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ مَوْعِدًا يُرِيدُ أَنْ يُنْجِزَكُمُوه. فَيَقُولُونَ: وَمَا هُوَ؟ أَلَمْ يُثقِّل مَوَازِينَنَا، وَيُبِيِّضْ وُجُوهَنَا، وَيُدْخِلْنَا الْجَنَّةَ، وَيُزَحْزِحْنَا مِنَ النَّارِ؟ ". قَالَ: "فَيَكْشِفُ لَهُمُ الْحِجَابَ، فَيَنْظُرُونَ إِلَيْهِ، فَوَاللَّهِ مَا أَعْطَاهُمُ اللَّهُ شَيْئًا أَحَبَّ إِلَيْهِمْ مِنَ النَّظَرِ إِلَيْهِ، وَلَا أَقَرَّ لِأَعْيُنِهِمْ".

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ وَجَمَاعَةٌ مِنَ الْأَئِمَّةِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ حَمَّادِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ، به. وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: أَخْبَرَنَا يُونُسُ، أَخْبَرَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ: أَخْبَرَنَا شَبِيبٌ، عَنْ أَبَانٍ عَنْ أَبِي تَمِيمَة الهُجَيْمي؛ أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ أَبَا مُوسَى الْأَشْعَرِيَّ يُحَدِّثُ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَبْعَثُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ مُنَادِيًا يُنَادِي: يَا أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ -بصَوْت يُسْمعُ أوَّلهم وَآخِرَهُمْ -: إِنَّ اللَّهَ وَعْدَكُمُ الْحُسْنَى وَزِيَادَةً، الْحُسْنَى: الْجَنَّةُ. وَزِيَادَةٌ: النَّظَرُ إِلَى وَجْهِ الرَّحْمَنِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ".

 وَرَوَاهُ أَيْضًا ابنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي بَكْرِ الهُذلي عَنْ أَبِي تَمِيمَةَ الْهُجَيْمِيِّ، بِهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ حُمَيْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ الْمُخْتَارِ عَنِ ابْنِ جُرَيْج، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنْ كَعْبِ بْنِ عُجْرة، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لِلَّذِينَ أَحْسَنُوا الْحُسْنَى وَزِيَادَةٌ﴾ قَالَ: النَّظَرُ إِلَى وَجْهِ الرَّحْمَنِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ. 

وَقَالَ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحِيمِ حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، سَمِعْتُ زُهَيْرًا عَمَّنْ سَمِعَ أَبَا الْعَالِيَةِ، حَدَّثَنَا أُبَيُّ بْنُ كَعْبٍ: أَنَّهُ سَأَلَ رسولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَنْ قَوْلِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿لِلَّذِينَ أَحْسَنُوا الْحُسْنَى وَزِيَادَةٌ﴾ قَالَ: "الْحُسْنَى: الْجَنَّةُ، وَالزِّيَادَةُ: النَّظَرُ إِلَى وَجْهِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ". 

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ أَيْضًا مِنْ حَدِيثِ زُهَيْرٍ، بِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا يَرْهَقُ وُجُوهَهُمْ قَتَرٌ﴾ أَيْ: قَتَامٌ وَسَوَادٌ فِي عَرَصات الْمَحْشَرِ، كَمَا يَعْتَرِي وُجُوهَ الْكَفَرَةِ الْفَجَرَةِ مِنَ القُتْرة والغُبْرة، ﴿وَلا ذِلَّةٌ﴾ أَيْ: هَوَانٌ وَصَغَارٌ، أَيْ: لَا يَحْصُلُ لَهُمْ إِهَانَةٌ فِي الْبَاطِنِ، وَلَا فِي الظَّاهِرِ، بَلْ هُمْ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى فِي حَقِّهِمْ: ﴿فَوَقَاهُمُ اللَّهُ شَرَّ ذَلِكَ الْيَوْمِ وَلَقَّاهُمْ نَضْرَةً وَسُرُورًا﴾ أَيْ: نَضْرَةً فِي وُجُوهِهِمْ، وَسُرُورًا فِي قُلُوبِهِمْ، جَعَلَنَا اللَّهُ مِنْهُمْ بِفَضْلِهِ وَرَحْمَتِهِ، آمِينَ.

---

## 10:27 — verse 27

### Translation

When the Exalted informed us about the state of the fortunate ones, for whom good deeds are multiplied and who receive even more beyond that, He followed this by mentioning the state of the wretched ones. He mentioned His justice, exalted is He, in dealing with them, and that He repays them for the evil deed with its like, adding nothing beyond that. {And humiliation covers them}, meaning: abasement befalls them and overtakes them because of their sins and their fear of them, just as the Exalted said: {And you will see them being brought to it, humbled by abasement, looking with a furtive glance} [al-Shura: 45]. And the Exalted said: {And do not think that Allah is unaware of what the wrongdoers do. He only defers them to a Day when eyes will stare in horror, hastening forward, their heads raised up, their eyes not returning to them, and their hearts empty. And warn the people of a Day when the punishment will come to them} [Ibrahim: 42-44]. And His saying {They will have no protector against Allah}, meaning: no preventer and no guardian to shield them from the punishment, just as the Exalted said: {Man will say on that Day, "Where is the escape?" No! There is no refuge. To your Lord that Day is the final place of rest} [al-Qiyamah: 10-12].

And His saying: {As if their faces were covered with pieces of the darkest night} is an announcement of the blackness of their faces in the Hereafter, just as the Exalted said: {On the Day when some faces will turn white and other faces will turn black. As for those whose faces turn black, it will be said: Did you disbelieve after your belief? Then taste the punishment for what you used to disbelieve. And as for those whose faces turn white, they will be in the mercy of Allah, abiding therein forever} [Al Imran: 106, 107]. And as the Exalted said: {Some faces on that Day will be bright, laughing, rejoicing. And other faces on that Day will have upon them dust, overcast by darkness. Those are the disbelievers, the wicked} [Abasa: 38-42], the verse.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى عَنْ حَالِ السُّعَدَاءِ الَّذِينَ يُضاعف لَهُمُ الْحَسَنَاتِ، وَيَزْدَادُونَ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، عَطَفَ بِذِكْرِ حَالِ الْأَشْقِيَاءِ، فَذَكَرَ عَدْلَهُ تَعَالَى فِيهِمْ، وَأَنَّهُ يُجَازِيهِمْ عَلَى السَّيِّئَةِ بِمِثْلِهَا، لَا يَزِيدُهُمْ عَلَى ذلك، ﴿وَتَرْهَقُهُم﴾ أَيْ: تَعْتَرِيهِمْ وَتَعْلُوهُمْ ذِلَّةٌ مِنْ مَعَاصِيهِمْ وَخَوْفِهِمْ مِنْهَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَتَرَاهُمْ يُعْرَضُونَ عَلَيْهَا خَاشِعِينَ مِنَ الذُّلِّ يَنْظُرُونَ مِنْ طَرْفٍ خَفِيٍّ﴾ [الشُّورَى: ٤٥] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا تَحْسَبَنَّ اللَّهَ غَافِلا عَمَّا يَعْمَلُ الظَّالِمُونَ إِنَّمَا يُؤَخِّرُهُمْ لِيَوْمٍ تَشْخَصُ فِيهِ الأبْصَارُ * مُهْطِعِينَ مُقْنِعِي رُءُوسِهِمْ لَا يَرْتَدُّ إِلَيْهِمْ طَرْفُهُمْ وَأَفْئِدَتُهُمْ هَوَاءٌ * وَأَنْذِرِ النَّاسَ يَوْمَ يَأْتِيهِمُ الْعَذَاب﴾ [إِبْرَاهِيمَ: ٤٢ -٤٤] ، وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿مَا لَهُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ مِنْ عَاصِمٍ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ مَانَعٍ وَلَا وَاقٍ يَقِيهِمُ الْعَذَابَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَقُولُ الإنْسَانُ يَوْمَئِذٍ أَيْنَ الْمَفَرُّ * كَلا لَا وَزَرَ * إِلَى رَبِّكَ يَوْمَئِذٍ الْمُسْتَقَرُّ﴾ [الْقِيَامَةِ: ١٠ -١٢] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿كَأَنَّمَا أُغْشِيَتْ وُجُوهُهُمْ قِطَعًا مِنَ اللَّيْلِ مُظْلِمًا﴾ إِخْبَارٌ عَنْ سَوَادِ وُجُوهِهِمْ فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ تَبْيَضُّ وُجُوهٌ وَتَسْوَدُّ وُجُوهٌ فَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ اسْوَدَّتْ وُجُوهُهُمْ أَكَفَرْتُمْ بَعْدَ إِيمَانِكُمْ فَذُوقُوا الْعَذَابَ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَكْفُرُونَ * وَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ ابْيَضَّتْ وُجُوهُهُمْ فَفِي رَحْمَةِ اللَّهِ هُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٠٦، ١٠٧] ، وَكَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وُجُوهٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ مُسْفِرَةٌ ضَاحِكَةٌ مُسْتَبْشِرَةٌ وَوُجُوهٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ عَلَيْهَا غَبَرَةٌ تَرْهَقُهَا قَتَرَةٌ أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْكَفَرَةُ الْفَجَرَةُ﴾ [عَبَسَ: ٣٨ -٤٢] . الْآيَةَ.

---

## 10:28-30 — verses 28-30 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: {And the Day We gather them} that is, all the inhabitants of the earth, humans and jinn alike, righteous and wicked, as He said: {And We gathered them, and We left not out of them anyone} [al-Kahf: 47].

{Then We will say to those who ascribed partners: "Stay in your places, you and your partners"} that is, remain, you and they, in a specific place, set apart there from the standing-place of the believers, as the Almighty said: {And separate yourselves this Day, O criminals} [Ya-Sin: 59], and He said: {And on the Day the Hour arises, on that Day they will be divided} [al-Rum: 14], and in another verse: {On that Day they will be sundered} [al-Rum: 43], meaning they will become split apart. This occurs when the Lord, the Almighty, comes to render final judgment. It is for this reason that it is said that the believers will intercede with God, the Almighty, asking that He come to render final judgment and give them relief from this standing-place of theirs. And in another hadith: "We on the Day of Resurrection will be upon a hillock above the people."

God, the Almighty, said in this noble verse, informing of what He will command the polytheists and their idols on the Day of Resurrection: {"Stay in your places, you and your partners." Then We separated them, and their partners said, "You were not worshipping us"} They denied being worshipped by them and disavowed them, as the Almighty said: {[No] they will deny their worship and will be against them opponents} the verse. [Maryam: 82]. And He said: {When those who were followed disown those who followed [them]} [al-Baqarah: 166], and He said: {And who is more astray than one who calls upon, besides God, that which does not answer him until the Day of Resurrection, and they are unaware of their calling upon them? And when mankind is gathered, they will be enemies to them, and will be deniers of their worship} [al-Ahqaf: 5, 6].

And He said in this verse, informing of what the partners will say in their reply to their worshippers when the latter claim to have worshipped them: {"So God is sufficient as a witness between us and you. Indeed, we were unaware of your worship"} that is: we did not perceive it and did not know of it; rather, you used to worship us without our being aware of you, and God is a witness between us and you that we did not call you to worship us, nor command you to do so, nor were We pleased with that from you.

In this there is a tremendous rebuke of the polytheists who worshipped, besides God, others who neither hear nor see, and can avail them nothing, and who did not command them to do so, nor were pleased with it, nor desired it. Rather, they disown them at the very time when they are in greatest need of them, after they had abandoned the worship of the Ever-Living, the Self-Subsisting, the All-Hearing, the All-Seeing, the One capable of all things, the All-Knowing of all things, who had sent His messengers and revealed His books, commanding worship of Him alone with no partner, and forbidding worship of anything besides Him, as the Almighty said: {And We have certainly sent into every nation a messenger, [saying], "Worship God and avoid al-Taghut (false deities)."} Then some of them were guided by God, and some of them deserved to be led astray} [al-Nahl: 36], and the Almighty said: {And We sent not before you any messenger except that We revealed to him that, "There is no deity except Me, so worship Me"} [al-Anbiya: 25], and He said: {And ask those We sent before you of Our messengers, "Did We make, besides the Most Merciful, deities to be worshipped?"} [al-Zukhruf: 45].

The polytheists are of many kinds and categories, which God has mentioned in His Book, clarifying their states and their sayings, and refuting them, regarding what they were engaged in, with the most complete refutation.

His saying: {There every soul will be tested for what it did before} that is, in the standing-place of reckoning on the Day of Resurrection, every soul will be tested and will come to know what it sent ahead of [its deeds], of good and evil, as the Almighty said: {The Day when secrets will be tested} [al-Tariq: 9], and the Almighty said: {Man will be informed, that Day, of what he put forth and what he left behind} [al-Qiyamah: 13], and the Almighty said: {And We will bring forth for him on the Day of Resurrection a record which he will encounter spread open. "Read your record. Sufficient is yourself against you this Day as a reckoner"} [al-Isra: 13, 14].

Some have recited it: {There every soul will follow what it did before} (tatlu instead of tabluu), and some have interpreted it as meaning recitation, while others have interpreted it as meaning that it follows what it had sent ahead of good and evil, and others have interpreted it by the hadith: "Every nation will follow what it used to worship: the one who used to worship the sun will follow the sun, the one who used to worship the moon will follow the moon, and the one who used to worship the false deities (tawaghit) will follow the false deities" the hadith [continues].

His saying: {And they are returned to God, their true Protector} that is, all matters return to God, the Just Arbiter, who will decide between them, admitting the people of Paradise into Paradise and the people of the Fire into the Fire.

{And lost from them} that is, it vanished from the polytheists, {what they used to invent} that is, what they used to worship besides God, in fabrication against Him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَوْمَ نَحْشُرُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَهْلَ الْأَرْضِ كُلَّهُمْ، مِنْ إِنْسٍ وَجِنٍّ وَبَرٍّ وَفَاجِرٍ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَحَشَرْنَاهُمْ فَلَمْ نُغَادِرْ مِنْهُمْ أَحَدًا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ٤٧] .

﴿ثُمَّ نَقُولُ لِلَّذِينَ أَشْرَكُوا مَكَانَكُمْ أَنْتُمْ وَشُرَكَاؤُكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: الْزَمُوا أَنْتُمْ وَهَمَ مَكَانًا مُعَيَّنًا، امْتَازُوا فِيهِ عَنْ مَقَامِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَامْتَازُوا الْيَوْمَ أَيُّهَا الْمُجْرِمُونَ﴾ [يس: ٥٩] ، وَقَالَ ﴿وَيَوْمَ تَقُومُ السَّاعَةُ يَوْمَئِذٍ يَتَفَرَّقُونَ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ١٤] ، وَفِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿يَوْمَئِذٍ يَصَّدَّعُونَ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٤٣] أَيْ: يَصِيرُونَ صِدعين، وَهَذَا يَكُونُ إِذَا جَاءَ الرَّبُّ تَعَالَى لِفَصْلِ الْقَضَاءِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قِيلَ: ذَلِكَ يَسْتَشْفِعُ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ إِلَى اللَّهِ تَعَالَى أَنْ يَأْتِيَ لِفَصْلِ الْقَضَاءِ وَيُرِيحَنَا مِنْ مَقَامِنَا هَذَا، وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الْآخَرِ: "نَحْنُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ على كَوْم فوق الناس. وَقَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ إِخْبَارًا عَمَّا يَأْمُرُ بِهِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ وَأَوْثَانَهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ: ﴿مَكَانَكُمْ أَنْتُمْ وَشُرَكَاؤُكُمْ فَزَيَّلْنَا بَيْنَهُمْ وَقَالَ شُرَكَاؤُهُمْ مَا كُنْتُمْ إِيَّانَا تَعْبُدُونَ﴾ أَنْكَرُوا عِبَادَتَهُمْ، وَتَبَرَّءُوا مِنْهُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ [كَلا] سَيَكْفُرُونَ بِعِبَادَتِهِمْ وَيَكُونُونَ عَلَيْهِمْ ضِدًّا﴾ الْآيَةَ. [مَرْيَمَ: ٨٢] . وَقَالَ: ﴿إِذْ تَبَرَّأَ الَّذِينَ اتُّبِعُوا مِنَ الَّذِينَ اتَّبَعُوا﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ١٦٦] ، وَقَالَ ﴿وَمَنْ أَضَلُّ مِمَّنْ يَدْعُو مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ مَنْ لَا يَسْتَجِيبُ لَهُ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ وَهُمْ عَنْ دُعَائِهِمْ غَافِلُونَ وَإِذَا حُشِرَ النَّاسُ كَانُوا لَهُمْ أَعْدَاءً وَكَانُوا بِعِبَادَتِهِمْ كَافِرِينَ﴾ [الْأَحْقَافِ: ٥، ٦] .

وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ إِخْبَارًا عَنْ قَوْلِ الشُّرَكَاءِ فِيمَا رَاجَعُوا فِيهِ عَابِدِيهِمْ عِنْدَ ادِّعَائِهِمْ عِبَادَتَهُمْ: ﴿فَكَفَى بِاللَّهِ شَهِيدًا بَيْنَنَا وَبَيْنَكُمْ إِنْ كُنَّا عَنْ عِبَادَتِكُمْ لَغَافِلِينَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا كُنَّا نَشْعُرُ بِهَا وَلَا نَعْلَمُ، وَإِنَّمَا أَنْتُمْ كُنْتُمْ تَعْبُدُونَنَا مِنْ حَيْثُ لَا نَدْرِي بِكُمْ، وَاللَّهُ شَهِيدٌ بَيْنَنَا وَبَيْنَكُمْ أَنَّا مَا دَعَوْنَاكُمْ إِلَى عِبَادَتِنَا، وَلَا أَمَرْنَاكُمْ بِهَا، وَلَا رَضِينَا مِنْكُمْ بِذَلِكَ.

وَفِي هَذَا تَبْكِيتٌ عَظِيمٌ لِلْمُشْرِكِينَ الَّذِينَ عَبَدُوا مَعَ اللَّهِ غَيْرَهُ، مِمَّنْ لَا يَسْمَعُ وَلَا يُبَصِّرُ، وَلَا يُغْنِي عَنْهُمْ شَيْئًا، وَلَمْ يَأْمُرْهُمْ بِذَلِكَ وَلَا رَضِيَ بِهِ وَلَا أَرَادَهُ، بَلْ تَبْرَأُ مِنْهُمْ فِي وَقْتٍ أَحْوَجَ مَا يَكُونُونَ إِلَيْهِ، وَقَدْ تَرَكُوا عِبَادَةَ الْحَيِّ الْقَيُّومِ، السَّمِيعِ الْبَصِيرِ، الْقَادِرِ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، الْعَلِيمِ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ وَقَدْ أَرْسَلَ رُسُلَهُ وَأَنْزَلَ كُتُبَهُ، آمِرًا بِعِبَادَتِهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، نَاهِيًا عَنْ عِبَادَةِ مَا سِوَاهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ بَعَثْنَا فِي كُلِّ أُمَّةٍ رَسُولا أَنِ اُعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ وَاجْتَنِبُوا الطَّاغُوتَ فَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ هَدَى اللَّهُ وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ حَقَّتْ عَلَيْهِ الضَّلالَةُ﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ٣٦] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِكَ مِنْ رَسُولٍ إِلا نُوحِي إِلَيْهِ أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا أَنَا فَاعْبُدُونِ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ٢٥] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَاسْأَلْ مَنْ أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِكَ مِنْ رُسُلِنَا أَجَعَلْنَا مِنْ دُونِ الرَّحْمَنِ آلِهَةً يُعْبَدُونَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ: ٤٥] .

وَالْمُشْرِكُونَ أَنْوَاعٌ وَأَقْسَامٌ كَثِيرُونَ، قَدْ ذَكَرَهُمُ اللَّهُ فِي كِتَابِهِ، وبَيّن أَحْوَالَهُمْ وَأَقْوَالَهُمْ، ورَد عَلَيْهِمْ فِيمَا هُمْ فِيهِ أَتَمَّ رَدٍّ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿هُنَالِكَ تَبْلُو كُلُّ نَفْسٍ مَا أَسْلَفَتْ﴾ أَيْ: فِي مَوْقِفِ الْحِسَابِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ تُخْتَبَرُ كُلُّ نَفْسٍ وَتَعْلَمُ مَا أَسْلَفَتْ مِنْ [عَمَلِهَا مِنْ] خَيْرٍ وَشَرٍّ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ تُبْلَى السَّرَائِرُ﴾ [الطَّارِقِ: ٩] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يُنَبَّأُ الإنْسَانُ يَوْمَئِذٍ بِمَا قَدَّمَ وَأَخَّرَ﴾ [الْقِيَامَةِ: ١٣] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَنُخْرِجُ لَهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ كِتَابًا يَلْقَاهُ مَنْشُورًا اقْرَأْ كِتَابَكَ كَفَى بِنَفْسِكَ الْيَوْمَ عَلَيْكَ حَسِيبًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ١٣، ١٤] .

وَقَدْ قَرَأَ بَعْضُهُمْ: ﴿هُنَالِكَ تَتْلُو كُلُّ نَفْسٍ مَا أَسْلَفَتْ﴾ وفسَّرها بَعْضُهُمْ بِالْقِرَاءَةِ، وَفَسَّرَهَا بَعْضُهُمْ بِمَعْنَى تَتْبَعُ مَا قَدَّمَتْهُ مِنْ خَيْرٍ وَشَرٍّ، وَفَسَّرَهَا بَعْضُهُمْ بِحَدِيثِ: "تَتْبَعُ كُلُّ أُمَّةٍ مَا كَانَتْ تعبد، فيتبع من كَانَ يَعْبُدُ الشَّمْسَ الشَّمْسَ، وَيَتْبَعُ مَنْ كَانَ يَعْبُدُ الْقَمَرَ الْقَمَرَ، وَيَتْبَعُ مَنْ كَانَ يَعْبُدُ الطَّوَاغِيتَ الطَّوَاغِيتَ" الْحَدِيثَ. 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَرُدُّوا إِلَى اللَّهِ مَوْلاهُمُ الْحَقِّ﴾ أَيْ: وَرَجَعْتِ الْأُمُورُ كُلُّهَا إِلَى اللَّهِ الْحَكَمِ الْعَدْلِ، فَفَصَّلَهَا، وَأَدْخَلَ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ الْجَنَّةَ، وَأَهْلَ النَّارِ النَّارَ.

﴿وَضَلَّ عَنْهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: ذَهَبَ عَنِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ ﴿مَا كَانُوا يَفْتَرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا كَانُوا يَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ افْتِرَاءً عَلَيْهِ.

---

## 10:31-33 — verses 31-33 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Allah, exalted is He, argues against the polytheists by way of their own acknowledgment of His oneness and His lordship, in order to establish the oneness of divinity. He says: {Say: Who provides for you from the heaven and the earth} that is, who is it that sends down from the sky the water of rain, then cleaves the earth open by His power and His will, and brings forth from it {grain and grapes and fresh vegetation, and olives and palm trees, and gardens dense with trees, and fruit and fodder} [Abasa: 27-31]? Is there a god alongside Allah? They will say: Allah. {Or who is it that provides for you if He withholds His provision?} [al-Mulk: 21]. Likewise His saying: {Or who possesses hearing and sight?} [Yunus: 31], that is, He who granted you this faculty of hearing and this faculty of sight, and had He willed He could have taken them away and stripped them from you, as He, exalted is He, says: {Say: He is the One who brought you into being and made for you hearing and sight and hearts; little do you give thanks} [al-Mulk: 23]. And He says: {Say: Have you considered, if Allah took away your hearing and your sight and sealed your hearts, what god other than Allah could bring it back to you?} [al-An'am: 46].

His saying: {And who brings forth the living from the dead and brings forth the dead from the living}, that is, by His tremendous power and His all-encompassing favor. The disagreement concerning this matter has already been mentioned, and that the verse is general, covering all of it.

His saying: {And who arranges every matter}, that is, He in whose hand is dominion over everything, He grants protection and none can grant protection against Him, He is the One who disposes and rules, whose judgment none can overturn, who is not questioned about what He does while they themselves will be questioned. {Whoever is in the heavens and the earth asks of Him; every day He is upon some matter} [al-Rahman: 29]. So the entire dominion, the higher and the lower, and whatever is within them of angels, humans, and jinn, are all in need of Him, servants to Him, submissive before Him. {They will say: Allah}, that is, they know this and acknowledge it. {Say: Will you not then fear Him?}, that is, will you not fear Him, that you should worship besides Him another, out of your own opinions and your ignorance?

His saying: {That, then, is Allah, your true Lord. What is there after truth except error? How then are you turned away?}, that is, this One whom you have acknowledged to be the doer of all of that, He is your Lord and your true God, who deserves to be worshipped alone. {What is there after truth except error?}, that is, every object of worship besides Him is false; there is no god but He, One, having no partner.

{How then are you turned away?}, that is, how are you turned away from His worship to the worship of something other than Him, while you know that He is the Lord who created everything and who disposes of everything?

His saying: {Thus has the word of your Lord been realized against those who transgressed, that they do not believe}, that is, just as these polytheists disbelieved and persisted in their idolatry and in worshipping besides Allah others, despite the fact that they acknowledge that He is the Creator, the Provider, the sole Disposer of the dominion, who sent His messengers with His oneness. For this reason the word of Allah was realized against them, that they are among the wretched, the inhabitants of the Fire, just as He says: {They will say: Yes indeed, but the word of punishment has been realized against the disbelievers} [al-Zumar: 71].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَحْتَجُّ تَعَالَى عَلَى الْمُشْرِكِينَ بِاعْتِرَافِهِمْ بِوَحْدَانِيَّتِهِ وَرُبُوبِيَّتِهِ عَلَى وَحْدَانِيَّةِ الْإِلَهِ فَقَالَ: ﴿قُلْ مَنْ يَرْزُقُكُمْ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ أَيْ: مَنْ ذَا الَّذِي يُنْزِلُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مَاءَ الْمَطَرِ، فَيَشُقُّ الْأَرْضَ شَقًا بِقُدْرَتِهِ وَمَشِيئَتِهِ، فَيُخْرِجُ مِنْهَا ﴿حَبًّا وَعِنَبًا وَقَضْبًا وَزَيْتُونًا وَنَخْلا وَحَدَائِقَ غُلْبًا وَفَاكِهَةً وَأَبًّا﴾ [عَبَسَ: ٢٧ -٣١] ، أَإِلَهٌ مَعَ اللَّهِ؟ فَسَيَقُولُونَ: اللَّهُ، ﴿أَمَّنْ هَذَا الَّذِي يَرْزُقُكُمْ إِنْ أَمْسَكَ رِزْقَهُ﴾ [الْمُلْكِ: ٢١] ؟، وَكَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَمَّنْ يَمْلِكُ السَّمْعَ وَالأبْصَارَ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٣١] ؟ ؟ أَيْ: الَّذِي وَهَبَكُمْ هَذِهِ الْقُوَّةَ السَّامِعَةَ، وَالْقُوَّةَ الْبَاصِرَةَ، وَلَوْ شَاءَ لَذَهَبَ بِهَا وَلَسَلَبَكُمْ إِيَّاهَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ هُوَ الَّذِي أَنْشَأَكُمْ وَجَعَلَ لَكُمُ السَّمْعَ وَالأبْصَارَ وَالأفْئِدَةَ قَلِيلا مَا تَشْكُرُونَ﴾ [الْمُلْكِ: ٢٣] ، وَقَالَ ﴿قُلْ أَرَأَيْتُمْ إِنْ أَخَذَ اللَّهُ سَمْعَكُمْ وَأَبْصَارَكُمْ وَخَتَمَ عَلَى قُلُوبِكُمْ مَنْ إِلَهٌ غَيْرُ اللَّهِ يَأْتِيكُمْ بِهِ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٤٦] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَنْ يُخْرِجُ الْحَيَّ مِنَ الْمَيِّتِ وَيُخْرِجُ الْمَيِّتَ مِنَ الْحَيِّ﴾ أَيْ: بِقُدْرَتِهِ الْعَظِيمَةِ، وَمِنَّتِهِ الْعَمِيمَةِ، وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ ذِكْرُ الْخِلَافِ فِي ذَلِكَ، وَأَنَّ الْآيَةَ عَامَّةٌ فِي ذَلِكَ كُلِّهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَنْ يُدَبِّرُ الأمْرَ﴾ أَيْ: مَنْ بِيَدِهِ مَلَكُوتُ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ وَهُوَ يُجِيرُ وَلَا يُجَارُ عَلَيْهِ، وَهُوَ الْمُتَصَرِّفُ الْحَاكِمُ الَّذِي لَا مُعَقِّبَ لِحُكْمِهِ، وَلَا يُسأل عَمَّا يَفْعَلُ وَهُمْ يُسْألُون، ﴿يَسْأَلُهُ مَنْ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ كُلَّ يَوْمٍ هُوَ فِي شَأْنٍ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ: ٢٩] ، فَالْمُلْكُ كُلُّهُ الْعُلْوِيُّ وَالسُّفْلِيُّ، وَمَا فِيهِمَا مِنْ مَلَائِكَةٍ وَإِنْسٍ وَجَانٍّ، فَقِيرُونَ إِلَيْهِ، عَبِيدٌ لَهُ، خَاضِعُونَ لَدَيْهِ، ﴿فَسَيَقُولُونَ اللَّهُ﴾ أَيْ: هم يعلمون ذلك وَيَعْتَرِفُونَ بِهِ، ﴿فَقُلْ أَفَلا تَتَّقُونَ﴾ أَيْ: أَفَلَا تَخَافُونَ مِنْهُ أَنْ تَعْبُدُوا مَعَهُ غَيْرَهُ بِآرَائِكُمْ وَجَهِلِكُمْ؟.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَذَلِكُمُ اللَّهُ رَبُّكُمُ الْحَقُّ فَمَاذَا بَعْدَ الْحَقِّ إِلا الضَّلالُ فَأَنَّى تُصْرَفُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فَهَذَا الَّذِي اعْتَرَفْتُمْ بِأَنَّهُ فَاعِلٌ ذَلِكَ كُلَّهُ هُوَ رَبُّكُمْ وَإِلَهُكُمُ الْحَقُّ الَّذِي يَسْتَحِقُّ أَنْ يُفْرَدَ بِالْعِبَادَةِ، ﴿فَمَاذَا بَعْدَ الْحَقِّ إِلا الضَّلالُ﴾ أَيْ: فَكُلُّ مَعْبُودٍ سِوَاهُ بَاطِلٌ، لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ، وَاحِدٌ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ.

﴿فَأَنَّى تُصْرَفُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فَكَيْفَ تُصْرَفُونَ عَنْ عِبَادَتِهِ إِلَى عِبَادَةِ مَا سِوَاهُ، وَأَنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّهُ الرَّبُّ الَّذِي خَلَقَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ، وَالْمُتَصَرِّفُ فِي كُلِّ شَيْءٍ؟

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿كَذَلِكَ حَقَّتْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ عَلَى الَّذِينَ فَسَقُوا أَنَّهُمْ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: كَمَا كَفَرَ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُشْرِكُونَ وَاسْتَمَرُّوا عَلَى شِرْكِهِمْ وَعِبَادَتِهِمْ مَعَ اللَّهِ غَيْرَهُ، مَعَ أَنَّهُمْ يَعْتَرِفُونَ بِأَنَّهُ الْخَالِقُ الرَّازِقُ الْمُتَصَرِّفُ فِي الْمُلْكِ وَحْدَهُ، الَّذِي بَعَثَ رُسُلَهُ بِتَوْحِيدِهِ؛ فَلِهَذَا حَقَّتْ عَلَيْهِمْ كَلِمَةُ اللَّهِ أَنَّهُمْ أَشْقِيَاءُ مِنْ سَاكِنِي النَّارِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿قَالُوا بَلَى وَلَكِنْ حَقَّتْ كَلِمَةُ الْعَذَابِ عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ﴾ [الزمر: ٧١] .

---

## 10:34-36 — verses 34-36 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is a refutation of their claim regarding what they associated with Allah besides Him, and what they worshipped among idols and rivals. {Say: Is there among your partners one who originates creation and then repeats it?} That is: who originated the creation of these heavens and earth, then brings into being the creatures within them, and disperses the bodies of the heavens and earth and replaces them after what is in them has perished, then repeats creation as a new creation? {Say: Allah}, He is the One who does this and does it alone, He alone with no partner, {so how are you turned away?} That is: how are you diverted from the path of right guidance to falsehood?!

{Say: Is there among your partners one who guides to the truth? Say: Allah guides to the truth.} That is: you yourselves know that your partners are not able to guide anyone astray back to guidance, whereas it is Allah who guides the bewildered and the misguided, and turns hearts from error to right guidance, He besides whom there is no god.

{Is then He who guides to the truth more worthy to be followed, or he who does not guide unless he is guided?} That is: should the servant who guides to the truth and gives insight after blindness be followed, or the one who guides to nothing unless he himself is guided, because of his blindness and muteness? As Allah relates, informing us about Ibrahim (peace be upon him), that he said: {O my father, why do you worship that which does not hear, does not see, and cannot benefit you in anything?} [Maryam: 42], and he said to his people: {Do you worship what you carve, when Allah has created you and what you make?} [al-Saffat: 95-96], among other similar verses.

Regarding His saying: {What is the matter with you, how do you judge?} That is: what has happened to you, that your minds have been carried away, that you have made Allah and His creation equal, equating this with that, and worshipping this and that? Why did you not single out the Lord, exalted is His majesty, the Owner, the Judge, the One who guides out of misguidance, with worship alone, and devote to Him alone your calling and your turning in repentance?

Then Allah, exalted is He, makes clear that they do not follow, in this religion of theirs, any proof or evidence, rather it is mere conjecture on their part, that is, supposition and imagination, and that avails them nothing. {Indeed Allah is fully aware of what they do} is a warning to them and a severe threat, for Allah, exalted is He, informs that He will requite them for that with the fullest requital.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

وَهَذَا إِبْطَالٌ لِدَعْوَاهُمْ فِيمَا أَشْرَكُوا بِاللَّهِ غَيْرَهُ، وَعَبَدُوا مِنَ الْأَصْنَامِ وَالْأَنْدَادِ، ﴿قُلْ هَلْ مِنْ شُرَكَائِكُمْ مَنْ يَبْدَأُ الْخَلْقَ ثُمَّ يُعِيدُهُ﴾ أَيْ: مَنْ بَدَأَ خَلْقَ هَذِهِ السموات وَالْأَرْضِ ثُمَّ يُنْشِئُ مَا فِيهِمَا مِنَ الْخَلَائِقِ، ويفرق أجرام السموات وَالْأَرْضِ وَيُبْدِلْهُمَا بِفَنَاءِ مَا فِيهِمَا، ثُمَّ يُعِيدُ الْخَلْقَ خَلْقًا جَدِيدًا؟ ﴿قُلِ اللَّهُ﴾ هُوَ الَّذِي يَفْعَلُ هَذَا وَيَسْتَقِلُّ بِهِ، وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، ﴿فَأَنَّى تُؤْفَكُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فَكَيْفَ تُصْرَفُونَ عَنْ طَرِيقِ الرُّشْدِ إِلَى الْبَاطِلِ؟!

﴿قُلْ هَلْ مِنْ شُرَكَائِكُمْ مَنْ يَهْدِي إِلَى الْحَقِّ قُلِ اللَّهُ يَهْدِي لِلْحَقِّ﴾ أَيْ: أَنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّ شُرَكَاءَكُمْ لَا تَقْدِرُ عَلَى هِدَايَةِ ضَالٍّ، وَإِنَّمَا يَهْدِي الْحَيَارَى وَالضُّلَّالَ، وَيُقَلِّبُ الْقُلُوبَ مِنَ الْغَيِّ إِلَى الرُّشْدِ اللَّهُ، الَّذِي لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ.

﴿أَفَمَنْ يَهْدِي إِلَى الْحَقِّ أَحَقُّ أَنْ يُتَّبَعَ أَمَّنْ لَا يَهِدِّي إِلا أَنْ يُهْدَى﴾ أَيْ: أَفَيُتَّبَع [العبد الذي يهدي إلى الْحَقِّ ويُبَصّر بَعْدَ الْعَمَى، أَمِ الَّذِي لَا يَهْدِي إِلَى شَيْءٍ إِلَّا] أَنْ يُهْدَى، لِعَمَاهُ وَبُكْمِهِ؟ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى إِخْبَارًا عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: ﴿يَا أَبَتِ لِمَ تَعْبُدُ مَا لَا يَسْمَعُ وَلا يُبْصِرُ وَلا يُغْنِي عَنْكَ شَيْئًا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ: ٤٢] ، وَقَالَ لِقَوْمِهِ: ﴿أَتَعْبُدُونَ مَا تَنْحِتُونَ وَاللَّهُ خَلَقَكُمْ وَمَا تَعْمَلُون﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ: ٩٥، ٩٦] إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَمَا لَكُمْ كَيْفَ تَحْكُمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فَمَا بَالُكُمْ يُذْهَبُ بِعُقُولِكُمْ، كَيْفَ سَوَّيْتُمْ بَيْنَ اللَّهِ وَبَيْنَ خَلقه، وَعَدَلْتُمْ هَذَا بِهَذَا، وَعَبَدْتُمْ هَذَا وَهَذَا؟ وَهَلَّا أَفْرَدْتُمُ الرَّبَّ جَلَّ جَلَالُهُ الْمَالِكَ الْحَاكِمَ الْهَادِيَ مِنَ الضَّلَالَةِ بِالْعِبَادَةِ وَحْدَهُ، وَأَخْلَصْتُمْ إِلَيْهِ الدَّعْوَةَ وَالْإِنَابَةَ.

ثُمَّ بَيَّنَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُمْ لَا يَتَّبِعُونَ فِي دِينِهِمْ هَذَا دَلِيلًا وَلَا بُرْهَانًا، وَإِنَّمَا هُوَ ظَنٌّ مِنْهُمْ، أَيْ: تَوَهُّمٌ وَتَخَيُّلٌ، وَذَلِكَ لَا يُغْنِي عَنْهُمْ شَيْئًا، ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَلِيمٌ بِمَا يَفْعَلُونَ﴾ تَهْدِيدٌ لَهُمْ، وَوَعِيدٌ شَدِيدٌ؛ لِأَنَّهُ تَعَالَى أَخْبَرَ أَنَّهُ سَيُجَازِيهِمْ عَلَى ذَلِكَ أَتَمَّ الْجَزَاءِ.

---

## 10:37-40 — verses 37-40 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is a clarification of the inimitability of the Qur'an, and that human beings are not able to produce its like, nor the like of ten surahs of it, nor the like of a single surah of it, because by its eloquence, its rhetorical excellence, its conciseness, its sweetness, and its containing precious meanings beneficial in this world and the next, it cannot be but from God, to whom nothing is similar in His essence, nor in His attributes, nor in His acts and words. His speech does not resemble the speech of created beings. This is why the Exalted said: {And this Qur'an is not such as could be produced by other than God} meaning, the like of this Qur'an cannot be but from God, and this does not resemble the speech of human beings, {but is a confirmation of what came before it} meaning, of the previous scriptures, and a guardian over them, and a clarification of the distortion, misinterpretation, and alteration that occurred in them.

His saying: {and a detailed explanation of the Book, about which there is no doubt, from the Lord of the worlds} means, and a clarification of the rulings, the lawful and the unlawful, a clarification that is complete, sufficient, true, in which there is no doubt, from God, Lord of the worlds. As was mentioned previously in the hadith of al-Harith al-A'war, from Ali ibn Abi Talib: "In it is news of what came before you, and information of what will come after you, and a judgment concerning what is between you," meaning, news of what has passed and of what is to come, and a ruling among people by the Law which God loves and is pleased with.

His saying: {Or do they say he fabricated it? Say: Then bring a surah like it, and call upon whomever you can besides God, if you are truthful} means, if you claim, fabricate, and doubt that this is from God, and say falsely and deceitfully: "This is from Muhammad," then Muhammad is a human being like you, and he has come with what you claim to be this Qur'an, so you bring a surah like it, that is, of the same kind as the Qur'an, and seek help in that from whomever you are able to, of humans and jinn.

This is the third stage in the challenge. For the Exalted challenged them and called upon them, if they were truthful in their claim that it was from Muhammad, to oppose it with the like of what he alone brought, and to seek help from whomever they wished. And He informed that they would not be able to do that, and that there was no way for them to it. So the Exalted said: {Say: If mankind and the jinn gathered together to produce the like of this Qur'an, they could not produce the like of it, even if they were to each other assistants} [al-Isra: 88]. Then He reduced it for them to ten surahs of it, saying at the beginning of Surah Hud: {Or do they say he fabricated it? Say: Then bring ten fabricated surahs like it, and call upon whomever you can besides God, if you are truthful} [Hud: 13]. Then He lowered it further to a single surah, saying in this surah: {Or do they say he fabricated it? Say: Then bring a surah like it, and call upon whomever you can besides God, if you are truthful}. Likewise in Surat al-Baqarah, which is Medinan, He challenged them with a surah of it, and informed that they would never be able to do that, saying: {And if you do not, and you will never do it, then fear the Fire} the verse [al-Baqarah: 24].

Now, eloquence was among their innate dispositions, and their poetry and their suspended odes reached the utmost limit in this regard. But there came to them from God what no one had the power to match. This is why those among them who believed did so on account of what they recognized of the eloquence of this speech, its sweetness, its stateliness and its charm, its usefulness and its excellence. So they were the most knowledgeable of people concerning it, the most understanding of it, the most following of it, and the most submissive to it. Just as the magicians recognized, by virtue of their knowledge of the arts of magic, that what Moses (peace be upon him) had done could not have issued except from one supported, guided, and sent by God, and that this was not something a human being could achieve except by God's permission. Likewise, Jesus (peace be upon him) was sent in the time of scholars of medicine and treatment of the sick, and he used to heal the blind and the leper, and bring the dead to life by God's permission, and the like of this has no room for treatment or medicine in it. So those among them who recognized this recognized that he was the servant of God and His messenger. This is why it has come in the Sahih, from the Messenger of God ﷺ, that he said: "There was no prophet among the prophets but was given signs of the sort that made people believe. What I was given was revelation which God revealed to me, so I hope that I will be the one with the most followers among them on the Day of Resurrection."

His saying: {Rather, they denied that which they could not encompass in knowledge, and whose interpretation had not yet come to them} means, rather these people denied the Qur'an, and did not understand it nor recognize it. {and whose interpretation had not yet come to them} means, they had not attained what it contains of guidance and the true religion, up until the time of their denial of it, out of ignorance and folly. {Thus did those before them deny} meaning, of the past nations. {So look how was the end of the wrongdoers} means, so look how We destroyed them for their denial of Our messengers, out of wrongdoing and arrogance, disbelief, obstinacy, and ignorance. So beware, you who deny, lest what befell them befall you.

His saying: {And among them are those who believe in it, and among them are those who do not believe in it, and your Lord is most knowing of the corrupters} means, and among these people to whom you were sent, O Muhammad, are those who believe in this Qur'an, and follow you, and benefit from what you were sent with, {and among them are those who do not believe in it}, but rather die upon that and will be resurrected upon it. {and your Lord is most knowing of the corrupters} means, and He is most knowing of who deserves guidance, so He guides him, and who deserves misguidance, so He leads him astray. And He is the Just One who does not wrong, rather He gives each what he deserves. Blessed and Exalted and Holy and Transcendent is He, there is no god but He.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا بَيَانٌ لِإِعْجَازِ الْقُرْآنِ، وَأَنَّهُ لَا يَسْتَطِيعُ الْبَشَرُ أَنْ يَأْتُوا بِمِثْلِهِ، وَلَا بِعَشْرِ سُوَرٍ، وَلَا بِسُورَةٍ مِنْ مِثْلِهِ، لِأَنَّهُ بِفَصَاحَتِهِ وَبَلَاغَتِهِ ووَجازته وحَلاوته، واشتماله على المعاني العزيزة [للعزيرة] النَّافِعَةِ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، لَا يَكُونُ إِلَّا مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ الَّذِي لَا يُشْبِهُهُ شَيْءٌ فِي ذَاتِهِ وَلَا صِفَاتِهِ، وَلَا فِي أَفْعَالِهِ وَأَقْوَالِهِ، فَكَلَامُهُ لَا يُشْبِهُ كَلَامَ الْمَخْلُوقِينَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ هَذَا الْقُرْآنُ أَنْ يُفْتَرَى مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: مِثْلُ هَذَا الْقُرْآنِ لَا يَكُونُ إِلَّا مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ، وَلَا يُشْبِهُ هَذَا كَلَامَ الْبَشَرِ، ﴿وَلَكِنْ تَصْدِيقَ الَّذِي بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْكُتُبِ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةِ، وَمُهَيْمِنًا عَلَيْهَا، وَمُبَيِّنًا لِمَا وَقَعَ فِيهَا مِنَ التَّحْرِيفِ وَالتَّأْوِيلِ وَالتَّبْدِيلِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَتَفْصِيلَ الْكِتَابِ لَا رَيْبَ فِيهِ مِنْ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وَبَيَانُ الأحكام والحلال والحرام، بيانًا شَافِيًا كَافِيًا حَقًّا لَا مِرْيَةَ فِيهِ مِنَ اللَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ، كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ فِي حَدِيثِ الْحَارِثِ الْأَعْوَرِ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ: "فِيهِ خَبَرُ مَا قَبْلَكُمْ، وَنَبَأُ مَا بَعْدَكُمْ، وَفَصْلُ مَا بَيْنَكُمْ"، أَيْ: خَبَر عَمَّا سَلَفَ وَعَمَّا سَيَأْتِي، وَحُكْمٌ فِيمَا بَيْنَ النَّاسِ بِالشَّرْعِ الَّذِي يُحِبُّهُ اللَّهُ وَيَرْضَاهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَمْ يَقُولُونَ افْتَرَاهُ قُلْ فَأْتُوا بِسُورَةٍ مِثْلِهِ وَادْعُوا مَنِ اسْتَطَعْتُمْ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ﴾ أَيْ: إِنِ ادَّعَيْتُمْ وَافْتَرَيْتُمْ وَشَكَكْتُمْ فِي أَنَّ هَذَا مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ، وَقُلْتُمْ كَذِبًا ومَيْنا: "إِنَّ هَذَا مِنْ عِنْدِ مُحَمَّدٍ"، فَمُحَمَّدٌ بَشَرٌ مِثْلُكُمْ، وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِيمَا زَعَمْتُمْ بِهَذَا الْقُرْآنِ، فَأْتُوا أَنْتُمْ بِسُورَةٍ مِثْلِهِ، أَيْ: مِنْ جِنْسِ الْقُرْآنِ، وَاسْتَعِينُوا عَلَى ذَلِكَ بِكُلِّ مَنْ قَدرتم عَلَيْهِ مِنْ إِنْسٍ وَجَانٍّ.

وَهَذَا هُوَ الْمَقَامُ الثَّالِثُ فِي التَّحَدِّي، فَإِنَّهُ تَعَالَى تَحَدَّاهُمْ وَدَعَاهُمْ، إِنْ كَانُوا صَادِقِينَ فِي دَعْوَاهُمْ، أَنَّهُ مِنْ عِنْدِ مُحَمَّدٍ، فَلْتُعَارِضُوهُ بِنَظِيرِ مَا جَاءَ بِهِ وَحْدَهُ وَاسْتَعِينُوا بِمَنْ شِئْتُمْ وَأَخْبَرَ أَنَّهُمْ لَا يَقْدِرُونَ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، وَلَا سَبِيلَ لَهُمْ إِلَيْهِ، فَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ لَئِنِ اجْتَمَعَتِ الإنْسُ وَالْجِنُّ عَلَى أَنْ يَأْتُوا بِمِثْلِ هَذَا الْقُرْآنِ لَا يَأْتُونَ بِمِثْلِهِ وَلَوْ كَانَ بَعْضُهُمْ لِبَعْضٍ ظَهِيرًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٨٨] ، ثُمَّ تَقَاصَرَ مَعَهُمْ إِلَى عَشْرِ سُوَرٍ مِنْهُ، فَقَالَ فِي أَوَّلِ سُورَةِ هُودٍ: ﴿أَمْ يَقُولُونَ افْتَرَاهُ قُلْ فَأْتُوا بِعَشْرِ سُوَرٍ مِثْلِهِ مُفْتَرَيَاتٍ وَادْعُوا مَنِ اسْتَطَعْتُمْ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١٣] ، ثُمَّ تَنَازَلَ إِلَى سُورَةٍ، فَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ السُّورَةِ: ﴿أَمْ يَقُولُونَ افْتَرَاهُ قُلْ فَأْتُوا بِسُورَةٍ مِثْلِهِ وَادْعُوا مَنِ اسْتَطَعْتُمْ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ﴾ وَكَذَا فِي سُورَةِ الْبَقَرَةِ -وَهِيَ مَدَنِيَّةٌ -تَحَدَّاهُمْ بِسُورَةٍ مِنْهُ، وَأَخْبَرَ أَنَّهُمْ لَا يَسْتَطِيعُونَ ذَلِكَ أَبَدًا، فَقَالَ: ﴿فَإِنْ لَمْ تَفْعَلُوا وَلَنْ تَفْعَلُوا فَاتَّقُوا النَّارَ﴾ الْآيَةَ: [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٤] .

هَذَا وَقَدْ كَانَتِ الْفَصَاحَةُ مِنْ سَجَايَاهُمْ، وَأَشْعَارِهِمْ وَمُعَلَّقَاتِهِمْ إِلَيْهَا الْمُنْتَهَى فِي هَذَا الْبَابِ، وَلَكِنْ جَاءَهُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ مَا لَا قِبَلَ لِأَحَدٍ بِهِ، وَلِهَذَا آمَنَ مَنْ آمَنَ مِنْهُمْ بِمَا عَرَفَ مِنْ بَلَاغَةِ هَذَا الْكَلَامِ وَحَلَاوَتِهِ، وَجَزَالَتِهِ وَطَلَاوَتِهِ، وَإِفَادَتِهِ وَبَرَاعَتِهِ، فَكَانُوا أَعْلَمَ النَّاسِ بِهِ، وَأَفْهَمَهُمْ لَهُ، وَأَتْبَعَهُمْ لَهُ وَأَشَدَّهُمْ لَهُ انْقِيَادًا، كَمَا عَرَفَ السَّحَرَةُ، لِعِلْمِهِمْ بِفُنُونِ السِّحْرِ، أَنَّ هَذَا الَّذِي فَعَلَهُ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، لَا يَصْدُرُ إِلَّا عَنْ مُؤيَّد مُسَدد مُرْسَلٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ، وَأَنَّ هَذَا لَا يُسْتَطَاعُ لِبَشَرٍ إِلَّا بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ. وَكَذَلِكَ عِيسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، بُعِث فِي زَمَانِ عُلَمَاءِ الطِّبِّ وَمُعَالَجَةِ الْمَرْضَى، فَكَانَ يُبْرِئُ الْأَكْمَهَ وَالْأَبْرَصَ، وَيُحْيِي الْمَوْتَى بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ، وَمِثْلُ هَذَا لَا مَدْخَلَ لِلْعِلَاجِ وَالدَّوَاءِ فِيهِ، فَعَرَفَ مَنْ عَرَفَ مِنْهُمْ أَنَّهُ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ وَرَسُولُهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "مَا مِنْ نَبِيٍّ مِنَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ إِلَّا وَقَدْ أُوتِيَ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ مَا آمَنَ عَلَى مِثْلِهِ الْبَشَرُ، وَإِنَّمَا كَانَ الَّذِي أُوتِيتُهُ وَحْيًا أَوْحَاهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيَّ، فَأَرْجُو أَنْ أَكُونَ أَكْثَرَهُمْ تَابِعًا .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بَلْ كَذَّبُوا بِمَا لَمْ يُحِيطُوا بِعِلْمِهِ وَلَمَّا يَأْتِهِمْ تَأْوِيلُهُ﴾ يَقُولُ: بَلْ كَذَّبَ هَؤُلَاءِ بِالْقُرْآنِ، وَلَمْ يَفْهَمُوهُ وَلَا عَرَفُوهُ، ﴿وَلَمَّا يَأْتِهِمْ تَأْوِيلُهُ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَمْ يُحصّلوا مَا فِيهِ مِنَ الْهُدَى وَدِينِ الْحَقِّ إِلَى حِينِ تَكْذِيبِهِمْ بِهِ جَهْلًا وَسَفَهًا ﴿كَذَلِكَ كَذَّبَ الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْأُمَمِ السَّالِفَةِ ﴿فَانْظُرْ كَيْفَ كَانَ عَاقِبَةُ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: فَانْظُرْ كَيْفَ أَهْلَكْنَاهُمْ بِتَكْذِيبِهِمْ رُسُلَنَا ظُلْمًا وَعُلُوًّا، وَكُفْرًا وَعِنَادًا وَجَهْلًا فَاحْذَرُوا أَيُّهَا الْمُكَذِّبُونَ أَنْ يُصِيبَكُمْ مَا أَصَابَهُمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يُؤْمِنُ بِهِ وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ لَا يُؤْمِنُ بِهِ وَرَبُّكَ أَعْلَمُ بِالْمُفْسِدِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وَمِنْ هَؤُلَاءِ الَّذِينَ بُعثتَ إِلَيْهِمْ يَا مُحَمَّدُ مَنْ يُؤْمِنُ بِهَذَا الْقُرْآنِ، وَيَتَّبِعُكَ وَيَنْتَفِعُ بِمَا أُرْسِلْتَ بِهِ، ﴿وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ لَا يُؤْمِنُ بِهِ﴾ بَلْ يَمُوتُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ وَيُبْعَثُ عَلَيْهِ، ﴿وَرَبُّكَ أَعْلَمُ بِالْمُفْسِدِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وَهُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِمَنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ الْهِدَايَةَ فَيَهْدِيهِ، وَمَنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ الضَّلَالَةَ فَيُضِلُّهُ، وَهُوَ الْعَادِلُ الَّذِي لَا يَجُورُ، بَلْ يُعْطِي كُلًّا مَا يَسْتَحِقُّهُ، تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى وَتَقَدَّسَ وَتَنَزَّهَ، لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ.

---

## 10:41-44 — verses 41-44 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says to His Prophet ﷺ: if these polytheists deny you, then disown them and their deeds, {so say: to me is my deed and to you is your deed}, just as He says: {Say: O disbelievers * I do not worship what you worship * nor do you worship what I worship * nor am I a worshipper of what you have worshipped * nor do you worship what I worship * to you is your religion and to me is mine} [Surat al-Kafirun]. And Ibrahim the Intimate Friend (peace be upon him) and his followers said to their polytheist people: {Indeed we are disowned of you and of what you worship besides Allah, we disbelieve in you, and enmity and hatred has appeared between us and you forever, until you believe in Allah alone} [al-Mumtahanah: 4].

His saying: {And among them are those who listen to you}, meaning: they hear your good speech, the Mighty Qur'an, and the sound, eloquent hadiths that are beneficial for the hearts, the bodies, and the religion. In this there is a tremendous sufficiency, but that guidance is not up to you nor up to them, for you are not able to make the deaf, that is, the one who cannot hear, hear, and likewise you are not able to guide these people, except that Allah wills it.

{And among them are those who look at you}, meaning: they look at you and at what Allah has given you of gravity, good demeanor, tremendous character, and manifest proof of your prophethood, for those possessed of insight and understanding. But these people look just as others look, and they do not attain from that looking any of the guidance that others attain. Rather the believers look at you with an eye of reverence, while the disbelievers look at you with an eye of contempt. {And when they see you, they take you only in mockery, saying: is this the one whom Allah has sent as a messenger? * He would have almost led us astray from our gods, had we not been steadfast in adherence to them. But they will know, when they see the punishment, who is more astray in path} [al-Furqan: 41, 42].

Then the Exalted informs that He does not wrong anyone in anything, even though He may have guided through him whom He guided from misguidance, given sight through him to one who was blind, opened through him blind eyes, deaf ears, and covered hearts, and led others astray from faith through him. For He is the Ruler who disposes of His dominion as He wills, who is not questioned about what He does while they are questioned, on account of His knowledge, His wisdom, and His justice. It is for this that the Exalted says: {Indeed Allah does not wrong the people in anything, but it is the people themselves who wrong themselves}.

And in the hadith from Abu Dharr, from the Prophet ﷺ, in what he relates from his Lord, Mighty and Majestic: "O My servants, I have forbidden wrongdoing for Myself, and I have made it forbidden among you, so do not wrong one another," until he said at the end of it: "O My servants, they are but your deeds which I record for you, then I repay you for them in full. So whoever finds good, let him praise Allah, and whoever finds other than that, let him blame no one but himself." Narrated by Muslim in full length.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِنَبِيِّهِ ﷺ: وَإِنَّ كَذَبَّكَ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُشْرِكُونَ، فَتَبَرَّأَ مِنْهُمْ وَمِنْ عَمَلِهِمْ، ﴿فَقُلْ لِي عَمَلِي وَلَكُمْ عَمَلُكُمْ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ تعالى: ﴿قُلْ يَاأَيُّهَا الْكَافِرُونَ * لَا أَعْبُدُ مَا تَعْبُدُونَ * وَلا أَنْتُمْ عَابِدُونَ مَا أَعْبُدُ * وَلا أَنَا عَابِدٌ مَا عَبَدْتُمْ * وَلا أَنْتُمْ عَابِدُونَ مَا أَعْبُدُ * لَكُمْ دِينُكُمْ وَلِيَ دِين﴾ [سُورَةُ الْكَافِرُونَ] . وَقَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ الْخَلِيلُ وَأَتْبَاعُهُ لِقَوْمِهِمُ الْمُشْرِكِينَ: ﴿إِنَّا بُرَآءُ مِنْكُمْ وَمِمَّا تَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ كَفَرْنَا بِكُمْ وَبَدَا بَيْنَنَا وَبَيْنَكُمُ الْعَدَاوَةُ وَالْبَغْضَاءُ أَبَدًا حَتَّى تُؤْمِنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ﴾ [الْمُمْتَحَنَةِ: ٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يَسْتَمِعُونَ إِلَيْكَ﴾ أَيْ: يَسْمَعُونَ كَلَامَكَ الْحَسَنَ، وَالْقُرْآنَ الْعَظِيمَ، وَالْأَحَادِيثَ الصَّحِيحَةَ الْفَصِيحَةَ النَّافِعَةَ فِي الْقُلُوبِ وَالْأَبْدَانِ وَالْأَدْيَانِ، وَفِي هَذَا كِفَايَةٌ عَظِيمَةٌ، وَلَكِنْ لَيْسَ ذَلِكَ إِلَيْكَ وَلَا إِلَيْهِمْ، فَإِنَّكَ لَا تَقْدِرُ عَلَى إِسْمَاعِ الْأَصَمِّ -وَهُوَ الْأَطْرَشُ -فَكَذَلِكَ لَا تَقْدِرُ عَلَى هِدَايَةِ هَؤُلَاءِ، إِلَّا أَنْ يَشَاءَ اللَّهُ.

﴿وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يَنْظُرُ إِلَيْكَ﴾ أَيْ: يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَيْكَ وَإِلَى مَا أَعْطَاكَ اللَّهُ مِنَ التُّؤَدَةِ، وَالسَّمْتِ الْحَسَنِ، وَالْخُلُقِ الْعَظِيمِ، وَالدَّلَالَةِ الظَّاهِرَةِ، عَلَى نُبُوءَتِكَ لِأُولِي الْبَصَائِرِ وَالنُّهَى، وَهَؤُلَاءِ يَنْظُرُونَ كما ينظر غَيْرُهُمْ، وَلَا يَحْصُلُ لَهُمْ مِنَ الْهِدَايَةِ شَيْءٌ مِمَّا يَحْصُلُ لِغَيْرِهِمْ، بَلِ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَيْكَ بِعَيْنِ الْوَقَارِ، وَالْكَافِرُونَ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَيْكَ بِعَيْنِ الِاحْتِقَارِ، ﴿وَإِذَا رَأَوْكَ إِنْ يَتَّخِذُونَكَ إِلا هُزُوًا أَهَذَا الَّذِي بَعَثَ اللَّهُ رَسُولا * إِنْ كَادَ لَيُضِلُّنَا عَنْ آلِهَتِنَا لَوْلا أَنْ صَبَرْنَا عَلَيْهَا وَسَوْفَ يَعْلَمُونَ حِينَ يَرَوْنَ الْعَذَابَ مَنْ أَضَلُّ سَبِيلا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ: ٤١، ٤٢] .

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ لَا يَظْلِمُ أَحَدًا شَيْئًا، وَإِنْ كَانَ قَدْ هَدَى بِهِ مِنْ هَدَى [مِنَ الْغَيِّ] وَبَصَّرَ بِهِ مِنَ الْعَمَى، وَفَتَحَ بِهِ أَعْيُنًا عُمْيًا، وَآذَانًا صُمًّا، وَقُلُوبًا غُلْفًا، وَأَضَلَّ بِهِ عَنِ الْإِيمَانِ آخَرِينَ، فَهُوَ الْحَاكِمُ الْمُتَصَرِّفُ فِي مُلْكِهِ بِمَا يَشَاءُ، الَّذِي لَا يُسْأل عَمَّا يَفْعَلُ وَهُمْ يُسْأَلُونَ، لِعِلْمِهِ وَحِكْمَتِهِ وَعَدْلِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَظْلِمُ النَّاسَ شَيْئًا وَلَكِنَّ النَّاسَ أَنْفُسَهُمْ يَظْلِمُونَ﴾ وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ عَنْ أَبِي ذَرٍّ عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، فِيمَا يرويه عنه رَبِّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: "يَا عِبَادِي، إِنِّي حَرَّمْتُ الظُّلْمَ عَلَى نَفْسِي، وَجَعَلْتُهُ بَيْنَكُمْ مُحَرَّمًا فَلَا تَظَالَمُوا -إِلَى أَنْ قَالَ فِي آخِرِهِ: يَا عِبَادِي، إِنَّمَا هِيَ أَعْمَالُكُمْ أُحْصِيهَا لَكُمْ، ثُمَّ أُوَفِّيكُمْ إِيَّاهَا، فَمَنْ وَجَدَ خَيْرًا فَلْيَحْمَدِ اللَّهَ، ومن وجد غير ذلك فلا يَلُومَنَّ إلا نَفْسَهُ". رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ بِطُولِهِ.

---

## 10:45 — verse 45

### Translation

The Exalted says, reminding the people of the establishment of the Hour and their being gathered from their graves to the courtyards of the Resurrection: it is as though, on the day they arrive at it, they had not stayed in this world {except for an hour of the day}, as the Exalted said: {It is as though, on the day they see it, they had not stayed except for an evening or its morning} [al-Nazi'at: 46]. And the Exalted said: {The Day the Trumpet is blown, and We shall gather the sinners on that Day blue-eyed. They will murmur among themselves, "You stayed not except ten [days]." We know best what they say, when the most exemplary of them in conduct will say, "You stayed not except one day"} [Ta Ha: 102-104]. And the Exalted said: {And on the Day the Hour will be established, the sinners will swear they had stayed not but an hour. Thus were they ever deluded. But those who were given knowledge and faith will say, "You have stayed, according to the decree of Allah, until the Day of Resurrection. So this is the Day of Resurrection, but you did not used to know"} [al-Rum: 55, 56].

All of this is evidence that the life of this world will appear brief in comparison to the Hereafter, as He said: {He will say, "How many years did you remain on earth?" They will say, "We remained a day or part of a day; ask those who keep count." He will say, "You stayed not but a little, if only you had known"} [al-Mu'minun: 112-114].

His saying, {They will recognize one another among themselves}, means: the children will recognize the fathers and relatives will recognize one another, just as they did in this world, but each will be preoccupied with himself, {But when the Trumpet is blown, there will be no relationships among them that Day, nor will they ask about one another} [al-Mu'minun: 101]. And the Exalted said: {Nor will any intimate friend ask about his intimate friend, though they will be shown to each other. The criminal will wish that he could be ransomed from the punishment of that Day by his children, and his wife and his brother, and his nearest kindred who shelter him, and whoever is on earth entirely, then it would save him. No!} [al-Ma'arij: 10-15].

His saying, {Those have indeed lost who deny the meeting with Allah, and were not [rightly] guided}, is like His saying: {Woe that Day to the deniers} [al-Mursalat: 15]. This is because they will have lost themselves and their families on the Day of Resurrection: unquestionably, that is the clear loss. This is the tremendous loss, and there is no loss greater than the loss of one who is separated from his loved ones on the Day of anguish and regret.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُذكِّرًا لِلنَّاسِ قِيَامَ السَّاعَةِ وَحَشْرَهُمْ مِنْ أَجْدَاثِهِمْ إِلَى عَرَصات الْقِيَامَةِ: كَأَنَّهُمْ يَوْمَ يُوَافُونَهَا لَمْ يَلْبَثُوا فِي الدُّنْيَا ﴿إِلا سَاعَةً مِنَ النَّهَارِ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿كَأَنَّهُمْ يَوْمَ يَرَوْنَهَا لَمْ يَلْبَثُوا إِلا عَشِيَّةً أَوْ ضُحَاهَا﴾ [النَّازِعَاتِ: ٤٦] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ يُنْفَخُ فِي الصُّورِ وَنَحْشُرُ الْمُجْرِمِينَ يَوْمَئِذٍ زُرْقًا * يَتَخَافَتُونَ بَيْنَهُمْ إِنْ لَبِثْتُمْ إِلا عَشْرًا * نَحْنُ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا يَقُولُونَ إِذْ يَقُولُ أَمْثَلُهُمْ طَرِيقَةً إِنْ لَبِثْتُمْ إِلا يَوْمًا﴾ [طه: ١٠٢ -١٠٤] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَوْمَ تَقُومُ السَّاعَةُ يُقْسِمُ الْمُجْرِمُونَ مَا لَبِثُوا غَيْرَ سَاعَةٍ كَذَلِكَ كَانُوا يُؤْفَكُونَ * وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْعِلْمَ وَالإيمَانَ لَقَدْ لَبِثْتُمْ فِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْبَعْثِ فَهَذَا يَوْمُ الْبَعْثِ وَلَكِنَّكُمْ كُنْتُمْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٥٥، ٥٦] .

وَهَذَا كُلُّهُ دَلِيلٌ عَلَى اسْتِقْصَارِ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿قَالَ كَمْ لَبِثْتُمْ فِي الأرْضِ عَدَدَ سِنِينَ * قَالُوا لَبِثْنَا يَوْمًا أَوْ بَعْضَ يَوْمٍ فَاسْأَلِ الْعَادِّينَ * قَالَ إِنْ لَبِثْتُمْ إِلا قَلِيلا لَوْ أَنَّكُمْ كُنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ١١٢، ١١٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَتَعَارَفُونَ بَيْنَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: يَعْرِفُ الْأَبْنَاءُ الْآبَاءَ والقرابات بعضهم لبعض، كما كانوا في الدُّنْيَا، وَلَكِنْ كُلٌّ مَشْغُولٌ بِنَفْسِهِ ﴿فَإِذَا نُفِخَ فِي الصُّورِ فَلا أَنْسَابَ بَيْنَهُمْ يَوْمَئِذٍ وَلا يَتَسَاءَلُونَ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ١٠١] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا يَسْأَلُ حَمِيمٌ حَمِيمًا * يُبَصَّرُونَهُمْ يَوَدُّ الْمُجْرِمُ لَوْ يَفْتَدِي مِنْ عَذَابِ يَوْمِئِذٍ بِبَنِيهِ وَصَاحِبَتِهِ وَأَخِيهِ * وَفَصِيلَتِهِ الَّتِي تُؤْوِيهِ * وَمَنْ فِي الأرْضِ جَمِيعًا ثُمَّ يُنْجِيهِ * كَلا﴾ [الْمَعَارِجِ: ١٠، ١٥] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قَدْ خَسِرَ الَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوا بِلِقَاءِ اللَّهِ وَمَا كَانُوا مُهْتَدِينَ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيْلٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ لِلْمُكَذِّبِينَ﴾ [الْمُرْسَلَاتِ: ١٥] . لِأَنَّهُمْ خَسِرُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ وَأَهْلِيهِمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، أَلَا ذَلِكَ هُوَ الْخُسْرَانُ الْمُبِينُ. فَهَذِهِ هِيَ الْخَسَارَةُ الْعَظِيمَةُ، وَلَا خَسَارَةَ أَعْظَمُ مِنْ خَسارة مَنْ فُرّق بَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَ أَحِبَّتِهِ يَوْمَ الْحَسْرَةِ وَالنَّدَامَةِ.

---

## 10:46-47 — verses 46-47 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, addressing His Messenger ﷺ: {And whether We show you some of what We promise them} meaning: We take vengeance upon them during your lifetime so that your eye may be gladdened by them, {or We cause you to die, then to Us is their return} that is, their destination and their final course, and Allah is a witness over their deeds after you.

Al-Tabarani said: [chain] ...from Hudhayfah ibn Asid, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "My nation was presented to me last night beside this chamber, its first and its last." A man said: "O Messenger of Allah, those who have been created were presented to you, but how about those who have not yet been created?" He said: "They were shaped for me out of clay, so that indeed I know a man among them better than one of you knows his companion."

It was also narrated from Muhammad ibn Uthman ibn Abi Shaybah, from Uqbah ibn Mukram, from Yunus ibn Bukayr, from Ziyad ibn al-Mundhir, from Abu al-Tufayl, from Hudhayfah ibn Asid, with similar wording.

Concerning His saying: {And for every nation there is a messenger. So when their messenger comes} Mujahid said: this means on the Day of Resurrection.

{It will be judged between them in justice, and they will not be wronged} just as the Almighty said: {And the earth will shine with the light of its Lord, and the record will be placed, and the prophets and the witnesses will be brought, and it will be judged between them in truth, and they will not be wronged} [al-Zumar: 69]. So every nation will be presented before Allah in the presence of its messenger, and the record of its deeds, both good and evil, will be laid out bearing witness against them, and their guardian angels will also be witnesses, nation after nation. This noble nation, though it is the last of the nations in creation, is nevertheless the first of the nations on the Day of Resurrection to have judgment passed between them and rendered for them, as has come in the two Sahihs from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "We are the last, yet the foremost on the Day of Resurrection, the first to be judged before all creation." So his nation attained the palm of precedence only because of the nobility of its Messenger, may the prayers and peace of Allah be upon him always until the Day of Judgment.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخَاطِبًا لِرَسُولِهِ ﷺ: ﴿وَإِمَّا نُرِيَنَّكَ بَعْضَ الَّذِي نَعِدُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: نَنْتَقِمُ مِنْهُمْ فِي حَيَاتِكَ لِتَقَرَّ عينُك مِنْهُمْ، ﴿أَوْ نَتَوَفَّيَنَّكَ فَإِلَيْنَا مَرْجِعُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: مَصِيرُهُمْ ومتقَلَبهم، وَاللَّهُ شَهِيدٌ عَلَى أَفْعَالِهِمْ بَعْدَكَ.

وَقَدْ قَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَحْمَدَ، حَدَّثَنَا عُقْبَةُ بْنُ مَكْرَمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْحَنَفِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا دَاوُدُ بْنُ الْجَارُودِ، عَنْ أَبِي الطُّفَيْلِ عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ بْنِ أَسِيدٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "عُرضت عَلَيَّ أُمَّتِي الْبَارِحَةَ لَدَى هَذِهِ الْحُجْرَةِ، أَوَّلُهَا وَآخِرُهَا. فَقَالَ رَجُلٌ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، عُرِضَ عَلَيْكَ مَنْ خُلِق، فَكَيْفَ مَنْ لَمْ يُخْلَقْ؟ فَقَالَ: "صُوِّروا لِي فِي الطِّينِ، حَتَّى إِنِّي لأعْرَفُ بِالْإِنْسَانِ مِنْهُمْ مِنْ أَحَدِكُمْ بِصَاحِبِهِ". 

وَرَوَاهُ عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ، عَنْ عُقْبَةَ بْنِ مَكْرَمٍ، عَنْ يُونُسَ بْنِ بُكَيْر، عَنْ زِيَادِ بْنِ الْمُنْذِرِ، عَنْ أَبِي الطُّفَيْلِ، عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ بْنِ أَسِيدٍ، بِهِ نَحْوَهُ. 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلِكُلِّ أُمَّةٍ رَسُولٌ فَإِذَا جَاءَ رَسُولُهُمْ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: يَعْنِي يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ.

﴿قُضِيَ بَيْنَهُمْ بِالْقِسْطِ وَهُمْ لَا يُظْلَمُونَ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَشْرَقَتِ الأرْضُ بِنُورِ رَبِّهَا وَوُضِعَ الْكِتَابُ وَجِيءَ بِالنَّبِيِّينَ وَالشُّهَدَاءِ وَقُضِيَ بَيْنَهُمْ بِالْحَقِّ وَهُمْ لَا يُظْلَمُونَ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ: ٦٩] ، فَكُلُّ أُمَّةٍ تُعْرَضُ عَلَى اللَّهِ بِحَضْرَةِ رَسُولِهَا، وكتابُ أَعْمَالِهَا مِنْ خَيْرٍ وَشَرٍّ موضوعٌ شَاهِدٌ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَحَفَظَتُهُمْ مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ شهودٌ أَيْضًا أُمَّةً بَعْدَ أُمَّةٍ. وَهَذِهِ الْأُمَّةُ الشَّرِيفَةُ وَإِنْ كَانَتْ آخِرَ الْأُمَمِ فِي الْخَلْقِ، إِلَّا أَنَّهَا أَوَّلُ الْأُمَمِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يُفْصَلُ بَيْنَهُمْ، وَيُقْضَى لَهُمْ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أنه قال: "نحن الْآخِرُونَ السَّابِقُونَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، الْمَقْضِيُّ لَهُمْ قَبْلَ الْخَلَائِقِ" فَأُمَّتُهُ إِنَّمَا حَازَتْ قَصَب السَّبْقِ لِشَرَفِ رَسُولِهَا، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ [دَائِمًا] إِلَى يَوْمِ الدِّينِ.

---

## 10:48-52 — verses 48-52 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing of the disbelief of these polytheists in their haste for the punishment and their asking about its time before it was appointed, which is of no benefit to them, as the Almighty said: {Those who do not believe in it seek to hasten it, while those who believe are apprehensive of it and know that it is the truth} [al-Shura: 18], meaning: it is bound to occur and will certainly happen, even if they do not know its exact time. For this reason He guided His Messenger ﷺ to their answer, saying: {Say, "I have no power for myself over any harm or benefit except what Allah wills"}, meaning: I say nothing except what He has taught me, and I have no power over anything He has reserved to Himself except that He inform me of it. I am His servant and His messenger to you, and I have told you of the coming of the Hour and that it will occur, but He has not informed me of its time. [However,] {for every nation there is a term}, meaning: for every generation there is an appointed span of life, and when their term expires, {they will not delay it an hour, nor will they advance it}, as the Almighty said: {And Allah will never delay a soul when its term has come} [al-Munafiqun: 11].

Then He informed them that the punishment of Allah would come upon them suddenly, saying: {Say, "Have you considered: if His punishment came upon you by night or by day}, meaning: at night or in the daytime, {what part of it would the criminals seek to hasten? Then, when it has befallen, will you then believe in it?}, meaning: that when the punishment comes to them they will say: {Our Lord, we have seen and heard, so return us that we may do righteous deeds; indeed we are now certain} [al-Sajdah: 12]. And the Almighty said: {But when they saw Our punishment, they said, "We believe in Allah alone, and we disbelieve in what we used to associate with Him." But their belief was of no benefit to them when they saw Our punishment. That is the established way of Allah which has always applied to His servants, and there the disbelievers were lost} [Ghafir: 84-85].

{Then it will be said (6) to those who wronged, "Taste the punishment of eternity"}, meaning: on the Day of Resurrection this will be said to them, as a rebuke and reproach, similar to His saying: {The Day they are thrust into the Fire of Hell with a violent thrust. This is the Fire which you used to deny. Is this magic, or do you not see? Enter it, then bear it patiently or do not bear it patiently, it is the same for you. You are only being repaid for what you used to do} [al-Tur: 13-16].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this
