As for those who say that the pronoun in His saying {and their council} refers back to Pharaoh, on account of the greatness of his kingdom because of those who followed him, or by dropping "the household of" Pharaoh and putting the object of the genitive construction in its place, this is a far-fetched view, even though Ibn Jarir related both of these opinions from some grammarians. Among the things that indicate that there was no believer among the Children of Israel except this one is the saying of the Almighty:

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ لَمْ يُؤْمِنْ بِمُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، مَعَ مَا جَاءَ بِهِ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الْبَيِّنَاتِ وَالْحُجَجِ الْقَاطِعَاتِ وَالْبَرَاهِينِ السَّاطِعَاتِ، إِلَّا قَلِيلٌ مِنْ قَوْمِ فِرْعَوْنَ، مِنَ الذُّرِّيَّةِ -وَهُمُ الشَّبَابُ -عَلَى وَجِلٍ وَخَوْفٍ مِنْهُ وَمِنْ مَلَئه، أَنْ يَرُدُّوهُمْ إِلَى مَا كَانُوا عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْكُفْرِ؛ لِأَنَّ فِرْعَوْنَ كَانَ جَبَّارًا عَنِيدًا مُسْرِفًا فِي التَّمَرُّدِ وَالْعُتُوِّ، وَكَانَتْ لَهُ سَطْوة ومَهابة، تَخَافُ رَعِيَّتُهُ مِنْهُ خَوْفًا شَدِيدًا.

قَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ: عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿فَمَا آمَنَ لِمُوسَى إِلا ذُرِّيَّةٌ مِنْ قَوْمِهِ عَلَى خَوْفٍ مِنْ فِرْعَوْنَ وَمَلَئِهِمْ أَنْ يَفْتِنَهُمْ﴾ قَالَ: فَإِنَّ الذُّرِّيَّةَ الَّتِي آمَنَتْ لِمُوسَى، مِنْ أُنَاسٍ غَيْرِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، مِنْ قَوْمِ فِرْعَوْنَ يَسِيرٌ، مِنْهُمْ: امْرَأَةُ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَمُؤْمِنُ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَخَازِنُ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَامْرَأَةُ خَازِنِهِ.

وَرَوَى عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَمَا آمَنَ لِمُوسَى إِلا ذُرِّيَّةٌ مِنْ قَوْمِهِ﴾ يَقُولُ: بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ.

وَعَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَقَتَادَةُ (الذُّرِّيَّةُ) : الْقَلِيلُ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِلا ذُرِّيَّةٌ مِنْ قَوْمِهِ﴾ يَقُولُ: بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. قَالَ: هُمْ أَوْلَادُ الَّذِينَ أُرْسِلَ إِلَيْهِمْ مُوسَى، مِنْ طُولِ الزَّمَانِ، وَمَاتَ آبَاؤُهُمْ.

وَاخْتَارَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ قَوْلَ مُجَاهِدٍ فِي الذُّرِّيَّةِ: أَنَّهَا مِنْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ لَا مِنْ قَوْمِ فِرْعَوْنَ، لِعُودِ الضَّمِيرُ عَلَى أقرب المذكورين.

وَفِي هَذَا نَظَرٌ؛ لِأَنَّهُ أَرَادَ بِالذُّرِّيَّةِ الْأَحْدَاثَ وَالشَّبَابَ وَأَنَّهُمْ مِنْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، فَالْمَعْرُوفُ أَنَّ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ كُلَّهُمْ آمَنُوا بِمُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَاسْتَبْشَرُوا بِهِ، وَقَدْ كَانُوا يَعْرِفُونَ نَعْتَهُ وَصِفَتَهُ وَالْبِشَارَةَ بِهِ مِنْ كُتُبِهِمُ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةِ، وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى سَيُنْقِذُهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ أَسْرِ فِرْعَوْنَ وَيُظْهِرُهُمْ عَلَيْهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا بَلَغَ هَذَا فِرْعَوْنَ حَذَر كُلَّ الْحَذَرِ فَلَمْ يُجْد عَنْهُ شَيْئًا. وَلَمَّا جَاءَ مُوسَى آذَاهُمْ فِرْعَوْنُ أَشَدَّ الْأَذَى، وَ ﴿قَالُوا أُوذِينَا مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ تَأْتِيَنَا وَمِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جِئْتَنَا قَالَ عَسَى رَبُّكُمْ أَنْ يُهْلِكَ عَدُوَّكُمْ وَيَسْتَخْلِفَكُمْ فِي الأرْضِ فَيَنْظُرَ كَيْفَ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٢٩] . وَإِذَا تَقَرَّرَ هَذَا فَكَيْفَ يَكُونُ الْمُرَادُ إِلَّا ذُرِّيَّةً مِنْ قَوْمِ مُوسَى، وَهُمْ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ؟.

﴿عَلَى خَوْفٍ مِنْ فِرْعَوْنَ وَمَلَئِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: وَأَشْرَافِ قَوْمِهِمْ أَنْ يَفْتِنَهُمْ، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ مَنْ يَخَافُ مِنْهُ أَنْ يَفتِنَ عَنِ الْإِيمَانِ سِوَى قَارُونَ، فَإِنَّهُ كَانَ مِنْ قَوْمِ مُوسَى، فَبَغَى عَلَيْهِمْ؛ لَكِنَّهُ كَانَ طَاوِيًا إِلَى فِرْعَوْنَ، مُتَّصِلًا بِهِ، مُتَعَلِّقًا بِحِبَالِهِ وَمَنْ قَالَ: إِنَّ الضَّمِيرَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَلَئِهِمْ﴾ عَائِدٌ إِلَى فِرْعَوْنَ، وَعِظَمِ الْمُلْكِ مِنْ أَجْلِ اتِّبَاعِهِ أَوْ بِحَذْفِ "آلِ" فِرْعَوْنَ، وَإِقَامَةِ الْمُضَافِ إِلَيْهِ مَقَامَهُ -فَقَدْ أَبْعَدَ، وَإِنْ كَانَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ قَدْ حَكَاهُمَا عَنْ بَعْضِ النُّحَاةِ. وَمِمَّا يَدُلُّ عَلَى أَنَّهُ لَمْ يَكُنْ فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ إِلَّا مُؤْمِنٌ قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى:

---

## 10:84-86 — verses 84-86 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing about Musa, that he said to the Children of Israel: {O my people, if you have believed in Allah, then rely upon Him, if you are submitters (Muslims)} that is, Allah is sufficient for whoever relies upon Him, {Is not Allah sufficient for His servant?} [al-Zumar: 36], {and whoever relies upon Allah, He is sufficient for him} [al-Talaq: 3].

Allah frequently joins worship with reliance (tawakkul), as in His saying: {So worship Him and rely upon Him} [Hud: 123], {Say: He is the Most Merciful, we have believed in Him and upon Him we rely} [al-Mulk: 29], {Lord of the east and the west, there is no god but He, so take Him as a guardian (wakil)} [al-Muzzammil: 9]. Allah the Exalted commanded the believers to say, in every one of their prayers, multiple times: {You alone we worship, and You alone we ask for help} [al-Fatiha: 5].

The Children of Israel complied with this, saying: {Upon Allah we rely. Our Lord, do not make us a trial (fitnah) for the wrongdoing people} that is, do not let them prevail over us and gain dominance over us, lest they suppose that they were only given dominance because they are upon truth and we upon falsehood, and thus be led into error by that. This is what has been related from Abu Mijlaz and Abu al-Duha.

Ibn Abi Najih and others, from one narrator, from Mujahid, said: do not punish us at the hands of the people of Pharaoh, nor with a punishment from Yourself, lest the people of Pharaoh say: if they were upon truth they would not have been punished, nor would we have been given dominance over them, and thereby they would be led into error because of us.

Abd al-Razzaq said: Ibn Uyaynah informed us, from Ibn Najih, from Mujahid: {Our Lord, do not make us a trial for the wrongdoing people}, that is, do not give them dominance over us, lest they put us to trial.

{And save us by Your mercy} that is, deliver us by a mercy and a favor from You, {from the disbelieving people} that is, those who disbelieved in the truth and concealed it, while we have believed in You and relied upon You.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ مُوسَى أَنَّهُ قَالَ لِبَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ: ﴿يَا قَوْمِ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ آمَنْتُمْ بِاللَّهِ فَعَلَيْهِ تَوَكَّلُوا إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُسْلِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ كَافٍ مَنْ تَوَكَّلَ عَلَيْهِ، ﴿أَلَيْسَ اللَّهُ بِكَافٍ عَبْدَهُ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ: ٣٦] ، ﴿وَمَنْ يَتَوَكَّلْ عَلَى اللَّهِ فَهُوَ حَسْبُهُ﴾ [الطَّلَاقِ: ٣] .

وَكَثِيرًا مَا يَقْرِنُ اللَّهُ بَيْنَ الْعِبَادَةِ وَالتَّوَكُّلِ، كَمَا فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَاعْبُدْهُ وَتَوَكَّلْ عَلَيْهِ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١٢٣] ، ﴿قُلْ هُوَ الرَّحْمَنُ آمَنَّا بِهِ وَعَلَيْهِ تَوَكَّلْنَا﴾ [الْمُلْكِ: ٢٩] ، ﴿رَبُّ الْمَشْرِقِ وَالْمَغْرِبِ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا هُوَ فَاتَّخِذْهُ وَكِيلا﴾ [الْمُزَّمِّلِ: ٩] ، وَأَمَرَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَنْ يَقُولُوا فِي كُلِّ صَلَوَاتِهِمْ مَرَّاتٍ مُتَعَدِّدَةً: ﴿إِيَّاكَ نَعْبُدُ وَإِيَّاكَ نَسْتَعِينُ﴾ [الْفَاتِحَةِ: ٥] .

وَقَدِ امْتَثَلَ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ ذَلِكَ، فَقَالُوا: ﴿عَلَى اللَّهِ تَوَكَّلْنَا رَبَّنَا لَا تَجْعَلْنَا فِتْنَةً لِلْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا تُظْفِرْهُمْ بِنَا، وَتُسَلِّطْهُمْ عَلَيْنَا، فَيَظُنُّوا أَنَّهُمْ إِنَّمَا سُلِّطُوا لِأَنَّهُمْ على الحق ونحن على الباطل، فَيُفْتَنُوا بِذَلِكَ. هَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنْ أَبِي مِجْلَز، وأبي الضُّحى.

وقال ابن أبي نَجِيح وغيره وَاحِدٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: لَا تُعَذِّبْنَا بِأَيْدِي قَوْمِ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَلَا بِعَذَابٍ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ، فَيَقُولُ قَوْمُ فِرْعَوْنَ: لَوْ كَانُوا عَلَى حَقٍّ مَا عُذِّبُوا، وَلَا سُلِّطنا عَلَيْهِمْ، فَيُفْتَنُوا بِنَا.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَنْبَأَنَا ابْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ، عَنْ ابْنِ نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿رَبَّنَا لَا تَجْعَلْنَا فِتْنَةً لِلْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ [أَيْ] لَا تُسَلِّطْهُمْ عَلَيْنَا، فَيَفْتِنُونَا.

﴿وَنَجِّنَا بِرَحْمَتِكَ﴾ أَيْ: خَلِّصْنَا بِرَحْمَةٍ مِنْكَ وَإِحْسَانٍ، ﴿مِنَ الْقَوْمِ الْكَافِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا الْحَقَّ وَسَتَرُوهُ، ونحن قد آمنا بك وتوكلنا علي.

---

## 10:87 — verse 87

### Translation

He, exalted is He, mentions the reason for His deliverance of the Children of Israel from Pharaoh and his people, and the manner of their escape from them. This was that God, exalted is He, commanded Moses and his brother Aaron, peace be upon them both, {that you two should settle} meaning that they should take dwellings for their people in Egypt.

The commentators differed concerning the meaning of His saying, exalted is He: {and make your houses a qiblah (direction of prayer)}. Al-Thawri and others said, from Khusayf, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas: {and make your houses a qiblah}, he said: they were commanded to take them as places of prayer (masajid).

Al-Thawri also said, from Ibn Mansur, from Ibrahim: {and make your houses a qiblah}, he said: they were in fear, so they were commanded to pray in their houses.

Mujahid, Abu Malik, al-Rabi ibn Anas, al-Dahhak, Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam, and his father Zayd ibn Aslam said likewise. It seems, and God knows best, that this was because when the trial from Pharaoh and his people intensified against them, and they were constrained, they were commanded to pray abundantly, just as He, exalted is He, said: {O you who believe, seek help through patience and prayer} [al-Baqarah: 156]. And in the hadith: the Messenger of God ﷺ, whenever a matter distressed him, would pray. Abu Dawud transmitted it. It is for this reason that He, exalted is He, said in this verse: {and make your houses a qiblah, and establish prayer, and give glad tidings to the believers}, meaning glad tidings of reward and of imminent aid.

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas, in the exegesis of this verse, he said: the Children of Israel said to Moses, peace be upon him: we are not able to display our prayer openly among the Pharaonic people, so God, exalted is He, permitted them to pray in their houses, and they were commanded to orient their houses toward the qiblah. Mujahid said: {and make your houses a qiblah}, he said: when the Children of Israel feared that Pharaoh would kill them in the communal places of worship, they were commanded to make their houses places of prayer facing the Kaaba, praying in them secretly. Qatadah and al-Dahhak said likewise.

Said ibn Jubayr said: {and make your houses a qiblah} meaning: facing one another.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَذْكُرُ تَعَالَى سَبَبَ إِنْجَائِهِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ مِنْ فِرْعَوْنَ وَقَوْمِهِ، وَكَيْفِيَّةِ خَلَاصِهِمْ مِنْهُمْ وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى أَمَرَ مُوسَى وَأَخَاهُ هَارُونَ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ ﴿أَنْ تَبَوَّءَا﴾ أَيْ: يَتَّخِذَا لِقَوْمِهِمَا بِمِصْرَ بُيُوتًا.

وَاخْتَلَفَ الْمُفَسِّرُونَ فِي مَعْنَى قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَاجْعَلُوا بُيُوتَكُمْ قِبْلَةً﴾ فَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ وَغَيْرُهُ، عَنْ خُصَيْف، عَنْ عِكْرِمة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَاجْعَلُوا بُيُوتَكُمْ قِبْلَةً﴾ قَالَ: أمرُوا أَنْ يَتَّخِذُوهَا مَسَاجِدَ.

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ أَيْضًا، عَنِ ابْنِ مَنْصُورٍ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ: ﴿وَاجْعَلُوا بُيُوتَكُمْ قِبْلَةً﴾ قَالَ: كَانُوا خَائِفِينَ، فَأُمِرُوا أَنْ يُصَلُّوا فِي بُيُوتِهِمْ.

وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَأَبُو مَالِكٍ، وَالرَّبِيعُ بْنُ أَنَسٍ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، وَأَبُوهُ زَيْدُ بْنُ أَسْلَمَ: وَكَأَنَّ هَذَا -وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ -لَمَّا اشْتَدَّ بِهِمُ الْبَلَاءُ مِنْ قبَل فِرْعَوْنَ وَقَوْمِهِ، وَضَيَّقُوا عَلَيْهِمْ، أُمِرُوا بِكَثْرَةِ الصَّلَاةِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا اسْتَعِينُوا بِالصَّبْرِ وَالصَّلاةِ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ١٥٦] . وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِذَا حَزَبَهُ أَمْرٌ صَلَّى. أَخْرَجَهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ. وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿وَاجْعَلُوا بُيُوتَكُمْ قِبْلَةً وَأَقِيمُوا الصَّلاةَ وَبَشِّرِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ أَيْ: بِالثَّوَابِ وَالنَّصْرِ الْقَرِيبِ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، فِي تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ قَالَ: قَالَتْ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ لِمُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: لَا نَسْتَطِيعُ أَنْ نُظْهِرَ صَلَاتَنَا مَعَ الْفَرَاعِنَةِ، فَأَذِنَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لَهُمْ أَنْ يُصَلُّوا فِي بُيُوتِهِمْ، وَأُمِرُوا أَنْ يَجْعَلُوا بُيُوتَهُمْ قِبَلَ الْقِبْلَةِ. وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿وَاجْعَلُوا بُيُوتَكُمْ قِبْلَةً﴾ قَالَ: لَمَّا خَافَ بَنُو إسرائيل من فِرْعَوْنَ أَنْ يُقْتَلُوا فِي الْكَنَائِسِ الْجَامِعَةِ، أُمِرُوا أَنْ يَجْعَلُوا بُيُوتَهُمْ مَسَاجِدَ مُسْتَقْبِلَةً الْكَعْبَةَ، يُصَلُّونَ فِيهَا سِرًّا. وَكَذَا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: ﴿وَاجْعَلُوا بُيُوتَكُمْ قِبْلَةً﴾ أَيْ: يُقَابِلُ بَعْضُهَا بَعْضًا.

---

## 10:88-89 — verses 88-89 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is a report from God, Exalted is He, about what Moses (peace be upon him) invoked against Pharaoh and his chiefs, when they refused to accept the truth and persisted in their misguidance and disbelief, being obstinate and denying, out of injustice, arrogance, pride, and insolence. He said: {Our Lord, You have given Pharaoh and his chiefs adornment}, meaning: from the furnishings and enjoyments of this world, {and wealth}, meaning: abundant and plentiful, {in} this {worldly life. Our Lord, that they may lead astray from Your path}, with the ya read as fatha, meaning: You gave them that while You knew that they would not believe in what You sent me to them with, as a gradual enticement (istidraj) from You for them, just as He said, Exalted is He: {that We may try them therein}.

Others read it: {li-yudillu} with the ya read as damma, meaning: that whoever among Your creatures You will may be tried through what You gave them, so that the one You have led astray might suppose that You gave these people this only out of love for them and concern for them.

{Our Lord, obliterate their wealth}. Ibn Abbas and Mujahid said: meaning, destroy it. Al-Dahhak, Abu al-Aliyah, and al-Rabi ibn Anas said: God turned it into engraved stones resembling the very shape it had been in before.

Qatadah said: it has reached us that their crops were turned into stones.

Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi said: make their sugar into stones.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Qays reported that Muhammad ibn Ka'b recited Surat Yunus before Umar ibn Abd al-Aziz: {And Moses said, Our Lord, You have given Pharaoh and his chiefs} up to His saying: {obliterate their wealth} to the end of it. [Umar said to him: O Abu Hamzah, what is al-tams (obliteration)? He said: All their wealth turned into stones.] Umar ibn Abd al-Aziz then said to a servant of his: bring me a purse. [He brought him a purse] and in it were chickpeas and eggs that had been cut from around a stone.

His saying: {and seal their hearts}. Ibn Abbas said: meaning, set a seal upon them, {so that they do not believe until they see the painful punishment}.

This supplication was made by Moses (peace be upon him) out of anger for God and His religion against Pharaoh and his chiefs, those whom it had become clear to him held no good and from whom nothing beneficial would come, just as Noah (peace be upon him) had supplicated, saying: {My Lord, do not leave upon the earth any dwelling place for the disbelievers. Indeed, if You leave them, they will lead Your servants astray and will not beget except a wicked, disbelieving one} [Nuh: 26, 27]. For this reason God, Exalted is He, answered Moses (peace be upon him) in this supplication of his against them, which his brother Aaron affirmed with "Amen," so He, Exalted is He, said: {Your plea has been answered}.

Abu al-Aliyah, Abu Salih, Ikrimah, Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi, and al-Rabi ibn Anas said: Moses supplicated and Aaron said "Amen," meaning: We have answered you both in what you asked concerning the destruction of the house of Pharaoh.

Some who hold the view that "the affirmation ('Amen') of the one following the imam in prayer upon the recitation of al-Fatihah is given the same standing as reciting it himself" have used this verse as evidence, saying: "for Moses supplicated and Aaron said Amen."

God, Exalted is He, said: {He said, Your plea has been answered, so remain steadfast, both of you, [and do not follow the path of those who do not know]}, meaning: just as your plea has been answered, so remain steadfast in My command, both of you.

Ibn Jurayj reported from Ibn Abbas: {so remain steadfast} means: proceed with My command, and that is steadfastness. Ibn Jurayj said: they say that Pharaoh remained for forty years after this supplication.

Muhammad ibn Ali ibn al-Husayn said: forty days.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا إِخْبَارٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى عَمَّا دَعَا بِهِ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، عَلَى فِرْعَوْنَ وَمَلَئه، لَمَّا أَبَوْا قَبُولَ الْحَقِّ وَاسْتَمَرُّوا عَلَى ضَلَالِهِمْ وَكُفْرِهِمْ مُعَانِدِينَ جَاحِدِينَ، ظُلْمًا وَعُلُوًّا وَتَكَبُّرًا وَعُتُوًّا، قَالَ: ﴿رَبَّنَا إِنَّكَ آتَيْتَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَمَلأهُ زِينَةً﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ أَثَاثِ الدُّنْيَا وَمَتَاعِهَا، ﴿وَأَمْوَالًا﴾ أَيْ: جَزِيلَةً كَثِيرَةً، ﴿فِي﴾ هَذِهِ ﴿الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا رَبَّنَا لِيَضِلُّوا عَنْ سَبِيلِكَ﴾ -بِفَتْحِ الْيَاءِ -أَيْ: أَعْطَيْتَهُمْ ذَلِكَ وَأَنْتَ تَعْلَمُ أَنَّهُمْ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِمَا أَرْسَلْتَنِي بِهِ إِلَيْهِمُ اسْتِدْرَاجًا مِنْكَ لَهُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لِنَفْتِنَهُمْ فِيهِ﴾

وَقَرَأَ آخَرُونَ: ﴿لِيُضِلُّوا﴾ بِضَمِّ الْيَاءِ، أَيْ: لِيَفْتَتِنَ بِمَا أَعْطَيْتَهُمْ مَنْ شِئْتَ مِنْ خَلْقِكَ، لِيَظُنَّ مَنْ أَغْوَيْتَهُ أَنَّكَ إِنَّمَا أَعْطَيْتَ هَؤُلَاءِ هَذَا لِحُبِّكَ إِيَّاهُمْ وَاعْتِنَائِكَ بِهِمْ.

﴿رَبَّنَا اطْمِسْ عَلَى أَمْوَالِهِمْ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ: أَيْ: أَهْلِكْهَا. وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، وَأَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ، وَالرَّبِيعُ بْنُ أَنَسٍ: جَعَلَهَا اللَّهُ حِجَارَةً مَنْقُوشَةً كَهَيْئَةِ مَا كَانَتْ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: بَلَغَنَا أَنَّ زُرُوعَهُمْ تَحَوَّلَتْ حِجَارَةً.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ القُرَظي: اجْعَلْ سُكَّرهم حِجَارَةً.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ أَبِي الْحَارِثِ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ أَبِي بُكَيْر، عَنْ أَبِي مَعْشَر، حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ قَيْسٍ: أَنَّ مُحَمَّدَ بْنَ كَعْبٍ قَرَأَ سُورَةَ يُونُسَ عَلَى عُمَرَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ: ﴿وَقَالَ مُوسَى رَبَّنَا إِنَّكَ آتَيْتَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَمَلأهُ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿اطْمِسْ عَلَى أَمْوَالِهِمْ﴾ إِلَى آخِرِهَا [فَقَالَ لَهُ: عُمَرُ يَا أَبَا حَمْزَةَ أَيُّ شَيْءٍ الطَّمْسُ؟ قَالَ: عَادَتْ أَمْوَالُهُمْ كُلُّهَا حِجَارَةً] فَقَالَ عُمَرُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ لِغُلَامٍ لَهُ: ائْتِنِي بِكِيسٍ. [فَجَاءَهُ بِكِيسٍ] فَإِذَا فِيهِ حِمَّصٌ وَبَيْضٌ، قَدْ قُطِعَ حَوْلَ حِجَارَةٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَاشْدُدْ عَلَى قُلُوبِهِمْ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: أَيِ اطْبَعْ عَلَيْهَا، ﴿فَلا يُؤْمِنُوا حَتَّى يَرَوُا الْعَذَابَ الألِيمَ﴾

وَهَذِهِ الدَّعْوَةُ كَانَتْ مِنْ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، غَضَبًا لِلَّهِ وَلِدِينِهِ عَلَى فِرْعَوْنَ وَمَلَئِهِ، الَّذِينَ تبين له أَنَّهُ لَا خَيْرَ فِيهِمْ، وَلَا يَجِيءُ مِنْهُمْ شَيْءٌ كَمَا دَعَا نُوحٌ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَقَالَ: ﴿رَبِّ لَا تَذَرْ عَلَى الأرْضِ مِنَ الْكَافِرِينَ دَيَّارًا إِنَّكَ إِنْ تَذَرْهُمْ يُضِلُّوا عِبَادَكَ وَلا يَلِدُوا إِلا فَاجِرًا كَفَّارًا﴾ [نُوحٍ: ٢٦، ٢٧] ؛ وَلِهَذَا اسْتَجَابَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لِمُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فِيهِمْ هَذِهِ الدَّعْوَةَ، الَّتِي أمَّنَ عَلَيْهَا أَخُوهُ هَارُونُ، فَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قَدْ أُجِيبَتْ دَعْوَتُكُمَا﴾

قَالَ أَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ، وَأَبُو صَالِحٍ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ الْقُرَظِيُّ، وَالرَّبِيعُ بْنُ أَنَسٍ: دَعَا مُوسَى وأمَّنَ هَارُونُ، أَيْ: قَدْ أَجَبْنَاكُمَا فِيمَا سَأَلْتُمَا مِنْ تَدْمِيرِ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ.

وَقَدْ يَحْتَجُّ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ مَنْ يَقُولُ: "إِنَّ تَأْمِينَ الْمَأْمُومِ عَلَى قِرَاءَةِ الْفَاتِحَةِ يُنزل مَنْزِلَةِ قِرَاءَتِهَا؛ لِأَنَّ مُوسَى دَعَا وَهَارُونَ أَمَّنَ".

وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قَالَ قَدْ أُجِيبَتْ دَعْوَتُكُمَا فَاسْتَقِيمَا [وَلا تَتَّبِعَانِّ سَبِيلَ الَّذِينَ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ] ﴾ أَيْ: كَمَا أُجِيبَتْ دَعْوَتُكُمَا فَاسْتَقِيمَا عَلَى أَمْرِي.

قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿فَاسْتَقِيمَا﴾ فَامْضِيَا لِأَمْرِي، وَهِيَ الِاسْتِقَامَةُ. قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: يَقُولُونَ: إِنَّ فِرْعَوْنَ مَكَثَ بَعْدَ هَذِهِ الدَّعْوَةِ أَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحُسَيْنِ: أَرْبَعِينَ يَوْمًا.

---

## 10:90-92 — verses 90-92 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted is He, relates the manner in which He drowned Pharaoh and his soldiers. For when the Children of Israel left Egypt in the company of Moses (peace be upon him), and they were, as it is said, six hundred thousand fighting men besides the offspring, they had borrowed a great quantity of jewelry from the Copts and had gone out taking it with them. Pharaoh's rage against them intensified, so he sent gatherers into the cities to assemble for him his soldiers from his provinces. He rode after them in tremendous pomp and awesome armies, in accordance with what God, exalted is He, willed to bring about concerning them, and no one possessed of power and authority in the whole of his kingdom held back from him. They caught up with them at the time of sunrise. {And when the two hosts saw one another, the companions of Moses said: We are indeed overtaken} [al-Shu'ara: 61]. That was because, when they reached the shore of the sea and Pharaoh caught up with them, nothing remained except that the two hosts should fight, and the companions of Moses (peace be upon him) pressed him insistently, asking: how is deliverance to be found from the situation we are in? He would say: I have been commanded to proceed this way. {Not at all! Indeed my Lord is with me; He will guide me} [al-Shu'ara: 62]. So when the matter grew constricted, it opened out, for God, exalted is He, commanded him to strike the sea with his staff. He struck it, and the sea split apart, {and each part was like a great mountain} [al-Shu'ara: 63], that is, like a huge mountain, and it became twelve paths, one for each tribe. God commanded the wind, and it dried up its ground: {So strike for them a dry path in the sea, fearing neither being overtaken nor being afraid} [Ta Ha: 77]. The water was pierced between the paths in the manner of lattices, so that each group could see the others, lest they think that they had perished.

The Children of Israel crossed the sea, and when the last of them had come out of it, Pharaoh and his soldiers reached its edge on the other side. He was accompanied by a hundred thousand black horses, not counting the rest of the colors. When he saw that, it terrified him, and he hesitated and shrank back, and he intended to turn back, but it was too late, there was no escape. The decree had taken effect, and the supplication had been answered. Gabriel (peace be upon him) came upon a mare in heat that had recently foaled, and passed by the side of Pharaoh's stallion. It neighed toward her, and Gabriel went forward and plunged into the sea and entered it, and the stallion plunged in after her. Pharaoh no longer had any control over himself, but he put on a brave face before his commanders and said to them: the Children of Israel have no greater right to the sea than we do. So they all plunged in, every last one of them, with Michael behind them in their rear, letting none of them escape without driving him to join the rest.

When they had all settled into it and were completely assembled, and the foremost of them intended to come out of it, God the Omnipotent commanded the sea to close in upon them, and it closed in upon them, and not one of them escaped. The waves began to raise them up and bring them down, and the waves piled up over Pharaoh, and the agonies of death overcame him. And he said, in that state: {I believe that there is no god except He in whom the Children of Israel believe, and I am among those who submit}. So he believed at a time when belief could no longer benefit him. {So when they saw Our punishment, they said: We believe in God alone, and we disbelieve in that which we used to associate with Him. But their belief was of no benefit to them when they saw Our punishment. This is the way of God which has already taken place among His servants, and there the disbelievers were lost} [Ghafir: 84-85].

Thus God, exalted is He, said in reply to Pharaoh when he said what he said: {What, now? When you had disobeyed before}, that is, is this the moment when you say this, when you had disobeyed God before this in what was between you and Him? {and you were among the corrupters}, that is, among those in the land who led people astray. {And We made them leaders calling to the Fire, and on the Day of Resurrection they will not be helped} [al-Qasas: 41].

This account which God, exalted is He, has related about Pharaoh, of what he said in that state of his, is among the secrets of the unseen that God made known to His Messenger. For this reason the Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal, may God have mercy on him, said:

[chain] Sulayman ibn Harb, from Hammad ibn Salama, from Ali ibn Zayd, from Yusuf ibn Mihran, from Ibn Abbas, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said, "When Pharaoh said {I believe that there is no god except He in whom the Children of Israel believe}, Gabriel said to me, 'O Muhammad, if only you had seen me taking a handful of the sea's mud and thrusting it into his mouth, fearing that mercy might reach him.'" Al-Tirmidhi, Ibn Jarir, and Ibn Abi Hatim related it in their tafsirs, from the hadith of Hammad ibn Salama, with this chain, and al-Tirmidhi said: a hasan (sound) hadith.

Abu Dawud al-Tayalisi said: [chain] Shu'ba, from Adi ibn Thabit and Ata ibn al-Sa'ib, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said, "Gabriel said to me: If only you had seen me taking a handful of the sea's mud and thrusting it into Pharaoh's mouth, fearing that mercy might overtake him." Abu Isa al-Tirmidhi also related it, and Ibn Jarir also, by more than one route, from Shu'ba, with this chain, and al-Tirmidhi said: hasan gharib (singular) sahih (authentic).

In a version transmitted by Ibn Jarir, from Muhammad ibn al-Muthanna, from Ghundar, from Shu'ba, from Ata and Adi, from Sa'id, from Ibn Abbas, one of the two narrators raised it to the Prophet ﷺ while it appears the other did not raise it. God knows best.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Sa'id al-Ashajj, from Abu Khalid al-Ahmar, from Umar ibn Abdullah ibn Ya'la al-Thaqafi, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, who said: When God drowned Pharaoh, he pointed with his finger and raised his voice, saying: {I believe that there is no god except He in whom the Children of Israel believe}. He said: Gabriel feared that God's mercy might overtake him before His wrath did, so he began taking the mud with his two wings and striking his face with it, pressing it down upon him.

Ibn Jarir related it likewise, from Sufyan ibn Wakee, from Abu Khalid, with this chain, as mawquf (halted report, i.e. attributed only to the companion, not the Prophet).

It has also been related from the hadith of Abu Hurayra. Ibn Jarir said:

[chain] Ibn Humayd, from Hakkam, from Anbasa, that is, ibn Sa'id, from Kathir ibn Zadhan, from Abu Hazim, from Abu Hurayra, may God be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said, "Gabriel said to me: O Muhammad, if only you had seen me choking him and thrusting mud into his mouth, fearing that God's mercy might overtake him and He would forgive him," meaning Pharaoh.

This Kathir ibn Zadhan: Ibn Ma'in said, I do not know him. Abu Zur'a and Abu Hatim said, unknown. The rest of its narrators are trustworthy.

This hadith has been transmitted in mursal (chain missing a link) form by a group of the early generations: Qatada, Ibrahim al-Taymi, and Maymun ibn Mihran. It has also been related concerning al-Dahhak ibn Qays that he delivered a sermon to the people with this account. God knows best.

Regarding His saying: {So today We shall save you in your body, that you may be a sign for those who come after you}, Ibn Abbas and others among the early generations said: some of the Children of Israel doubted Pharaoh's death, so God, exalted is He, commanded the sea to cast his body ashore, lifeless, wearing his well-known armor, upon a raised piece of ground, that being an elevated place, so that they might confirm his death and destruction. For this reason God, exalted is He, said: {So today We shall save you}, that is, We shall raise you up onto elevated ground, {in your body}. Mujahid said: in your corpse. Al-Hasan said: in a body without a spirit in it. Abdullah ibn Shaddad said: intact and whole, that is, not torn apart, so that they might verify it and recognize him. Abu Sakhr said: in your armor.

None of these statements contradicts the others, as has been mentioned previously. God knows best.

Regarding His saying: {that you may be a sign for those who come after you}, that is, so that it might be a proof for the Children of Israel of your death and destruction, and that God is the One with power, in whose hand is the forelock of every creature, and that nothing can withstand His wrath. For this reason, some of the early generations recited it: "that you may be a sign for the one who created you, and indeed many of the people are heedless of Our signs," that is, they do not take it as admonition nor take heed from it. The destruction of Pharaoh and his court took place on the day of Ashura, as al-Bukhari said:

[chain] Muhammad ibn Bashshar, from Ghundar, from Shu'ba, from Abu Bishr, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, who said: The Prophet ﷺ came to Medina, and the Jews were fasting on the day of Ashura. They said: this is the day on which Moses prevailed over Pharaoh. The Prophet ﷺ said to his companions, "You have a greater right to Moses than they do, so fast it."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَذْكُرُ تَعَالَى كَيْفِيَّةَ إِغْرَاقِهِ فِرْعَوْنَ وَجُنُودَهُ؛ فَإِنَّ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ لَمَّا خَرَجُوا مِنْ مِصْرَ صُحْبَةَ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَهُمْ -فِيمَا قِيلَ -سِتُّمِائَةِ أَلْفِ مُقَاتِلٍ سِوَى الذُّرِّيَّةِ، وَقَدْ كَانُوا اسْتَعَارُوا مِنَ الْقِبْطِ حُلِيّا كَثِيرًا، فَخَرَجُوا بِهِ مَعَهُمْ، فَاشْتَدَّ حَنَق فِرْعَوْنَ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَأَرْسَلَ فِي الْمَدَائِنِ حَاشِرِينَ يَجْمَعُونَ لَهُ جُنُودَهُ مِنْ أَقَالِيمِهِ، فَرَكَبَ وَرَاءَهُمْ فِي أُبَّهَةٍ عَظِيمَةٍ، وَجُيُوشٍ هَائِلَةٍ لِمَا يُرِيدُهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى بِهِمْ، وَلَمْ يَتَخَلَّفْ عَنْهُ أَحَدٌ مِمَّنْ لَهُ دَوْلَةٌ وَسُلْطَانٌ فِي سَائِرِ مَمْلَكَتِهِ، فَلَحِقُوهُمْ وَقْتَ شُرُوقِ الشَّمْسِ، ﴿فَلَمَّا تَرَاءَى الْجَمْعَانِ قَالَ أَصْحَابُ مُوسَى إِنَّا لَمُدْرَكُونَ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ: ٦١] وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهُمْ لَمَّا انْتَهَوْا إِلَى سَاحِلِ الْبَحْرِ، وَأَدْرَكَهُمْ فِرْعَوْنُ، وَلَمْ يَبْقَ إِلَّا أَنْ يَتَقَاتَلَ الْجَمْعَانِ، وَأَلَحَّ أَصْحَابُ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، عَلَيْهِ فِي السُّؤَالِ كَيْفَ الْمَخْلَصُ مِمَّا نَحْنُ فِيهِ؟ فَيَقُولُ: إِنِّي أُمِرْتُ أَنْ أَسْلُكَ هَاهُنَا، ﴿كَلا إِنَّ مَعِيَ رَبِّي سَيَهْدِينِ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ: ٦٢] فَعِنْدَمَا ضَاقَ الْأَمْرُ اتَّسَعَ، فَأَمَرَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى أَنْ يَضْرِبَ الْبَحْرَ بِعَصَاهُ، فَضَرَبَهُ فَانْفَلَقَ الْبَحْرُ، ﴿فَكَانَ كُلُّ فِرْقٍ كَالطَّوْدِ الْعَظِيمِ﴾ [الشعراء: ٦٣] أي: كَالْجَبَلِ الْعَظِيمِ، وَصَارَ اثْنَيْ عَشَرَ طَرِيقًا، لِكُلِّ سِبْطٍ وَاحِدٌ. وَأَمَرَ اللَّهُ الرِّيحَ فنَشَّفت أَرْضَهُ، ﴿فَاضْرِبْ لَهُمْ طَرِيقًا فِي الْبَحْرِ يَبَسًا لَا تَخَافُ دَرَكًا وَلا تَخْشَى﴾ [طه: ٧٧] وَتَخَرَّقَ الْمَاءُ بَيْنَ الطُّرُقِ كَهَيْئَةِ الشَّبَابِيكِ، لِيَرَى كُلُّ قَوْمِ الْآخَرِينَ لِئَلَّا يَظُنُّوا أَنَّهُمْ هَلَكُوا. وَجَازَتْ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ الْبَحْرَ، فَلَمَّا خَرَجَ آخِرُهُمْ مِنْهُ انْتَهَى فِرْعَوْنُ وَجُنُودُهُ إِلَى حَافَّتِهِ مِنَ النَّاحِيَةِ الْأُخْرَى، وَهُوَ فِي مِائَةِ أَلْفِ أَدْهَمَ سِوَى بَقِيَّةِ الْأَلْوَانِ، فَلَمَّا رَأَى ذَلِكَ هَالَهُ وَأَحْجَمَ وَهَابَ وَهَمَّ بِالرُّجُوعِ، وَهَيْهَاتَ وَلَاتَ حِينَ مَنَاصٍ، نَفَذَ الْقَدَرُ، وَاسْتُجِيبَتِ الدَّعْوَةُ. وَجَاءَ جِبْرِيلُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، عَلَى فَرَسٍ -وَدِيقٍ حَائِلٍ -فَمَرَّ إِلَى جَانِبِ حِصَانِ فِرْعَوْنَ فَحَمْحَمَ إِلَيْهَا وَتَقَدَّمَ جِبْرِيلُ فَاقْتَحَمَ الْبَحْرَ وَدَخَلَهُ، فاقْتحم الْحِصَانُ وَرَاءَهُ، وَلَمْ يَبْقَ فِرْعَوْنُ يَمْلِكُ مِنْ نَفْسِهِ شَيْئًا، فَتَجَلَّدَ لِأُمَرَائِهِ، وَقَالَ لَهُمْ: لَيْسَ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ بِأَحَقَّ بِالْبَحْرِ مِنَّا، فَاقْتَحَمُوا كُلُّهُمْ عَنْ آخِرِهِمْ وَمِيكَائِيلُ فِي سَاقَتِهِمْ، لَا يَتْرُكُ أَحَدًا مِنْهُمْ، إِلَّا أَلْحَقَهُ بِهِمْ. فَلَمَّا اسْتَوْسَقُوا فِيهِ وَتَكَامَلُوا، وَهَمَّ أَوَّلُهُمْ بِالْخُرُوجِ مِنْهُ، أَمَرَ اللهُ الْقَدِيرُ البحرَ أَنْ يَرْتَطِمَ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَارْتَطَمَ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَلَمْ يَنْجُ مِنْهُمْ أَحَدٌ، وَجَعَلَتِ الْأَمْوَاجُ تَرْفَعُهُمْ وَتَخْفِضُهُمْ، وَتَرَاكَمَتِ الْأَمْوَاجُ فَوْقَ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَغَشِيَتْهُ سَكَرَاتُ الْمَوْتِ، فَقَالَ وَهُوَ كَذَلِكَ: ﴿آمَنْتُ أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا الَّذِي آمَنَتْ بِهِ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ وَأَنَا مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ﴾ فَآمَنَ حَيْثُ لَا يَنْفَعُهُ الْإِيمَانُ، ﴿فَلَمَّا رَأَوْا بَأْسَنَا قَالُوا آمَنَّا بِاللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ وَكَفَرْنَا بِمَا كُنَّا بِهِ مُشْرِكِينَ فَلَمْ يَكُ يَنْفَعُهُمْ إِيمَانُهُمْ لَمَّا رَأَوْا بَأْسَنَا سُنَّةَ اللَّهِ الَّتِي قَدْ خَلَتْ فِي عِبَادِهِ وَخَسِرَ هُنَالِكَ الْكَافِرُونَ﴾ [غَافِرٍ: ٨٤، ٨٥] .

وَهَكَذَا قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى فِي جَوَابِ فِرْعَوْنَ حِينَ قَالَ مَا قَالَ: ﴿آلآنَ وَقَدْ عَصَيْتَ قَبْلُ﴾ أَيْ: أَهَذَا الْوَقْتُ تَقُولُ، وَقَدْ عَصَيْتَ اللَّهَ قَبْلَ هَذَا فِيمَا بَيْنَكَ وَبَيْنَهُ؟ ﴿وَكُنْتَ مِنَ الْمُفْسِدِينَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الْأَرْضِ الَّذِينَ أَضَلُّوا النَّاسَ، ﴿وَجَعَلْنَاهُمْ أَئِمَّةً يَدْعُونَ إِلَى النَّارِ وَيَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ لَا يُنْصَرُونَ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ: ٤١]

وَهَذَا الَّذِي حَكَى اللَّهُ تَعَالَى عَنْ فِرْعَوْنَ مِنْ قَوْلِهِ هَذَا فِي حَالِهِ ذَاكَ مِنْ أَسْرَارِ الْغَيْبِ الَّتِي أَعْلَمَ اللَّهُ بِهَا رَسُولَهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ حَنْبَلٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ:

حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ حَرْبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدٍ، عَنْ يُوسُفَ بْنِ مهْران، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَمَّا قَالَ فِرْعَوْنُ: ﴿آمَنْتُ أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا الَّذِي آمَنَتْ بِهِ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ﴾ قَالَ: قَالَ لِي جِبْرِيلُ: [يَا مُحَمَّدُ] لَوْ رَأَيْتَنِي وَقَدْ أَخَذْتُ [حَالًا] مِنْ حَالِ الْبَحْرِ، فَدَسَسْتُهُ فِي فِيهِ مَخَافَةَ أن تناله الرحمة" وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ فِي تَفَاسِيرِهِمْ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ حَمَّادِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ، بِهِ وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَدِيثٌ حَسَنٌ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ عَدِيِّ بْنِ ثَابِتٍ وَعَطَاءِ بْنِ السَّائِبِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "قَالَ لِي جِبْرِيلُ: لَوْ رَأَيْتَنِي وَأَنَا آخِذٌ مِنْ حَالِ الْبَحْرِ، فَأَدُسُّهُ فِي فَمِ فِرْعَوْنَ مَخَافَةَ أَنْ تُدْرِكَهُ الرَّحْمَةُ". وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ أَبُو عِيسَى التِّرْمِذِيُّ أَيْضًا، وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَيْضًا، مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ، عَنْ شُعْبَةَ، بِهِ وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ غَرِيبٌ صَحِيحٌ.

وَوَقَعَ فِي رِوَايَةٍ عِنْدَ ابْنِ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ الْمُثَنَّى، عَنْ غُنْدَر، عَنْ شُعْبَةَ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ وعَدِيّ، عَنْ سَعِيدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَفَعَهُ أَحَدُهُمَا -وَكَأَنَّ الْآخَرَ لَمْ يَرْفَعْهُ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ الأشَجّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو خَالِدٍ الْأَحْمَرُ، عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ يَعْلَى الثَّقَفِيِّ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا أَغْرَقَ اللَّهُ فِرْعَوْنَ، أَشَارَ بِأُصْبُعِهِ وَرَفَعَ صَوْتَهُ: ﴿آمَنْتُ أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا الَّذِي آمَنَتْ بِهِ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ﴾ قَالَ: فَخَافَ جِبْرِيلُ أَنْ تَسْبِقَ رَحْمَةُ اللَّهِ فِيهِ غَضَبَهُ، فَجَعَلَ يَأْخُذُ الْحَالَ بِجَنَاحَيْهِ فَيَضْرِبُ بِهِ وَجْهَهُ فَيَرْمُسُهُ.

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ وَكِيع، عَنْ أَبِي خَالِدٍ، بِهِ مَوْقُوفًا 

وَقَدْ رُوِيَ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ أَيْضًا، فَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ:

حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ حُمَيْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا حَكَّام، عَنْ عَنْبَسة -هُوَ ابْنُ سَعِيدٍ -عَنْ كَثِيرِ بْنِ زَاذَانَ، عَنْ أَبِي حَازِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "قَالَ لِي جِبْرِيلُ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، لَوْ رَأَيْتَنِي وَأَنَا أَغُطُّهُ وَأَدُسُّ مِنَ الْحَالِ فِي فِيهِ، مَخَافَةَ أَنْ تُدْرِكَهُ رَحْمَةُ اللَّهِ فَيَغْفِرَ لَهُ" يَعْنِي: فِرْعَوْنَ 

كَثِيرُ بْنُ زَاذَانَ هَذَا قَالَ ابْنُ مَعِين: لَا أَعْرِفُهُ، وَقَالَ أَبُو زُرْعَة وَأَبُو حَاتِمٍ: مَجْهُولٌ، وَبَاقِي رِجَالِهِ ثِقَاتٌ.

وَقَدْ أَرْسَلَ هَذَا الْحَدِيثَ جَمَاعَةٌ مِنَ السَّلَفِ: قَتَادَةُ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمُ التَّيْمِيُّ، وَمَيْمُونُ بْنُ مِهْران. وَنُقِلَ عَنِ الضَّحَّاكِ بْنِ قَيْسٍ: أَنَّهُ خَطَبَ بِهَذَا لِلنَّاسِ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَالْيَوْمَ نُنَجِّيكَ بِبَدَنِكَ لِتَكُونَ لِمَنْ خَلْفَكَ آيَةً﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ وَغَيْرُهُ مِنَ السَّلَفِ: إِنَّ بَعْضَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ شكُّوا فِي مَوْتِ فِرْعَوْنَ، فَأَمَرَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى الْبَحْرَ أَنْ يُلْقِيَهُ بِجَسَدِهِ بِلَا رُوحٍ، وَعَلَيْهِ دِرْعُهُ الْمَعْرُوفَةُ [بِهِ] عَلَى نَجْوَةٍ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ وَهُوَ الْمَكَانُ الْمُرْتَفِعُ، لِيَتَحَقَّقُوا مَوْتَهُ وَهَلَاكَهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَالْيَوْمَ نُنَجِّيكَ﴾ أَيْ: نَرْفَعُكَ عَلَى نَشز مِنَ الْأَرْضِ، ﴿بِبَدَنِك﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: بِجَسَدِكَ. وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ: بِجِسْمٍ لَا رُوحَ فِيهِ. وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ شَدَّادٍ: سَوِيًّا صَحِيحًا، أَيْ: لَمْ يَتَمَزَّقْ لِيَتَحَقَّقُوهُ وَيَعْرِفُوهُ. وَقَالَ أَبُو صَخْرٍ: بِدِرْعِكَ 

وَكُلُّ هَذِهِ الْأَقْوَالِ لَا مُنَافَاةَ بَيْنَهَا، كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لِتَكُونَ لِمَنْ خَلْفَكَ آيَةً﴾ أَيْ: لِتَكُونَ لِبَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ دَلِيلًا عَلَى مَوْتِكَ وَهَلَاكِكَ، وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ هُوَ الْقَادِرُ الَّذِي نَاصِيَةُ كُلِّ دَابَّةٍ بِيَدِهِ، وَأَنَّهُ لَا يَقُومُ لِغَضَبِهِ شَيْءٌ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَرَأَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ: " لِتَكُونَ لِمَنْ خَلَقَكَ آيَةً وَإِنَّ كَثِيرًا مِنَ النَّاسِ عَنْ آيَاتِنَا لَغَافِلُونَ" أَيْ: لَا يَتَّعِظُونَ بِهَا، وَلَا يَعْتَبِرُونَ. وَقَدْ كَانَ [إِهْلَاكُ فِرْعَوْنَ وَمَلَئِهِ] يَوْمَ عَاشُورَاءَ، كَمَا قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ:

حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَشَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنَا غُنْدَر، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي بِشْرٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَدِمَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ المدينَة، وَالْيَهُودُ تَصُومُ يَوْمَ عَاشُورَاءَ فَقَالُوا: هَذَا يَوْمٌ ظَهَرَ فِيهِ مُوسَى عَلَى فِرْعَوْنَ. فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ لِأَصْحَابِهِ: "أَنْتُمْ أَحَقُّ بِمُوسَى مِنْهُمْ، فَصُومُوهُ"

---

## 10:93 — verse 93

### Translation

The Almighty informs us of the religious and worldly favors He bestowed upon the Children of Israel. As for "a dwelling place of truth," it is said that this refers to the lands of Egypt and Syria, in the direction of Jerusalem and its surroundings. For when God Almighty destroyed Pharaoh and his soldiers, the authority of the Mosaic state became established over the entirety of the land of Egypt, as God Almighty said: {And We caused the people who had been oppressed to inherit the eastern parts of the land and the western parts thereof which We had blessed, and the fair word of your Lord was fulfilled for the Children of Israel because of their endurance, and We destroyed what Pharaoh and his people had built and what they had erected} [al-A'raf: 137]. And He said in another verse: {So We expelled them from gardens and springs, and treasures and honorable station, thus it was, and We caused the Children of Israel to inherit them} [al-Shu'ara: 57-59].

But they continued with Moses (peace be upon him), heading toward the land of Jerusalem [which is the land of al-Khalil (Abraham), peace be upon him, so Moses continued with those who were with him, seeking Jerusalem], and there were in it a people of the Amalekites [so the Children of Israel shrank back from fighting the Amalekites], and God Almighty caused them to wander lost in the wilderness for forty years. Aaron died there, then Moses (peace be upon them both) died as well, and after them the people went forth with Joshua son of Nun, and God granted them conquest of Jerusalem, and their authority became established over it until Nebuchadnezzar seized it from them for a period of time. Then it returned to them, then the kings of the Greeks took it, and it remained under their rule for a long period. God sent Jesus son of Mary (peace be upon him) during that period, and the Jews, may God disfigure them, sought the help of the Greek kings against Jesus (peace be upon him), since it was under their rule, and they slandered him before them and whispered to them that this man would corrupt their subjects. So they sent someone to seize him, but God raised him up to Himself, and one of the disciples was made to resemble him by the will and decree of God. So they seized that man and crucified him, believing that it was Jesus himself. {And they did not kill him with certainty; rather, God raised him up to Himself, and God is ever Mighty, Wise} [al-Nisa: 157-158].

Then, about three hundred years after the Messiah (peace be upon him), Constantine, one of the kings of the Greeks, entered into the religion of Christianity. He had been a philosopher before that. He entered the religion of the Christians, it is said, out of dissimulation, and it is said, as a scheme to corrupt it. So the bishops among them laid down for him canons, a legal code, and innovations they invented, and he built for them churches and places of worship, large and small, monastic cells, temples, houses of worship, and hermitages. The religion of Christianity spread in that era and became widely known, despite what it contained of alteration, change, distortion, fabrication, falsehood, and contradiction of the religion of the Messiah. None remained truly upon the religion of the Messiah among them except a few monks, who took for themselves cells in the wilderness, the deserts, and the wastelands.

The hand of the Christians took hold of the kingdom of Syria, the Jazira (Mesopotamia), and the lands of the Byzantines (Rum), and this aforementioned king built the city of Constantinople, and al-Qumama (the Church of the Holy Sepulcher), and Bethlehem, and the churches of the lands of Jerusalem, and the towns of Hawran such as Busra and other towns, with massive and skillfully constructed buildings. They worshipped the cross from that time onward, prayed toward the east, made images in the churches, permitted the eating of pork, and other things they innovated in the branches and foundations of their religion. They devised for it the trivial creed which they call "the Great," and they composed for it canons.

To elaborate on this would take long.

The point is that their hand remained over these lands until the Companions, may God be pleased with them, wrested them away. The conquest of Jerusalem took place at the hands of the Commander of the Faithful, Umar ibn al-Khattab, may God be pleased with him, and praise and grace belong to God.

His saying: {And We provided them with good things} means: lawful provision, of the good, beneficial sustenance deemed wholesome both by natural taste and by revealed law.

His saying: {And they did not differ until knowledge had come to them} means: they did not differ in any of the matters except after knowledge had come to them. That is, they had no excuse to differ, for God had made things clear to them and removed ambiguity from them. It has come in the hadith that the Jews split into seventy-one sects, and the Christians split into seventy-two sects, and this nation will split into seventy-three sects, one of which will be in Paradise and seventy-two in the Fire. It was asked, "Who are they, O Messenger of God?" He said, "Those who follow what I and my Companions are upon."

Al-Hakim related it in his Mustadrak with this wording, and it is found in the Sunan collections and the Musnads. For this reason God Almighty said: {Indeed your Lord will judge between them}, meaning He will decide between them, {on the Day of Resurrection concerning that over which they used to differ}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَمَّا أَنْعَمُ بِهِ عَلَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ مِنَ النِّعَمِ الدِّينِيَّةِ وَالدُّنْيَوِيَّةِ فَ ﴿مُبَوَّأَ صِدْقٍ﴾ قِيلَ: هُوَ بِلَادُ مِصْرَ وَالشَّامِ، مِمَّا يَلِي بَيْتَ الْمَقْدِسِ وَنَوَاحِيهِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى لَمَّا أَهْلَكَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَجُنُودَهُ اسْتَقَرَّتْ يَدُ الدَّوْلَةِ الْمُوسَوِيَّةِ عَلَى بِلَادِ مِصْرَ بِكَمَالِهَا، كَمَا قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَوْرَثْنَا الْقَوْمَ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا يُسْتَضْعَفُونَ مَشَارِقَ الأرْضِ وَمَغَارِبَهَا الَّتِي بَارَكْنَا فِيهَا وَتَمَّتْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ الْحُسْنَى عَلَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ بِمَا صَبَرُوا وَدَمَّرْنَا مَا كَانَ يَصْنَعُ فِرْعَوْنُ وَقَوْمُهُ وَمَا كَانُوا يَعْرِشُونَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٣٧] وَقَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿فَأَخْرَجْنَاهُمْ مِنْ جَنَّاتٍ وَعُيُونٍ وَكُنُوزٍ وَمَقَامٍ كَرِيمٍ كَذَلِكَ وَأَوْرَثْنَاهَا بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ﴾ [الشعراء: ٥٧-٥٩] ولكن اسْتَمَرُّوا مَعَ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، طَالِبِينَ إِلَى بِلَادِ بَيْتِ الْمَقْدِسِ [وَهِيَ بِلَادُ الْخَلِيلِ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ فَاسْتَمَرَّ مُوسَى بِمَنْ مَعَهُ طَالِبًا بَيْتَ الْمَقْدِسِ] وَكَانَ فِيهِ قَوْمٌ مِنَ الْعَمَالِقَةِ، [فَنَكَلَ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ عَنْ قِتَالِ الْعَمَالِقَةِ] فَشَرَّدَهُمُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى فِي التِّيهِ أَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً، وَمَاتَ فِيهِ هَارُونُ، ثُمَّ، مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ، وَخَرَجُوا بَعْدَهُمَا مَعَ يُوشَعَ بْنِ نُونٍ، فَفَتَحَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ بَيْتَ الْمَقْدِسِ، وَاسْتَقَرَّتْ أَيْدِيهِمْ عَلَيْهَا إِلَى أَنْ أَخْذَهَا مِنْهُمْ بُخْتُنَصَّرُ حِينًا مِنَ الدَّهْرِ، ثُمَّ عَادَتْ إِلَيْهِمْ، ثُمَّ أَخَذَهَا مُلُوكُ الْيُونَانِ، وَكَانَتْ تَحْتَ أَحْكَامِهِمْ مُدَّةً طَوِيلَةً، وَبَعَثَ اللَّهُ عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فِي تِلْكَ الْمُدَّةِ، فَاسْتَعَانَتِ الْيَهُودُ -قَبَّحَهُمُ اللَّهُ -عَلَى مُعَادَاةِ عِيسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، بِمُلُوكِ الْيُونَانِ، وَكَانَتْ تَحْتَ أَحْكَامِهِمْ، وَوَشَوْا عِنْدَهُمْ، وَأَوْحَوْا إِلَيْهِمْ أَنَّ هَذَا يُفْسِدُ عَلَيْكُمُ الرَّعَايَا فَبَعَثُوا مَنْ يَقْبِضُ عَلَيْهِ، فَرَفَعَهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ، وشُبّه لَهُمْ بَعْضُ الْحَوَارِيِّينَ بِمَشِيئَةِ اللَّهِ وَقَدَرِهِ فَأَخَذُوهُ فَصَلَبُوهُ، وَاعْتَقَدُوا أَنَّهُ هُوَ، ﴿وَمَا قَتَلُوهُ يَقِينًا بَلْ رَفَعَهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَزِيزًا حَكِيمًا﴾ [النِّسَاءِ: ١٥٧، ١٥٨] ثُمَّ بَعْدَ المسيح، عليه السلام بنحو [من] ثلثمائة سَنَةٍ، دَخَلَ قُسْطَنْطِينُ أَحَدُ مُلُوكِ الْيُونَانِ -فِي دِينِ النَّصْرَانِيَّةِ، وَكَانَ فَيْلَسُوفًا قَبْلَ ذَلِكَ. فَدَخَلَ فِي دِينِ النَّصَارَى قِيلَ: تَقِيَّةً، وَقِيلَ: حِيلَةً لِيُفْسِدَهُ، فَوَضَعَتْ لَهُ الْأَسَاقِفَةُ مِنْهُمْ قَوَانِينَ وَشَرِيعَةً وَبِدَعًا أَحْدَثُوهَا، فَبَنَى لَهُمُ الْكَنَائِسَ والبيَع الْكِبَارَ وَالصِّغَارَ، وَالصَّوَامِعَ وَالْهَيَاكِلَ، وَالْمَعَابِدَ، وَالْقَلَايَاتِ. وَانْتَشَرَ دِينُ النَّصْرَانِيَّةِ فِي ذَلِكَ الزَّمَانِ، وَاشْتَهَرَ عَلَى مَا فِيهِ مِنْ تَبْدِيلٍ وَتَغْيِيرٍ وَتَحْرِيفٍ، وَوَضْعٍ وَكَذِبٍ، وَمُخَالَفَةٍ لِدِينِ الْمَسِيحِ. وَلَمْ يَبْقَ عَلَى دِينِ الْمَسِيحِ عَلَى الْحَقِيقَةِ مِنْهُمْ إِلَّا الْقَلِيلُ مِنَ الرُّهْبَانِ، فَاتَّخَذُوا لَهُمُ الصَّوَامِعَ فِي الْبَرَارِي وَالْمَهَامَّةَ وَالْقِفَارِ، وَاسْتَحْوَذَتْ يدُ النَّصَارَى عَلَى مَمْلَكَةِ الشَّامِ وَالْجَزِيرَةِ وَبِلَادِ الرُّومِ، وَبَنَى هَذَا الْمَلِكُ الْمَذْكُورُ مَدِينَةَ قُسْطَنْطِينِيَّةَ، والقُمَامة، وَبَيْتَ لَحْمٍ، وَكَنَائِسَ [بِلَادِ] بَيْتِ الْمَقْدِسِ، وَمُدُنَ حَوْران كبُصرى وَغَيْرِهَا مِنَ الْبُلْدَانِ بِنَاءَاتٍ هَائِلَةً مَحْكَمَةً، وَعَبَدُوا الصَّلِيبَ مِنْ حِينَئِذٍ، وَصَلَّوْا إِلَى الشَّرْقِ، وَصَوَّرُوا الْكَنَائِسَ، وَأَحَلُّوا لَحْمَ الْخِنْزِيرِ، وَغَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِمَّا أَحْدَثُوهُ مِنَ الْفُرُوعِ فِي دِينِهِمْ وَالْأُصُولِ، وَوَضَعُوا لَهُ الْأَمَانَةَ الْحَقِيرَةَ، الَّتِي يُسَمُّونَهَا الْكَبِيرَةَ، وَصَنَّفُوا لَهُ الْقَوَانِينَ،

وَبَسْطُ هَذَا يَطُولُ.

وَالْغَرَضُ أَنَّ يَدَهُمْ لَمْ تَزَلْ عَلَى هَذِهِ الْبِلَادِ إِلَى أَنِ انْتَزَعَهَا مِنْهُمُ الصَّحَابَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ، وَكَانَ فَتْحُ بَيْتِ الْمَقْدِسِ عَلَى يَدَيْ أَمِيرِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ وَالْمِنَّةُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَرَزَقْنَاهُمْ مِنَ الطَّيِّبَاتِ﴾ أَيْ: الْحَلَالِ، مِنَ الرِّزْقِ الطَّيِّبِ النَّافِعِ الْمُسْتَطَابِ طَبْعًا وَشَرْعًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَمَا اخْتَلَفُوا حَتَّى جَاءَهُمُ الْعِلْمُ﴾ أَيْ: مَا اخْتَلَفُوا فِي شَيْءٍ مِنَ الْمَسَائِلِ إِلَّا مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جَاءَهُمُ الْعِلْمُ، أَيْ: وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُمْ أَنْ يَخْتَلِفُوا، وَقَدْ بَيَّنَ اللَّهُ لَهُمْ وَأَزَالَ عَنْهُمُ اللَّبْسَ. وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: أَنَّ الْيَهُودَ اخْتَلَفُوا عَلَى إِحْدَى وَسَبْعِينَ فِرْقَةً، وَأَنَّ النَّصَارَى اخْتَلَفُوا عَلَى اثْنَتَيْنِ وَسَبْعِينَ فِرْقَةً، وَسَتَفْتَرِقُ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةُ عَلَى ثَلَاثٍ وَسَبْعِينَ فِرْقَةً، مِنْهَا وَاحِدَةٌ فِي الْجَنَّةِ، وَثِنْتَانِ وَسَبْعُونَ فِي النَّارِ. قِيلَ: مَنْ هُمْ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "مَا أَنَا عَلَيْهِ وَأَصْحَابِي".

رَوَاهُ الْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ بِهَذَا اللَّفْظِ، وَهُوَ فِي السُّنَنِ وَالْمَسَانِيدِ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ رَبَّكَ يَقْضِي بَيْنَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: يَفْصِلُ بَيْنَهُمْ ﴿يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فِيمَا كَانُوا فِيهِ يَخْتَلِفُونَ﴾

---

## 10:94-97 — verses 94-97 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Qatadah ibn Di'amah said: it has reached us that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "I do not doubt and I do not ask."

Ibn Abbas, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and al-Hasan al-Basri said likewise. In this there is a firming up of the resolve of the community, and a notification to them that the description of their Prophet ﷺ is to be found in the earlier scriptures that are in the hands of the People of the Book, as He, Exalted is He, said: {Those who follow the Messenger, the unlettered Prophet, whom they find written down with them in the Torah and the Gospel} the verse [al-A'raf: 157]. Yet despite this knowledge, they recognize him from their own scriptures just as they recognize their own sons, they conceal that, distort it, and change it, and they do not believe in him despite the proof having been established against them. It is for this reason that He, Exalted is He, said: {Indeed, those against whom the word of your Lord has been justified will not believe, even if every sign should come to them, until they see the painful punishment}, meaning: they will not believe with a belief that benefits them, rather only at the moment when belief no longer benefits any soul. It is for this reason that when Musa (peace be upon him) prayed against Pharaoh and his chiefs he said: {Our Lord, obliterate their wealth and harden their hearts so that they will not believe until they see the painful punishment} [Yunus: 88], just as He, Exalted is He, said: {And even if We had sent down to them the angels, and the dead had spoken to them, and We had gathered together before them every single thing, they still would not have believed, unless Allah had willed. But most of them are ignorant} [al-An'am: 111]. Then He, Exalted is He, said:

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ بْنُ دِعَامة: بَلَغَنَا أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "لَا أَشُكُّ وَلَا أَسْأَلُ" 

وَكَذَا قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَالْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ، وَهَذَا فِيهِ تَثْبِيتٌ لِلْأُمَّةِ، وَإِعْلَامٌ لَهُمْ أَنَّ صِفَةَ نَبِيِّهِمْ ﷺ مَوْجُودَةٌ فِي الْكُتُبِ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةِ الَّتِي بِأَيْدِي أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿الَّذِينَ يَتَّبِعُونَ الرَّسُولَ النَّبِيَّ الأمِّيَّ الَّذِي يَجِدُونَهُ مَكْتُوبًا عِنْدَهُمْ فِي التَّوْرَاةِ وَالإنْجِيلِ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٥٧] . ثُمَّ مَعَ هَذَا الْعِلْمِ يَعْرِفُونَهُ مِنْ كُتُبِهِمْ كَمَا يَعْرِفُونَ أَبْنَاءَهُمْ، يَلْبَسُونَ ذَلِكَ وَيُحَرِّفُونَهُ وَيُبَدِّلُونَهُ، وَلَا يُؤَمِّنُونَ بِهِ مَعَ قِيَامِ الْحُجَّةِ عَلَيْهِمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ حَقَّتْ عَلَيْهِمْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ وَلَوْ جَاءَتْهُمْ كُلُّ آيَةٍ حَتَّى يَرَوُا الْعَذَابَ الألِيمَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ إِيمَانًا يَنْفَعُهُمْ، بَلْ حِينَ لَا يَنْفَعُ نَفْسًا إِيمَانُهَا؛ وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا دَعَا مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، عَلَى فِرْعَوْنَ وَمَلَئِهِ قَالَ: ﴿رَبَّنَا اطْمِسْ عَلَى أَمْوَالِهِمْ وَاشْدُدْ عَلَى قُلُوبِهِمْ فَلا يُؤْمِنُوا حَتَّى يَرَوُا الْعَذَابَ الألِيمَ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٨٨] ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ أَنَّنَا نزلْنَا إِلَيْهِمُ الْمَلائِكَةَ وَكَلَّمَهُمُ الْمَوْتَى وَحَشَرْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ قُبُلا مَا كَانُوا لِيُؤْمِنُوا إِلا أَنْ يَشَاءَ اللَّهُ وَلَكِنَّ أَكْثَرَهُمْ يَجْهَلُونَ﴾ [الأنعام: ١١١] ثم قال تعالى:

---

## 10:98 — verse 98

### Translation

The Exalted says: was there not any town among the peoples of old, to whom We sent messengers, that believed in its entirety? Rather, We sent no messenger before you, O Muhammad, except that his people, or most of them, disbelieved him, as the Exalted said: {Alas for the servants, no messenger comes to them but they mock him} [Ya-Sin: 30], {Likewise, no messenger came to those before them but they said, a sorcerer or a madman} [al-Dhariyat: 52], {And thus We sent no warner before you into a town except that its affluent ones said, indeed we found our fathers upon a way, and indeed we are following in their footsteps} [al-Zukhruf: 23]. And in the sound hadith: "The prophets were presented to me, and one prophet would pass with a huge crowd of people with him, and another prophet with a single man with him, and another prophet with two men with him, and another prophet with no one at all with him," then he mentioned the great number of the followers of Musa (peace be upon him), then he mentioned the great number of his own nation, may the prayers and peace of Allah be upon him, a number so vast that it filled both horizons, east and west.

The point is that no town was found that believed in its entirety in its prophet among the towns of old, except the people of Yunus, who were the people of Nineveh. And their belief came only out of fear of the arrival of the punishment which their messenger had warned them about, after they had witnessed its signs and their messenger had departed from among them. At that point they cried out to Allah, sought His aid, humbled themselves before Him, submitted, and brought out their children, their beasts of burden, and their livestock, and asked Allah the Exalted to lift from them the punishment their prophet had warned them of. Then Allah had mercy on them, removed the punishment from them, and they were granted respite, as the Exalted said: {Except the people of Yunus, when they believed, We removed from them the punishment of disgrace in the life of this world, and We gave them enjoyment for a time} .

The commentators differed as to whether the punishment of the Hereafter was removed from them along with that of this world, or whether it was removed from them only in this world. There are two opinions on this. The first is that this removal applied only to the life of this world, as is restricted in this verse. The second opinion is that it applied to both, based on the saying of the Exalted: {And We sent him to a hundred thousand or more, and they believed, so We gave them enjoyment for a time} [al-Saffat: 147, 148], where belief is attributed to them absolutely, and belief is a deliverer from the punishment of the Hereafter. This is the apparent meaning, and Allah knows best.

Qatada said regarding the interpretation of this verse: no town that disbelieved and then believed when the punishment came upon it was ever spared, except the people of Yunus. When they lost their prophet and thought that the punishment had drawn near to them, Allah cast repentance into their hearts. They wore sackcloth, separated every animal from its young, and then cried out to Allah for forty nights. When Allah recognized in them the sincerity of their hearts, their repentance, and their remorse for what had passed from them, Allah removed the punishment from them after it had already descended close upon them. Qatada said, and mentioned that the people of Yunus were in Nineveh, in the land of Mosul.

And likewise it has been narrated from Ibn Mas'ud, Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and more than one of the salaf (early generations). Ibn Mas'ud used to recite it: "Was there not any town that believed."

Abu Imran reported from Abu al-Jald, who said: when the punishment descended upon them, it began circling over their heads like pieces of dark night. So they went to a man among their scholars and said, "Teach us a supplication we may call upon, perhaps Allah will remove the punishment from us." He said, "Say: O Ever-Living, when there is no living one, O Reviver of the dead, there is no god but You." He said, and the punishment was then removed from them.

The complete story will come in detail in Surat al-Saffat, if Allah wills.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: فَهَلَّا كَانَتْ قَرْيَةٌ آمَنَتْ بِكَمَالِهَا مِنَ الْأُمَمِ السَّالِفَةِ الَّذِينَ بَعَثْنَا إِلَيْهِمُ الرُّسُلَ، بَلْ مَا أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِكَ يَا مُحَمَّدُ مِنْ رَسُولٍ إِلَّا كَذَّبَهُ قَوْمُهُ، أَوْ أَكْثَرُهُمْ كما قال تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا حَسْرَةً عَلَى الْعِبَادِ مَا يَأْتِيهِمْ مِنْ رَسُولٍ إِلا كَانُوا بِهِ يَسْتَهْزِئُونَ﴾ [يس: ٣٠] ، ﴿كَذَلِكَ مَا أَتَى الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ مِنْ رَسُولٍ إِلا قَالُوا سَاحِرٌ أَوْ مَجْنُونٌ﴾ [الذَّارِيَاتِ:٥٢] ، ﴿وَكَذَلِكَ مَا أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِكَ فِي قَرْيَةٍ مِنْ نَذِيرٍ إِلا قَالَ مُتْرَفُوهَا إِنَّا وَجَدْنَا آبَاءَنَا عَلَى أُمَّةٍ وَإِنَّا عَلَى آثَارِهِمْ مُقْتَدُونَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ:٢٣] وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الصَّحِيحِ: "عُرِضَ عَلَيَّ الْأَنْبِيَاءُ، فَجَعَلَ النَّبِيُّ يَمُرُّ وَمَعَهُ الْفِئَامُ مِنَ النَّاسِ، وَالنَّبِيُّ مَعَهُ الرَّجُلُ وَالنَّبِيُّ مَعَهُ الرَّجُلَانِ، وَالنَّبِيُّ لَيْسَ مَعَهُ أَحَدٌ" ثُمَّ ذَكَرَ كَثْرَةَ أَتْبَاعِ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، ثُمَّ ذَكَرَ كَثْرَةَ أُمَّتِهِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، كَثْرَةً سَدَّتِ الْخَافِقَيْنِ الشَّرْقِيَّ وَالْغَرْبِيَّ.

وَالْغَرَضُ أَنَّهُ لَمْ تُوجَدْ قَرْيَةٌ آمَنَتْ بِكَمَالِهَا بِنَبِيِّهِمْ مِمَّنْ سَلَفَ مِنَ الْقُرَى، إِلَّا قَوْمَ يُونُسَ، وَهُمْ أَهْلُ نِينَوى، وَمَا كَانَ إِيمَانُهُمْ إِلَّا خَوْفًا مِنْ وُصُولِ الْعَذَابِ الَّذِي أَنْذَرَهُمْ بِهِ رَسُولُهُمْ، بَعْدَ مَا عَايَنُوا أَسْبَابَهُ، وَخَرَجَ رَسُولُهُمْ مِنْ بَيْنِ أَظْهُرِهِمْ، فَعِنْدَهَا جَأَرُوا إِلَى اللَّهِ وَاسْتَغَاثُوا بِهِ، وَتَضَرَّعُوا لَدَيْهِ. وَاسْتَكَانُوا وَأَحْضَرُوا أَطْفَالَهُمْ وَدَوَابَّهُمْ وَمَوَاشِيَهُمْ، وَسَأَلُوا اللَّهَ تَعَالَى أَنْ يَرْفَعَ عَنْهُمُ الْعَذَابَ الَّذِي أَنْذَرَهُمْ بِهِ نَبِيُّهُمْ. فَعِنْدَهَا رَحِمَهُمُ اللَّهُ، وَكَشَفَ عَنْهُمُ الْعَذَابَ وَأُخِّرُوا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِلا قَوْمَ يُونُسَ لَمَّا آمَنُوا كَشَفْنَا عَنْهُمْ عَذَابَ الْخِزْيِ فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَمَتَّعْنَاهُمْ إِلَى حِينٍ﴾ .

وَاخْتَلَفَ الْمُفَسِّرُونَ: هَلْ كُشف عَنْهُمُ الْعَذَابُ الْأُخْرَوِيُّ مَعَ الدُّنْيَوِيِّ؟ أَوْ إِنَّمَا كُشِفَ عَنْهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا فَقَطْ؟ عَلَى قَوْلَيْنِ، أَحَدُهُمَا: إِنَّمَا كَانَ ذَلِكَ فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا، كَمَا هُوَ مُقَيَّدٌ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ. وَالْقَوْلُ الثَّانِي فِيهِمَا لِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَرْسَلْنَاهُ إِلَى مِائَةِ أَلْفٍ أَوْ يَزِيدُونَ فَآمَنُوا فَمَتَّعْنَاهُمْ إِلَى حِينٍ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ: ١٤٧، ١٤٨] فَأَطْلَقَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْإِيمَانَ، وَالْإِيمَانُ مُنْقِذٌ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ الْأُخْرَوِيِّ، وَهَذَا هُوَ الظَّاهِرُ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: لَمْ يَنْفَعْ قَرْيَةً كَفَرَتْ ثُمَّ آمَنَتْ حِينَ حَضَرَهَا الْعَذَابُ، فَتُرِكَتْ، إِلَّا قَوْمَ يُونُسَ، لَمَّا فَقَدُوا نَبِيَّهُمْ وَظَنُّوا أَنَّ الْعَذَابَ قَدْ دَنَا مِنْهُمْ، قَذَفَ اللَّهُ فِي قُلُوبِهِمُ التَّوْبَةَ، وَلَبِسُوا الْمُسُوحَ، وفَرّقوا بَيْنَ كُلِّ بَهِيمَةٍ وَوَلَدِهَا ثُمَّ عَجّوا إِلَى اللَّهِ أَرْبَعِينَ لَيْلَةً. فَلَمَّا عَرَفَ اللَّهُ مِنْهُمُ الصِّدْقَ مِنْ قُلُوبِهِمْ، وَالتَّوْبَةَ وَالنَّدَامَةَ عَلَى مَا مَضَى مِنْهُمْ كَشَفَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمُ الْعَذَابَ بَعْدَ أَنْ تَدَلَّى عَلَيْهِمْ -قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: وَذَكَرَ أَنَّ قَوْمَ يُونُسَ كَانُوا بِنِينَوَى أَرْضِ الْمَوْصِلِ.

وَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، وَغَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ، وَكَانَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ يَقْرَؤُهَا: "فَهَلا كَانَتْ قَرْيَةٌ آمَنَتْ".

وَقَالَ أَبُو عِمْرَانَ، عَنْ أَبِي الجَلْد قَالَ: لَمَّا نَزَلَ بِهِمُ الْعَذَابُ، جَعَلَ يَدُورُ عَلَى رُءُوسِهِمْ كَقِطَعِ اللَّيْلِ الْمُظْلِمِ، فَمَشَوْا إِلَى رَجُلٍ مِنْ عُلَمَائِهِمْ فَقَالُوا: عَلِّمْنَا دُعَاءً نَدْعُوا بِهِ، لَعَلَّ اللَّهَ يَكْشِفُ عَنَّا الْعَذَابَ، فَقَالَ: قُولُوا: يَا حَيُّ حِينَ لَا حَيَّ، يَا مُحْيِي الْمَوْتَى لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا أَنْتَ. قَالَ: فَكَشَفَ عَنْهُمُ الْعَذَابَ.

وَتَمَامُ الْقِصَّةِ سَيَأْتِي مُفَصَّلًا فِي سُورَةِ الصَّافَّاتِ إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ.

---

## 10:99-100 — verses 99-100 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted is He, says: {And had your Lord willed} O Muhammad, He would have permitted all the people of the earth, every one of them, to believe in what you brought to them, and they would all have believed. But He has wisdom in whatever He does, exalted is He, just as He, exalted is He, said: {And had your Lord willed, He would have made mankind one community, but they will not cease to differ, except whom your Lord has given mercy, and for that He created them. And the word of your Lord has been fulfilled: I will surely fill Hell with the jinn and mankind together} [Hud: 118, 119]. And He, exalted is He, said: {Have those who believed not yet despaired that had Allah willed, He would have guided all mankind?} [al-Ra'd: 31].

For this reason He, exalted is He, said: {Would you then compel the people}, meaning: force them and drive them, {until they become believers}, meaning: that is not for you to do, nor is it your responsibility, rather it belongs to Allah. {He sends astray whom He wills and guides whom He wills, so do not let your soul be consumed in grief over them} [Fatir: 8]. {Their guidance is not upon you, but Allah guides whom He wills} [al-Baqarah: 272]. {Perhaps you would destroy yourself with grief that they are not believers} [al-Shu'ara: 3]. {Indeed you do not guide whom you love} [al-Qasas: 56]. {Upon you is only the conveyance of the message, and upon Us is the reckoning} [al-Ra'd: 40]. {So remind, you are only a reminder. You are not over them a controller} [al-Ghashiyah: 21, 22], and other verses besides these that indicate that Allah, exalted is He, is the one who does what He wills, who guides whom He wills, and leads astray whom He wills, by virtue of His knowledge, His wisdom, and His justice.

For this reason He said: {And it is not for any soul to believe except by the permission of Allah, and He places defilement}, which is corruption and misguidance, {upon those who do not use reason}, meaning: the proofs of Allah and His evidences. And He is just in all of that, in guiding whom He guides and leading astray whom He leads astray.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ شَاءَ رَبُّكَ﴾ -يَا مُحَمَّدُ -لَأَذِنَ لِأَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ كُلِّهِمْ فِي الْإِيمَانِ بِمَا جِئْتَهُمْ بِهِ، فَآمَنُوا كُلُّهُمْ، وَلَكِنْ لَهُ حِكْمَةٌ فِيمَا يَفْعَلُهُ تَعَالَى كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ شَاءَ رَبُّكَ لَجَعَلَ النَّاسَ أُمَّةً وَاحِدَةً وَلا يَزَالُونَ مُخْتَلِفِينَ إِلا مَنْ رَحِمَ رَبُّكَ وَلِذَلِكَ خَلَقَهُمْ وَتَمَّتْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ لأمْلأنَّ جَهَنَّمَ مِنَ الْجِنَّةِ وَالنَّاسِ أَجْمَعِينَ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١١٨، ١١٩] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَفَلَمْ يَيْأَسِ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَنْ لَوْ يَشَاءُ اللَّهُ لَهَدَى النَّاسَ جَمِيعًا﴾ [الرَّعْدِ: ٣١] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَفَأَنْتَ تُكْرِهُ النَّاسَ﴾ أَيْ: تُلْزِمُهُمْ وَتُلْجِئُهُمْ ﴿حَتَّى يَكُونُوا مُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسَ ذَلِكَ عَلَيْكَ وَلَا إِلَيْكَ، بَلْ [إِلَى] اللَّهِ ﴿يُضِلُّ مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ فَلا تَذْهَبْ نَفْسُكَ عَلَيْهِمْ حَسَرَاتٍ﴾ [فَاطِرٍ: ٨] ، ﴿لَيْسَ عَلَيْكَ هُدَاهُمْ وَلَكِنَّ اللَّهَ يَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٧٢] ، ﴿لَعَلَّكَ بَاخِعٌ نَفْسَكَ أَلا يَكُونُوا مُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ: ٣] ، ﴿إِنَّكَ لَا تَهْدِي مَنْ أَحْبَبْتَ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ:٥٦] ، ﴿فَإِنَّمَا عَلَيْكَ الْبَلاغُ وَعَلَيْنَا الْحِسَابُ﴾ [الرَّعْدِ: ٤٠] ، ﴿فَذَكِّرْ إِنَّمَا أَنْتَ مُذَكِّرٌ لَسْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ بِمُصيْطِرٍ﴾ [الْغَاشِيَةِ: ٢١، ٢٢] إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الدَّالَّةِ عَلَى أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى هُوَ الْفَعَّالُ لِمَا يُرِيدُ، الْهَادِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ، الْمُضِلُّ لِمَنْ يَشَاءُ، لِعِلْمِهِ وَحِكْمَتِهِ وَعَدْلِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ لِنَفْسٍ أَنْ تُؤْمِنَ إِلا بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ وَيَجْعَلُ الرِّجْسَ﴾ وَهُوَ الْخَبَالُ وَالضَّلَالُ، ﴿عَلَى الَّذِينَ لَا يَعْقِلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: حججَ اللَّهِ وَأَدِلَّتَهُ، وَهُوَ الْعَادِلُ فِي كُلِّ ذَلِكَ، فِي هِدَايَةِ مَنْ هَدَى، وَإِضْلَالِ مَنْ ضَلَّ.

---

## 10:101-103 — verses 101-103 (shared commentary)

### Translation

God Most High guides His servants to reflect upon His signs of favor and upon what He created in the heavens and the earth of dazzling proofs for people of understanding: the luminous stars in the heavens, both the fixed ones and the moving ones, the sun and the moon, the night and the day and their alternation, and the entering of each into the other, so that this one grows long while that one grows short, then this one grows short while that one grows long; the height of the sky and its vastness, its beauty and its adornment; and what God sends down from it of rain, by which He gives life to the earth after its death, and brings forth from it the various kinds of fruits, crops, and blossoms, and the different types of plants; and what He has scattered upon it of creatures differing in form, color, and benefit; and what is upon it of mountains, plains, deserts, inhabited lands, and ruins. And what is in the sea of wonders and waves, which is nonetheless made subservient and tamed for those who travel upon it, carrying their ships and moving them gently by the subjugation of the All-Powerful for it. There is no god but He, and no lord besides Him.

His saying, {And of what benefit are the signs and the warnings to a people who do not believe?} means: what benefit are the heavenly and earthly signs, and the messengers with their signs, proofs, and demonstrations indicating their truthfulness, to a people who do not believe? As He said: {Indeed, those against whom your Lord's word has been justified will not believe, even if every sign came to them, until they see the painful punishment} [Yunus: 96, 69].

His saying, {So do they wait for anything except the like of the days of those who passed away before them?} means: do these deniers of you, O Muhammad, wait for anything of retribution and punishment except the like of the days of God that befell those who passed away before them among the nations that denied their messengers? {Say: Then wait; indeed I am with you among those who wait. Then We save Our messengers and those who believed} meaning, and We destroy those who denied the messengers. {Thus it is a duty upon Us to save the believers}, meaning, a truth and a duty that God Most High imposed upon Himself, exalted be He, just as He said: {He has decreed upon Himself mercy} [al-An'am: 12]. As has come in the two Sahihs, from the Messenger of God ﷺ, that he said: "Indeed God wrote a book, and it is with Him above the Throne: My mercy has preceded My wrath."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يرشدُ تَعَالَى عِبَادَهُ إِلَى التَّفَكُّرِ فِي آلَائِهِ وما خلق في السموات وَالْأَرْضِ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الْبَاهِرَةِ لِذَوِي الْأَلْبَابِ، مِمَّا في السموات مِنْ كَوَاكِبٍ نَيِّرَاتٍ، ثَوَابِتٍ وَسَيَّارَاتٍ، وَالشَّمْسِ وَالْقَمَرِ، وَاللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ، وَاخْتِلَافِهِمَا، وَإِيلَاجِ أَحَدِهِمَا فِي الْآخَرِ، حَتَّى يَطُولَ هَذَا وَيَقْصُرَ هَذَا، ثُمَّ يَقْصُرَ هَذَا وَيَطُولَ هَذَا، وَارْتِفَاعِ السَّمَاءِ وَاتِّسَاعِهَا، وَحُسْنِهَا وَزِينَتِهَا، وَمَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ مِنْهَا مِنْ مَطَرٍ فَأَحْيَا بِهِ الْأَرْضَ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهَا، وَأَخْرَجَ فِيهَا مِنْ أَفَانِينِ الثِّمَارِ وَالزُّرُوعِ وَالْأَزَاهِيرِ، وَصُنُوفِ النَّبَاتِ، وَمَا ذَرَأَ فِيهَا مِنْ دَوَابٍّ مُخْتَلِفَةِ الْأَشْكَالِ وَالْأَلْوَانِ وَالْمَنَافِعِ، وَمَا فِيهَا مِنْ جِبَالٍ وَسُهُولٍ وَقِفَارٍ وَعِمْرَانٍ وَخَرَابٍ. وَمَا فِي الْبَحْرِ مِنَ الْعَجَائِبِ وَالْأَمْوَاجِ، وَهُوَ مَعَ هَذَا [مُسَخَّرٌ] مُذَلَّلٌ لِلسَّالِكِينَ، يَحْمِلُ سُفُنَهُمْ، وَيَجْرِي بِهَا بِرِفْقٍ بِتَسْخِيرِ الْقَدِيرِ لَهُ، لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ، وَلَا رَبَّ سِوَاهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا تُغْنِي الآيَاتُ وَالنُّذُرُ عَنْ قَوْمٍ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَأَيُّ شَيْءٍ تُجدي الْآيَاتُ السَّمَاوِيَّةُ وَالْأَرْضِيَّةُ، وَالرُّسُلُ بِآيَاتِهَا وَحُجَجِهَا وَبَرَاهِينِهَا الدَّالَّةِ عَلَى صِدْقِهَا، عَنْ قَوْمٍ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ حَقَّتْ عَلَيْهِمْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ وَلَوْ جَاءَتْهُمْ كُلُّ آيَةٍ حَتَّى يَرَوُا الْعَذَابَ الألِيمَ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٩٦، ٦٩] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَهَلْ يَنْتَظِرُونَ إِلا مِثْلَ أَيَّامِ الَّذِينَ خَلَوْا مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: فَهَلْ يَنْتَظِرُ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُكَذِّبُونَ لَكَ يَا مُحَمَّدُ مِنَ النِّقْمَةِ وَالْعَذَابِ إِلَّا مِثْلَ أَيَّامِ اللَّهِ فِي الَّذِينَ خَلَوْا مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ مِنَ الْأُمَمِ الْمُكَذِّبَةِ لِرُسُلِهِمْ، ﴿قُلْ فَانْتَظِرُوا إِنِّي مَعَكُمْ مِنَ الْمُنْتَظِرِينَ ثُمَّ نُنَجِّي رُسُلَنَا وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا﴾ أَيْ: وَنُهْلِكُ الْمُكَذِّبِينَ بِالرُّسُلِ، ﴿كَذَلِكَ حَقًّا عَلَيْنَا نُنْجِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ [أَيْ] حَقًّا: أَوْجَبَهُ تَعَالَى عَلَى نَفْسِهِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: كَقَوْلِهِ ﴿كَتَبَ عَلَى نَفْسِهِ الرَّحْمَةَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١٢] كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَتَبَ كِتَابًا فَهُوَ عِنْدَهُ فَوْقَ الْعَرْشِ: إِنَّ رَحْمَتِي سَبَقَتْ غَضَبِي"

---

## 10:104-107 — verses 104-107 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says to His Messenger Muhammad ﷺ: Say, "O people, if you are in doubt concerning the soundness of what I have brought you of the upright religion that God revealed to me, then behold, I do not worship those whom you worship besides God. Rather I worship God alone, having no partner, and He is the One who takes your souls just as He gave you life, and then to Him is your return. So if your gods, whom you call upon besides God, were true, then I would not worship them; so call upon them, and let them harm me if they can, for they can neither harm nor benefit anyone. Rather, the One in whose hand lies harm and benefit is God alone, having no partner, and I have been commanded to be among the believers."

Concerning His saying, {And that I should direct my face toward the religion, upright, and not be among the polytheists}: that is, devote worship sincerely to God alone, upright, meaning turning away from polytheism. This is why He said, {and not be among the polytheists}, which is connected to His saying, {and I have been commanded to be among the believers}.

Concerning His saying, {And if God should touch you with harm} to the end of the verse: this is a clarification that good and evil, benefit and harm, all return to God alone, and no one shares with Him in that. He alone is the One deserving of worship, having no partner.

Al-Hafiz Ibn Asakir related, in the biographical entry on Safwan ibn Sulaym, by way of Abdullah ibn Wahb: Yahya ibn Ayyub informed me, from Isa ibn Musa, from Safwan ibn Sulaym, from Anas ibn Malik, that the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Seek good throughout all your time, and expose yourselves to the outpourings of God's mercy, for God has outpourings of His mercy with which He touches whomever He wills of His servants. And ask Him to conceal your shortcomings and to grant security from your fears."

He then related it by way of al-Layth, from Isa ibn Musa, from Safwan, from a man of the Ashja tribe, from Abu Hurayrah, as a raised report (marfu'), identical in wording.

Concerning His saying, {and He is the Forgiving, the Merciful}: that is, toward whoever turns to Him in repentance and relies upon Him, whatever sin it may be, even shirk (associating partners) with Him, for He will accept his repentance.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِرَسُولِهِ مُحَمَّدٍ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ: قُلْ: يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، إِنْ كُنْتُمْ فِي شَكٍّ مِنْ صِحَّةِ مَا جِئْتُكُمْ مِنَ الدِّينِ الْحَنِيفِ، الَّذِي أَوْحَاهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيَّ، فَهَا أَنَا لَا أَعْبُدُ الَّذِينَ تَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ، وَلَكِنْ أَعْبُدُ اللَّهَ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي يَتَوَفَّاكُمْ كَمَا أَحْيَاكُمْ، ثُمَّ إِلَيْهِ مَرْجِعُكُمْ؛ فَإِنْ كَانَتْ آلِهَتُكُمُ الَّتِي تَدْعُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ حَقًّا، فَأَنَا لَا أَعْبُدُهَا فَادْعُوهَا فَلْتَضُرَّنِي، فَإِنَّهَا لَا تَضُرُّ وَلَا تَنْفَعُ، وَإِنَّمَا الَّذِي بِيَدِهِ الضر والنفع هو الله وحده لا شريك لَهُ، وَأُمِرْتُ أَنْ أَكُونَ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأَنْ أَقِمْ وَجْهَكَ لِلدِّينِ حَنِيفًا وَلا تَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ﴾ أَيْ: أَخْلِصِ الْعِبَادَةَ لِلَّهِ وَحْدَهُ حَنِيفًا، أَيْ: مُنْحَرِفًا عَنِ الشِّرْكِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلا تَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ﴾ وَهُوَ مَعْطُوفٌ عَلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَأُمِرْتُ أَنْ أَكُونَ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنْ يَمْسَسْكَ اللَّهُ بِضُرٍّ﴾ إِلَى آخِرِهَا، بَيَانٌ لِأَنَّ الْخَيْرَ وَالشَّرَّ وَالنَّفْعَ وَالضُّرَّ إِنَّمَا هُوَ رَاجِعٌ إِلَى اللَّهِ تَعَالَى وَحْدَهُ لَا يُشَارِكُهُ فِي ذَلِكَ أَحَدٌ، فَهُوَ الَّذِي يَسْتَحِقُّ الْعِبَادَةَ وَحْدَهُ، لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ.

رَوَى الْحَافِظُ ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ، فِي تَرْجَمَةِ صَفْوَانَ بْنِ سُلَيْمٍ، مِنْ طَرِيقِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ وَهْبٍ: أَخْبَرَنِي يَحْيَى بْنُ أَيُّوبَ عَنْ عِيسَى بْنِ مُوسَى، عَنْ صَفْوَانَ بْنِ سُلَيْمٍ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم قَالَ: "اطْلُبُوا الْخَيْرَ دَهْرَكُمْ كُلَّهُ، وَتَعَرَّضُوا لِنَفَحَاتِ رَحْمَةِ اللَّهِ، فَإِنَّ لِلَّهِ نَفَحَاتٍ مِنْ رَحِمَتِهِ، يُصِيبُ بِهَا مَنْ يَشَاءُ مِنْ عِبَادِهِ وَاسْأَلُوهُ أَنْ يَسْتُرَ عَوْرَاتِكُمْ، وَيُؤَمِّنَ رَوْعَاتِكُمْ" 

ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ مِنْ طَرِيقِ اللَّيْثِ، عَنْ عِيسَى بْنِ مُوسَى، عَنْ صَفْوَانَ، عَنْ رَجُلٍ مِنْ أَشْجَعَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ مَرْفُوعًا؛ بِمِثْلِهِ سَوَاءٌ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَهُوَ الْغَفُورُ الرَّحِيمُ﴾ أَيْ: لِمَنْ تَابَ إِلَيْهِ وَتَوَكَّلَ عَلَيْهِ، وَلَوْ مِنْ أَيِّ ذَنْبٍ كَانَ، حَتَّى مِنَ الشِّرْكِ بِهِ، فَإِنَّهُ يَتُوبُ عَلَيْهِ.

---

## 10:108-109 — verses 108-109 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, commanding His Messenger, the prayers and peace of Allah be upon him, to inform the people that what he has brought to them from Allah is the truth in which there is no doubt and no uncertainty. Whoever is guided by it and follows it, the benefit of that following returns only to himself, [and whoever strays from it, the harm of that returns only to himself.]

{And I am not a keeper over you}, meaning: I am not charged with responsibility over you such that you must be believers in it; I am only a warner to you, and guidance rests with Allah, the Exalted.

His saying: {And follow what is revealed to you, and be patient} means: hold fast to what Allah has sent down to you and revealed to you, and be patient with the opposition of those among the people who oppose you, {until Allah judges}, meaning: until He decides between you and them, {and He is the best of judges}, meaning: the best of those who decide with His justice and His wisdom.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى آمِرًا لِرَسُولِهِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، أَنْ يُخْبِرَ النَّاسَ أَنَّ الَّذِي جَاءَهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ عند اللَّهُ هُوَ الْحَقُّ الذِي لَا مِرْيَةَ فِيهِ وَلَا شَكَّ، فَمَنِ اهْتَدَى بِهِ وَاتَّبَعَهُ فَإِنَّمَا يَعُودُ نَفْعُ ذَلِكَ الِاتِّبَاعِ عَلَى نَفْسِهِ، [وَمَنْ ضَلَّ عَنْهُ فَإِنَّمَا يَرْجِعُ وَبَالُ ذَلِكَ عَلَيْهِ ] 

﴿وَمَا أَنَا عَلَيْكُمْ بِوَكِيلٍ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَا أَنَا مُوَكَّلٌ بِكُمْ حَتَّى تَكُونُوا مُؤْمِنِينَ بِهِ، وَإِنَّمَا أَنَا نَذِيرٌ لَكُمْ، وَالْهِدَايَةُ عَلَى اللَّهِ تَعَالَى.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَاتَّبِعْ مَا يُوحَى إِلَيْكَ وَاصْبِرْ﴾ أَيْ: تَمَسَّكَ بِمَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْكَ وَأَوْحَاهُ وَاصْبِرْ عَلَى مُخَالَفَةِ مَنْ خَالَفَكَ مِنَ النَّاسِ، ﴿حَتَّى يَحْكُمَ اللَّهُ﴾ أَيْ: يَفْتَحَ بَيْنَكَ وَبَيْنَهُمْ، ﴿وَهُوَ خَيْرُ الْحَاكِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: خَيْرُ الْفَاتِحِينَ بِعَدْلِهِ وَحِكْمَتِهِ.

---
